<h1>Release 2.8.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Added TFLite builtin op support for the following TF ops:<ul>
<li><code>tf.raw_ops.Bucketize</code> op on CPU.</li>
<li><code>tf.where</code> op for data types
    <code>tf.int32</code>/<code>tf.uint32</code>/<code>tf.int8</code>/<code>tf.uint8</code>/<code>tf.int64</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.random.normal</code> op for output data type <code>tf.float32</code> on CPU.</li>
<li><code>tf.random.uniform</code> op for output data type <code>tf.float32</code> on CPU.</li>
<li><code>tf.random.categorical</code> op for output data type <code>tf.int64</code> on CPU.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tensorflow.experimental.tensorrt</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>conversion_params</code> is now deprecated inside <code>TrtGraphConverterV2</code> in
    favor of direct arguments: <code>max_workspace_size_bytes</code>, <code>precision_mode</code>,
    <code>minimum_segment_size</code>, <code>maximum_cached_engines</code>, <code>use_calibration</code> and
    <code>allow_build_at_runtime</code>.</li>
<li>Added a new parameter called <code>save_gpu_specific_engines</code> to the
    <code>.save()</code> function inside <code>TrtGraphConverterV2</code>. When <code>False</code>, the
    <code>.save()</code> function won't save any TRT engines that have been built. When
    <code>True</code> (default), the original behavior is preserved.</li>
<li><code>TrtGraphConverterV2</code> provides a new API called <code>.summary()</code> which
    outputs a summary of the inference converted by TF-TRT. It namely shows
    each <code>TRTEngineOp</code> with their input(s)' and output(s)' shape and dtype.
    A detailed version of the summary is available which prints additionally
    all the TensorFlow OPs included in each of the <code>TRTEngineOp</code>s.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.tpu.experimental.embedding</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.tpu.experimental.embedding.FeatureConfig</code> now takes an additional
    argument <code>output_shape</code> which can specify the shape of the output
    activation for the feature.</li>
<li><code>tf.tpu.experimental.embedding.TPUEmbedding</code> now has the same behavior
    as <code>tf.tpu.experimental.embedding.serving_embedding_lookup</code> which can
    take arbitrary rank of dense and sparse tensor. For ragged tensor,
    though the input tensor remains to be rank 2, the activations now can be
    rank 2 or above by specifying the output shape in the feature config or
    via the build method.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Add
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/config/experimental/enable_op_determinism"><code>tf.config.experimental.enable_op_determinism</code></a>,
    which makes TensorFlow ops run deterministically at the cost of performance.
    Replaces the <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> environmental variable, which is now
    deprecated. The "Bug Fixes and Other Changes" section lists more
    determinism-related changes.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>(Since TF 2.7) Add
    <a href="https://blog.tensorflow.org/2021/06/pluggabledevice-device-plugins-for-TensorFlow.html">PluggableDevice</a>
    support to
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/community/blob/master/rfcs/20210513-pluggable-profiler-for-tensorflow.md">TensorFlow Profiler</a>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug where setting <code>options.deterministic = False</code> would only
    modify one transformation to run non-deterministically, leaving other
    transformations deterministic. The option will now apply the same across
    all transformations.</li>
<li>The optimization <code>parallel_batch</code> now becomes default if not disabled by
    users, which will parallelize copying of batch elements.</li>
<li>Added the ability for <code>TensorSliceDataset</code> to identify and handle inputs
    that are files. This enables creating hermetic SavedModels when using
    datasets created from files.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds GPU Delegation support for serialization to Java API. This boosts
    initialization time up to 90% when OpenCL is available.</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>Interpreter::SetNumThreads</code>, in favor of
    <code>InterpreterBuilder::SetNumThreads</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Adds <code>tf.compat.v1.keras.utils.get_or_create_layer</code> to aid migration to
    TF2 by enabling tracking of nested keras models created in TF1-style,
    when used with the <code>tf.compat.v1.keras.utils.track_tf1_style_variables</code>
    decorator.</li>
<li>Added a <code>tf.keras.layers.experimental.preprocessing.HashedCrossing</code>
    layer which applies the hashing trick to the concatenation of crossed
    scalar inputs. This provides a stateless way to try adding feature
    crosses of integer or string data to a model.</li>
<li>Removed <code>keras.layers.experimental.preprocessing.CategoryCrossing</code>.
    Users should migrate to the <code>HashedCrossing</code> layer or use
    <code>tf.sparse.cross</code>/<code>tf.ragged.cross</code> directly.</li>
<li>Added additional <code>standardize</code> and <code>split</code> modes to <code>TextVectorization</code>:<ul>
<li><code>standardize="lower"</code> will lowercase inputs.</li>
<li><code>standardize="string_punctuation"</code> will remove all punctuation.</li>
<li><code>split="character"</code> will split on every unicode character.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added an <code>output_mode</code> argument to the <code>Discretization</code> and <code>Hashing</code>
    layers with the same semantics as other preprocessing layers. All
    categorical preprocessing layers now support <code>output_mode</code>.</li>
<li>All preprocessing layer output will follow the compute dtype of a
    <code>tf.keras.mixed_precision.Policy</code>, unless constructed with
    <code>output_mode="int"</code> in which case output will be <code>tf.int64</code>. The output
    type of any preprocessing layer can be controlled individually by
    passing a <code>dtype</code> argument to the layer.</li>
<li><code>tf.random.Generator</code> for keras initializers and all RNG code.</li>
<li>Added 3 new APIs for enable/disable/check the usage of
    <code>tf.random.Generator</code> in keras backend, which will be the new backend
    for all the RNG in Keras. We plan to switch on the new code path by
    default in tf 2.8, and the behavior change will likely to cause some
    breakage on user side (eg if the test is checking against some golden
    number). These 3 APIs will allow user to disable and switch back to
    legacy behavior if they prefer. In future (eg TF 2.10), we expect to
    totally remove the legacy code path (stateful random Ops), and these 3
    APIs will be removed as well.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.callbacks.experimental.BackupAndRestore</code> is now available as
    <code>tf.keras.callbacks.BackupAndRestore</code>. The experimental endpoint is
    deprecated and will be removed in a future release.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.experimental.SidecarEvaluator</code> is now available as
    <code>tf.keras.utils.SidecarEvaluator</code>. The experimental endpoint is
    deprecated and will be removed in a future release.</li>
<li>Metrics update and collection logic in default <code>Model.train_step()</code> is
    now customizable via overriding <code>Model.compute_metrics()</code>.</li>
<li>Losses computation logic in default <code>Model.train_step()</code> is now
    customizable via overriding <code>Model.compute_loss()</code>.</li>
<li><code>jit_compile</code> added to <code>Model.compile()</code> on an opt-in basis to compile
    the model's training step with <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/xla">XLA</a>.
    Note that <code>jit_compile=True</code> may not necessarily work for all models.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Deterministic Op Functionality:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fix regression in deterministic selection of deterministic cuDNN
    convolution algorithms, a regression that was introduced in v2.5. Note
    that nondeterministic out-of-memory events while selecting algorithms
    could still lead to nondeterminism, although this is very unlikely. This
    additional, unlikely source will be eliminated in a later version.</li>
<li>Add deterministic GPU implementations of:<ul>
<li><code>tf.function(jit_compile=True)</code>'s that use <code>Scatter</code>.</li>
<li>(since v2.7) Stateful ops used in <code>tf.data.Dataset</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.convert_to_tensor</code> when fed with (sparse)
    <code>tf.IndexedSlices</code> (because it uses <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sum</code>)</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.gather</code> backprop (because <code>tf.convert_to_tensor</code>
    reduces <code>tf.gather</code>'s (sparse) <code>tf.IndexedSlices</code> gradients into its
    dense <code>params</code> input)</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.segment_mean</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.segment_prod</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.segment_sum</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_mean</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_prod</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sum</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sqrt</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.nn.ctc_loss</code> (resolved, possibly in prior release,
    and confirmed with tests)</li>
<li>(since v2.7)<code>tf.nn.sparse_softmax_crossentropy_with_logits</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>(since v2.7) Run <code>tf.scatter_nd</code> and other related scatter functions,
    such as <code>tf.tensor_scatter_nd_update</code>, on CPU (with significant
    performance penalty).</li>
<li>Add determinism-unimplemented exception-throwing to the following ops.
    When op-determinism is expected (i.e. after
    <code>tf.config.experimental.enable_op_determinism</code> has been called), an
    attempt to use the specified paths through the following ops on a GPU
    will cause <code>tf.errors.UnimplementedError</code> (with an understandable
    message), unless otherwise specified, to be thrown.<ul>
<li><code>FakeQuantWithMinMaxVarsGradient</code> and
    <code>FakeQuantWithMinMaxVarsPerChannelGradient</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.compat.v1.get_seed</code> if the global random seed has
    not yet been set (via <code>tf.random.set_seed</code>). Throws <code>RuntimeError</code>
    from Python or <code>InvalidArgument</code> from C++</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.compat.v1.nn.fused_batch_norm</code> backprop to <code>offset</code>
    when <code>is_training=False</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.image.adjust_contrast</code> forward</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.image.resize</code> with <code>method=ResizeMethod.NEAREST</code>
    backprop</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.linalg.svd</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.math.bincount</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.nn.depthwise_conv2d</code> backprop to <code>filter</code> when not
    using cuDNN convolution</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.nn.dilation2d</code> gradient</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.nn.max_pool_with_argmax</code> gradient</li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.raw_ops.DebugNumericSummary</code> and
    <code>tf.raw_ops.DebugNumericSummaryV2</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.timestamp</code>. Throws <code>FailedPrecondition</code></li>
<li>(since v2.7) <code>tf.Variable.scatter_add</code> (and other scatter methods,
    both on ref and resource variables)</li>
<li>(since v2.7) The random-number-generating ops in the <code>tf.random</code>
    module when the global random seed has not yet been set (via
    <code>tf.random.set_seed</code>). Throws <code>RuntimeError</code> from Python or
    <code>InvalidArgument</code> from C++</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>TensorFlow-oneDNN no longer supports
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/53288">explicit use of oneDNN blocked tensor format</a>,
    e.g., setting the environment variable <code>TF_ENABLE_MKL_NATIVE_FORMAT</code> will
    not have any effect.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>TensorFlow has been validated on Windows Subsystem for Linux 2 (aka WSL 2)
    for both GPUs and CPUs.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Due to security issues (see section below), all boosted trees code has been
    deprecated. Users should switch to
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/decision-forests">TensorFlow Decision Forests</a>.
    TF's boosted trees code will be eliminated before the branch cut for TF 2.9
    and will no longer be present since that release.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Security</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a floating point division by 0 when executing convolution operators
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21725">CVE-2022-21725</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in shape inference for <code>ReverseSequence</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21728">CVE-2022-21728</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB access in <code>Dequantize</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21726">CVE-2022-21726</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer overflow in shape inference for <code>Dequantize</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21727">CVE-2022-21727</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB access in <code>FractionalAvgPoolGrad</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21730">CVE-2022-21730</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an overflow and divide by zero in <code>UnravelIndex</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21729">CVE-2022-21729</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a type confusion in shape inference for <code>ConcatV2</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21731">CVE-2022-21731</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an OOM in <code>ThreadPoolHandle</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21732">CVE-2022-21732</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an OOM due to integer overflow in <code>StringNGrams</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21733">CVE-2022-21733</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes more issues caused by incomplete validation in boosted trees code
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41208">CVE-2021-41208</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer overflows in most sparse component-wise ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23567">CVE-2022-23567</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer overflows in <code>AddManySparseToTensorsMap</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23568">CVE-2022-23568</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a number of <code>CHECK</code>-failures in <code>MapStage</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21734">CVE-2022-21734</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a division by zero in <code>FractionalMaxPool</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21735">CVE-2022-21735</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a number of <code>CHECK</code>-fails when building invalid/overflowing tensor
    shapes
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23569">CVE-2022-23569</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an undefined behavior in <code>SparseTensorSliceDataset</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21736">CVE-2022-21736</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an assertion failure based denial of service via faulty bin count
    operations
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21737">CVE-2022-21737</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a reference binding to null pointer in <code>QuantizedMaxPool</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21739">CVE-2022-21739</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer overflow leading to crash in <code>SparseCountSparseOutput</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21738">CVE-2022-21738</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41206">CVE-2021-41206</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23593">CVE-2022-23593</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23595">CVE-2022-23595</a>)</li>
<li>Updates <code>icu</code> to <code>69.1</code> to handle
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-10531">CVE-2020-10531</a></li>

<h1>Release 2.7.1</h1>
<p>This releases introduces several vulnerability fixes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a floating point division by 0 when executing convolution operators
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-21725">CVE-2022-21725</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in shape inference for <code>ReverseSequence</code>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41197">CVE-2021-41197</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a stack overflow due to self-recursive function in <code>GraphDef</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2022-23591">CVE-2022-23591</a>)</li>

<h1>Release 2.7.0</h1>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>The methods <code>Model.fit()</code>, <code>Model.predict()</code>, and <code>Model.evaluate()</code>
    will no longer uprank input data of shape <code>(batch_size,)</code> to become
    <code>(batch_size, 1)</code>. This enables <code>Model</code> subclasses to process scalar
    data in their <code>train_step()</code>/<code>test_step()</code>/<code>predict_step()</code> methods. \
    Note that this change may break certain subclassed models. You can
    revert back to the previous behavior by adding upranking yourself in the
    <code>train_step()</code>/<code>test_step()</code>/<code>predict_step()</code> methods, e.g. <code>if
    x.shape.rank == 1: x = tf.expand_dims(x, axis=-1)</code>. Functional models as
    well as Sequential models built with an explicit input shape are not
    affected.</li>
<li>The methods <code>Model.to_yaml()</code> and <code>keras.models.model_from_yaml</code> have
    been replaced to raise a <code>RuntimeError</code> as they can be abused to cause
    arbitrary code execution. It is recommended to use JSON serialization
    instead of YAML, or, a better alternative, serialize to H5.</li>
<li><code>LinearModel</code> and <code>WideDeepModel</code> are moved to the
    <code>tf.compat.v1.keras.models.</code> namespace
    (<code>tf.compat.v1.keras.models.LinearModel</code> and
    <code>tf.compat.v1.keras.models.WideDeepModel</code>), and their <code>experimental</code>
    endpoints (<code>tf.keras.experimental.models.LinearModel</code> and
    <code>tf.keras.experimental.models.WideDeepModel</code>) are being deprecated.</li>
<li>RNG behavior change for all <code>tf.keras.initializers</code> classes. For any
    class constructed with a fixed seed, it will no longer generate same
    value when invoked multiple times. Instead, it will return different
    value, but a deterministic sequence. This change will make the
    initialize behavior align between v1 and v2.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Rename fields <code>SignatureDef</code> table in schema to maximize the parity with
    TF SavedModel's Signature concept.</li>
<li>Deprecate Makefile builds. Makefile users need to migrate their builds
    to CMake or Bazel. Please refer to the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/lite/guide/build_cmake">Build TensorFlow Lite with CMake</a>
    and
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/lite/guide/build_arm">Build TensorFlow Lite for ARM boards</a>
    for the migration.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tflite::OpResolver::GetDelegates</code>. The list returned by
    TfLite's <code>BuiltinOpResolver::GetDelegates</code> is now always empty. Instead,
    recommend using new method <code>tflite::OpResolver::GetDelegateCreators</code> in
    order to achieve lazy initialization on TfLite delegate instances.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>TF Core:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.Graph.get_name_scope()</code> now always returns a string, as documented.
    Previously, when called within <code>name_scope("")</code> or <code>name_scope(None)</code>
    contexts, it returned <code>None</code>; now it returns the empty string.</li>
<li><code>tensorflow/core/ir/</code> contains a new MLIR-based Graph dialect that is
    isomorphic to GraphDef and will be used to replace GraphDef-based (e.g.,
    Grappler) optimizations.</li>
<li>Deprecated and removed <code>attrs()</code> function in shape inference. All
    attributes should be queried by name now (rather than range returned) to
    enable changing the underlying storage there.</li>
<li>The following Python symbols were accidentally added in earlier versions
    of TensorFlow and now are removed. Each symbol has a replacement that
    should be used instead, but note the replacement's argument names are
    different.<ul>
<li><code>tf.quantize_and_dequantize_v4</code> (accidentally introduced in
    TensorFlow 2.4): Use <code>tf.quantization.quantize_and_dequantize_v2</code>
    instead.</li>
<li><code>tf.batch_mat_mul_v3</code> (accidentally introduced in TensorFlow 2.6):
    Use <code>tf.linalg.matmul</code> instead.</li>
<li><code>tf.sparse_segment_sum_grad</code> (accidentally introduced in TensorFlow
    2.6): Use <code>tf.raw_ops.SparseSegmentSumGrad</code> instead. Directly
    calling this op is typically not necessary, as it is automatically
    used when computing the gradient of <code>tf.sparse.segment_sum</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Renaming of tensorflow::int64 to int_64_t in numerous places (the former
    is an alias for the latter) which could result in needing to regenerate
    selective op registration headers else execution would fail with
    unregistered kernels error.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Modular File System Migration:</p>
<ul>
<li>Support for S3 and HDFS file systems has been migrated to a modular file
    systems based approach and is now available in
    https://github.com/tensorflow/io. The <code>tensorflow-io</code> python package
    should be installed for S3 and HDFS support with tensorflow.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Improvements to the TensorFlow debugging experience:</p>
<ul>
<li>Previously, TensorFlow error stack traces involved many internal frames,
    which could be challenging to read through, while not being actionable
    for end users. As of TF 2.7, TensorFlow filters internal frames in most
    errors that it raises, to keep stack traces short, readable, and focused
    on what's actionable for end users (their own code).</li>
</ul>
<p>This behavior can be disabled by calling
<code>tf.debugging.disable_traceback_filtering()</code>, and can be re-enabled via
<code>tf.debugging.enable_traceback_filtering()</code>. If you are debugging a
TensorFlow-internal issue (e.g. to prepare a TensorFlow PR), make sure to
disable traceback filtering. You can check whether this feature is currently
enabled by calling <code>tf.debugging.is_traceback_filtering_enabled()</code>.</p>
<p>Note that this feature is only available with Python 3.7 or higher.</p>
<ul>
<li>Improve the informativeness of error messages raised by Keras
    <code>Layer.__call__()</code>, by adding the full list of argument values passed to
    the layer in every exception.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Introduce the <code>tf.compat.v1.keras.utils.track_tf1_style_variables</code>
    decorator, which enables using large classes of tf1-style variable_scope,
    <code>get_variable</code>, and <code>compat.v1.layer</code>-based components from within TF2
    models running with TF2 behavior enabled.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>tf.data service now supports auto-sharding. Users specify the sharding
    policy with <code>tf.data.experimental.service.ShardingPolicy</code> enum. It can
    be one of <code>OFF</code> (equivalent to today's <code>"parallel_epochs"</code> mode),
    <code>DYNAMIC</code> (equivalent to today's <code>"distributed_epoch"</code> mode), or one of
    the static sharding policies: <code>FILE</code>, <code>DATA</code>, <code>FILE_OR_DATA</code>, or <code>HINT</code>
    (corresponding to values of <code>tf.data.experimental.AutoShardPolicy</code>).</p>
<p>Static sharding (auto-sharding) requires the number of tf.data service
workers be fixed. Users need to specify the worker addresses in
<code>tensorflow.data.experimental.DispatcherConfig</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data.experimental.service.register_dataset</code> now accepts optional
    <code>compression</code> argument.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Keras:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras.layers.Conv</code> now includes a public <code>convolution_op</code> method.
    This method can be used to simplify the implementation of Conv
    subclasses. There are two primary ways to use this new method. The first
    is to use the method directly in your own <code>call</code> method: <code>python class
    StandardizedConv2D(tf.keras.layers.Conv2D): def call(self, inputs):
    mean, var = tf.nn.moments(self.kernel, axes=[0, 1, 2], keepdims=True)
    return self.convolution_op(inputs, (self.kernel - mean) / tf.sqrt(var +
    1e-10))</code> Alternatively, you can override <code>convolution_op</code>: <code>python class
    StandardizedConv2D(tf.keras.Layer): def convolution_op(self, inputs,
    kernel): mean, var = tf.nn.moments(kernel, axes=[0, 1, 2],
    keepdims=True) # Author code uses std + 1e-5 return
    super().convolution_op(inputs, (kernel - mean) / tf.sqrt(var + 1e-10))</code></li>
<li>Added <code>merge_state()</code> method to <code>tf.keras.metrics.Metric</code> for use in
    distributed computations.</li>
<li>Added <code>sparse</code> and <code>ragged</code> options to
    <code>tf.keras.layers.TextVectorization</code> to allow for <code>SparseTensor</code> and
    <code>RaggedTensor</code> outputs from the layer.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>distribute.experimental.rpc package:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>distribute.experimental.rpc package introduces APIs to create a GRPC
    based server to register tf.function methods and a GRPC client to invoke
    remote registered methods. RPC APIs are intended for multi-client setups
    i.e. server and clients are started in separate binaries independently.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Example usage to create server: ```python server =
    tf.distribute.experimental.rpc.Server.create("grpc", "127.0.0.1:1234")
    @tf.function(input_signature=[ tf.TensorSpec([], tf.int32),
    tf.TensorSpec([], dtypes.int32) ]) def _remote_multiply(a, b): return
    tf.math.multiply(a, b)</p>
<p>server.register("multiply", _remote_multiply) ```</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Example usage to create client: <code>python client =
    tf.distribute.experimental.rpc.Client.create("grpc", address) a =
    tf.constant(2, dtype=tf.int32) b = tf.constant(3, dtype=tf.int32)
    result = client.multiply(a, b)</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Add experimental API <code>experimental_from_jax</code> to support conversion from
    Jax models to TensorFlow Lite.</li>
<li>Support uint32 data type for cast op.</li>
<li>Support int8 data type for cast op.</li>
<li>Add experimental quantization debugger <code>tf.lite.QuantizationDebugger</code></li>
<li>Add lite.experimental.authoring.compatible API<ul>
<li>A Python decorator to provide a way to check TFLite compatibility
    issue of <code>tf.function</code>. This returns a callable object which
    validates TFLite compatibility. If an incompatible operation is
    encountered during execution, an exception will be raised with
    information about the incompatible ops.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add lite.experimental.Analyzer API<ul>
<li>An experimental tool to analyze TFLite flatbuffer models. This API
    can be used to investigate TFLite model structure and check
    compatibility with GPU delegate.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Extension Types</p>
<ul>
<li>Add experimental API to define new Python classes that can be handled by
    TensorFlow APIs. To create an extension type, simply define a Python
    class with <code>tf.experimental.ExtensionType</code> as its base, and use type
    annotations to specify the type for each field. E.g.: <code>python class
    MaskedTensor(tf.experimental.ExtensionType): values: tf.Tensor mask:
    tf.Tensor</code> The <code>tf.ExtensionType</code> base class works similarly to
    <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#typing.NamedTuple"><code>typing.NamedTuple</code></a>
    and
    <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/dataclasses.html#dataclasses.dataclass"><code>@dataclasses.dataclass</code></a>
    from the standard Python library.</li>
<li>Extension types are supported by Keras, tf.data, TF-hub, SavedModel,
    tf.function, control flow ops, py_function, and distribution strategy.</li>
<li>Add "dispatch decorators" that can be used to override the default
    behavior of TensorFlow ops (such as <code>tf.add</code> or <code>tf.concat</code>) when they
    are applied to ExtensionType values.</li>
<li>The <code>BatchableExtensionType</code> API can be used to define extension types
    that support APIs that make use of batching, such as <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>
    and <code>tf.map_fn</code>.</li>
<li>For more information, see the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/extension_type">Extension types guide</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF Core:<ul>
<li>Random number generation (RNG) system<ul>
<li>Add argument <code>alg</code> to <code>tf.random.stateless_*</code> functions to
    explicitly select the RNG algorithm.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.nn.experimental.stateless_dropout</code>, a stateless version of
    <code>tf.nn.dropout</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.random.Generator</code> now can be created inside the scope of
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental.ParameterServerStrategy</code> and
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental.CentralStorageStrategy</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add an experimental session config
    <code>tf.experimental.disable_functional_ops_lowering</code> which disables
    functional control flow op lowering optimization. This is useful when
    executing within a portable runtime where control flow op kernels may
    not be loaded due to selective registration.</li>
<li>Add a new experimental argument <code>experimental_is_anonymous</code> to
    <code>tf.lookup.StaticHashTable.__init__</code> to create the table in anonymous
    mode. In this mode, the table resource can only be accessed via resource
    handles (not resource names) and will be deleted automatically when all
    resource handles pointing to it are gone.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li>Introduce the <code>tf.data.experimental.at</code> API which provides random access
    for input pipelines that consist of transformations that support random
    access. The initial set of transformations that support random access
    includes:
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.from_tensor_slices</code>,<code>tf.data.Dataset.shuffle</code>,
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.batch</code>, <code>tf.data.Dataset.shard</code>, <code>tf.data.Dataset.map</code>,
    and <code>tf.data.Dataset.range</code>.</li>
<li>Promote <code>tf.data.Options.experimental_deterministic</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Options.deterministic</code> and deprecate the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Move autotuning options
    from<code>tf.data.Options.experimental_optimization.autotune*</code> to a newly
    created <code>tf.data.Options.autotune.*</code> and remove support for
    <code>tf.data.Options.experimental_optimization.autotune_buffers</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for user-defined names of tf.data core Python API, which can
    be used to disambiguate tf.data events in TF Profiler Trace Viewer.</li>
<li>Promote <code>tf.data.experimental.sample_from_datasets</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.sample_from_datasets</code> and deprecate the experimental
    endpoint.</li>
<li>Added <code>TF_GPU_ALLOCATOR=cuda_malloc_async</code> that use cudaMallocAsync from
    CUDA 11.2. This could become the default in the future.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TF SavedModel:<ul>
<li>Custom gradients are now saved by default. See
    <code>tf.saved_model.SaveOptions</code> to disable this.</li>
<li>The saved_model_cli's <code>--input_examples</code> inputs are now restricted to
    python literals to avoid code injection.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>XLA:<ul>
<li>Add a new API that allows custom call functions to signal errors. The
    old API will be deprecated in a future release. See
    https://www.tensorflow.org/xla/custom_call for details.</li>
<li>XLA:GPU reductions are deterministic by default (reductions within
    <code>jit_compile=True</code> are now deterministic).</li>
<li>XLA:GPU works with Horovod (OSS contribution by Trent Lo from NVidia)</li>
<li>XLA:CPU and XLA:GPU can compile tf.unique and tf.where when shapes are
    provably correct at compile time.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.saved_model.save</code>:<ul>
<li>When saving a model, not specifying a namespace whitelist for custom ops
    with a namespace will now default to allowing rather than rejecting them
    all.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Deterministic Op Functionality (enabled by setting the environment variable
    <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> to <code>"true"</code> or <code>"1"</code>):<ul>
<li>Add determinsitic GPU implementations of:<ul>
<li><code>tf.math.segment_sum</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.segment_prod</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.segment_mean</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sum</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_prod</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sqrt</code></li>
<li><code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_mean</code></li>
<li><code>tf.gather</code> backprop</li>
<li><code>tf.convert_to_tensor</code> when fed with (sparse) <code>tf.IndexedSlices</code></li>
<li><code>tf.nn.sparse_softmax_crossentropy_with_logits</code></li>
<li><code>tf.nn.ctc_loss</code> (resolved, possibly in prior release, and confirmed
    with tests)</li>
<li>stateful ops used in <code>tf.data.Dataset</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Run the following ops on CPU (with significant performance penalty):<ul>
<li><code>tf.scatter_nd</code> and other related scatter functions, such as
    <code>tf.tensor_scatter_nd_update</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add determinism-unimplemented exception-throwing to the following ops.
    When op-determinism is expected (i.e. when the environment variable
    <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> is set to <code>"true"</code> or <code>"1"</code>), an attempt to use
    the specified paths through the following ops on a GPU will cause
    <code>tf.errors.UnimplementedError</code> (with an understandable message), unless
    otherwise specified, to be thrown.<ul>
<li><code>tf.compat.v1.nn.fused_batch_norm</code> backprop to <code>offset</code> when
    <code>is_training=False</code></li>
<li><code>tf.image.adjust_contrast</code> forward</li>
<li><code>tf.nn.depthwise_conv2d</code> backprop to <code>filter</code> when not using cuDNN
    convolution</li>
<li><code>tf.image.resize</code> with <code>method=ResizeMethod.NEAREST</code> backprop</li>
<li><code>tf.math.bincount</code> - TODO: confirm exception added</li>
<li><code>tf.raw_ops.DebugNumericSummary</code> and
    <code>tf.raw_ops.DebugNumericSummaryV2</code></li>
<li><code>tf.Variable.scatter_add</code> (and other scatter methods, both on ref
    and resource variables)</li>
<li><code>tf.linalg.svd</code></li>
<li><code>tf.nn.dilation2d</code> gradient</li>
<li><code>tf.nn.max_pool_with_argmax</code> gradient</li>
<li><code>tf.timestamp</code>. Throws <code>FailedPrecondition</code></li>
<li>The random-number-generating ops in the <code>tf.random</code> module when the
    global random seed has not yet been set (via <code>tf.random.set_seed</code>).
    Throws <code>RuntimeError</code> from Python or <code>InvalidArgument</code> from C++</li>
<li><code>tf.compat.v1.get_seed</code> if the global random seed has not yet been
    set (via <code>tf.random.set_seed</code>). Throws <code>RuntimeError</code> from Python or
    <code>InvalidArgument</code> from C++</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Security</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a code injection issue in <code>saved_model_cli</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41228">CVE-2021-41228</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a vulnerability due to use of uninitialized value in Tensorflow
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41225">CVE-2021-41225</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in <code>FusedBatchNorm</code> kernels
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41223">CVE-2021-41223</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an arbitrary memory read in <code>ImmutableConst</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41227">CVE-2021-41227</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in <code>SparseBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41226">CVE-2021-41226</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in <code>SparseFillEmptyRows</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41224">CVE-2021-41224</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a segfault due to negative splits in <code>SplitV</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41222">CVE-2021-41222</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes segfaults and vulnerabilities caused by accesses to invalid memory
    during shape inference in <code>Cudnn*</code> ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41221">CVE-2021-41221</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer exception when <code>Exit</code> node is not preceded by <code>Enter</code>
    op
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41217">CVE-2021-41217</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer division by 0 in <code>tf.raw_ops.AllToAll</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41218">CVE-2021-41218</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a use after free and a memory leak in <code>CollectiveReduceV2</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41220">CVE-2021-41220</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an undefined behavior via <code>nullptr</code> reference binding in sparse matrix
    multiplication
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41219">CVE-2021-41219</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap buffer overflow in <code>Transpose</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41216">CVE-2021-41216</a>)</li>
<li>Prevents deadlocks arising from mutually recursive <code>tf.function</code> objects
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41213">CVE-2021-41213</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer exception in <code>DeserializeSparse</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41215">CVE-2021-41215</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an undefined behavior arising from reference binding to <code>nullptr</code> in
    <code>tf.ragged.cross</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41214">CVE-2021-41214</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in <code>tf.ragged.cross</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41212">CVE-2021-41212</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in shape inference for <code>QuantizeV2</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41211">CVE-2021-41211</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in all <code>tf.raw_ops.QuantizeAndDequantizeV*</code> ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41205">CVE-2021-41205</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41207">CVE-2021-41207</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41209">CVE-2021-41209</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41210">CVE-2021-41210</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41208">CVE-2021-41208</a>)</li>

    TF ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41206">CVE-2021-41206</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a segfault produced while copying constant resource tensor
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41204">CVE-2021-41204</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a vulnerability caused by unitialized access in
    <code>EinsumHelper::ParseEquation</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41201">CVE-2021-41201</a>)</li>

    during checkpoint loading
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41203">CVE-2021-41203</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41202">CVE-2021-41202</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an overflow producing a crash in <code>tf.image.resize</code> when size is large
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41199">CVE-2021-41199</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41198">CVE-2021-41198</a>)</li>

    <code>tf.summary.create_file_writer</code>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41195">CVE-2021-41195</a>)</li>
<li>Updates <code>curl</code> to <code>7.78.0</code> to handle
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22922">CVE-2021-22922</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22923">CVE-2021-22923</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22924">CVE-2021-22924</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22925">CVE-2021-22925</a>,
    and
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22926">CVE-2021-22926</a>.</li>

<h1>Release 2.6.2</h1>
<p>Fixes an issue where <code>keras</code>, <code>tensorflow_estimator</code> and <code>tensorboard</code> were
missing proper upper bounds and resulted in broken installs after TF 2.7 release</p>
<h1>Release 2.6.1</h1>
<p>This release introduces several vulnerability fixes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a code injection issue in <code>saved_model_cli</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41228">CVE-2021-41228</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41225">CVE-2021-41225</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41223">CVE-2021-41223</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41227">CVE-2021-41227</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41226">CVE-2021-41226</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41224">CVE-2021-41224</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41214">CVE-2021-41214</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in <code>tf.ragged.cross</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41212">CVE-2021-41212</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41211">CVE-2021-41211</a>)</li>

    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41205">CVE-2021-41205</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an FPE in <code>ParallelConcat</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41207">CVE-2021-41207</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes FPE issues in convolutions with zero size filters
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41209">CVE-2021-41209</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB read in <code>tf.raw_ops.SparseCountSparseOutput</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41210">CVE-2021-41210</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes vulnerabilities caused by incomplete validation in boosted trees code
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41208">CVE-2021-41208</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes vulnerabilities caused by incomplete validation of shapes in multiple
    TF ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41206">CVE-2021-41206</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a segfault produced while copying constant resource tensor
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41204">CVE-2021-41204</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a vulnerability caused by unitialized access in
    <code>EinsumHelper::ParseEquation</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41201">CVE-2021-41201</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes several vulnerabilities and segfaults caused by missing validation
    during checkpoint loading
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41203">CVE-2021-41203</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an overflow producing a crash in <code>tf.range</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41202">CVE-2021-41202</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an overflow producing a crash in <code>tf.image.resize</code> when size is large
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41199">CVE-2021-41199</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an overflow producing a crash in <code>tf.tile</code> when tiling tensor is large
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41198">CVE-2021-41198</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a vulnerability produced due to incomplete validation in
    <code>tf.summary.create_file_writer</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41200">CVE-2021-41200</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes multiple crashes due to overflow and <code>CHECK</code>-fail in ops with large
    tensor shapes
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41197">CVE-2021-41197</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a crash in <code>max_pool3d</code> when size argument is 0 or negative
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41196">CVE-2021-41196</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a crash in <code>tf.math.segment_*</code> operations
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-41195">CVE-2021-41195</a>)</li>
<li>Updates <code>curl</code> to <code>7.78.0</code> to handle
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22922">CVE-2021-22922</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22923">CVE-2021-22923</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22924">CVE-2021-22924</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22925">CVE-2021-22925</a>,
    and
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-22926">CVE-2021-22926</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 2.6.0</h1>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.train.experimental.enable_mixed_precision_graph_rewrite</code> is removed, as
    the API only works in graph mode and is not customizable. The function is
    still accessible under
    <code>tf.compat.v1.mixed_precision.enable_mixed_precision_graph_rewrite</code>, but it
    is recommended to use the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/mixed_precision">Keras mixed precision API</a>
    instead.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Remove <code>experimental.nn.dynamic_rnn</code>, <code>experimental.nn.TfLiteRNNCell</code>
    and <code>experimental.nn.TfLiteLSTMCell</code> since they're no longer supported.
    It's recommended to just use
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/keras/layers/LSTM">keras lstm</a>
    instead.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Keras been split into a separate PIP package (<code>keras</code>), and its code has
    been moved to the GitHub
    repository<a href="http://github.com/keras-team/keras">keras-team/keras</a>. The
    API endpoints for <code>tf.keras</code> stay unchanged, but are now backed by the
    <code>keras</code> PIP package. The existing code in tensorflow/python/keras is a
    staled copy and will be removed in future release (2.7). Please remove
    any imports to <code>tensorflow.python.keras</code> and replace them with public
    tf.keras API instead.</li>
<li>The methods <code>Model.to_yaml()</code> and <code>keras.models.model_from_yaml</code> have
    been replaced to raise a <code>RuntimeError</code> as they can be abused to cause
    arbitrary code execution. It is recommended to use JSON serialization
    instead of YAML, or, a better alternative, serialize to H5.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Caveats</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF Core:<ul>
<li>A longstanding bug in <code>tf.while_loop</code>, which caused it to execute
    sequentially, even when <code>parallel_iterations&gt;1</code>, has now been fixed.
    However, the increased parallelism may result in increased memory use.
    Users who experience unwanted regressions should reset their
    <code>while_loop</code>'s <code>parallel_iterations</code> value to 1, which is consistent
    with prior behavior.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Keras has been split into a separate PIP package (<code>keras</code>), and its code
    has been moved to the GitHub repository
    <a href="http://github.com/keras-team/keras">keras-team/keras</a>. The API
    endpoints for <code>tf.keras</code> stay unchanged, but are now backed by the
    <code>keras</code> PIP package. All Keras-related PRs and issues should now be
    directed to the GitHub repository.
    <a href="http://github.com/keras-team/keras">keras-team/keras</a>.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.utils.experimental.DatasetCreator</code> now takes an optional
    <code>tf.distribute.InputOptions</code> for specific options when used with
    distribution.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.experimental.SidecarEvaluator</code> is now available for a program
    intended to be run on an evaluator task, which is commonly used to
    supplement a training cluster running with
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental.ParameterServerStrategy</code> (see
    `https://www.tensorflow.org/tutorials/distribute/parameter_server_training).
    It can also be used with single-worker training or other strategies. See
    docstring for more info.</li>
<li>Preprocessing layers moved from experimental to core.<ul>
<li>Import paths moved from <code>tf.keras.layers.preprocessing.experimental</code>
    to <code>tf.keras.layers</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Updates to Preprocessing layers API for consistency and clarity:<ul>
<li><code>StringLookup</code> and <code>IntegerLookup</code> default for <code>mask_token</code> changed
    to <code>None</code>. This matches the default masking behavior of <code>Hashing</code>
    and <code>Embedding</code> layers. To keep existing behavior, pass
    <code>mask_token=""</code> during layer creation.</li>
<li>Renamed <code>"binary"</code> output mode to <code>"multi_hot"</code> for
    <code>CategoryEncoding</code>, <code>StringLookup</code>, <code>IntegerLookup</code>, and
    <code>TextVectorization</code>. Multi-hot encoding will no longer automatically
    uprank rank 1 inputs, so these layers can now multi-hot encode
    unbatched multi-dimensional samples.</li>
<li>Added a new output mode <code>"one_hot"</code> for <code>CategoryEncoding</code>,
    <code>StringLookup</code>, <code>IntegerLookup</code>, which will encode each element in
    an input batch individually, and automatically append a new output
    dimension if necessary. Use this mode on rank 1 inputs for the old
    <code>"binary"</code> behavior of one-hot encoding a batch of scalars.</li>
<li><code>Normalization</code> will no longer automatically uprank rank 1 inputs,
    allowing normalization of unbatched multi-dimensional samples.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>The recommended Android NDK version for building TensorFlow Lite has
    been changed from r18b to r19c.</li>
<li>Supports int64 for mul.</li>
<li>Supports native variable builtin ops - ReadVariable, AssignVariable.</li>
<li>Converter:<ul>
<li>Experimental support for variables in TFLite. To enable through
    conversion, users need to set
    <code>experimental_enable_resource_variables</code> on tf.lite.TFLiteConverter
    to True. Note: mutable variables is only available using
    <code>from_saved_model</code> in this release, support for other methods is
    coming soon.</li>
<li>Old Converter (TOCO) is getting removed from next release. It's been
    deprecated for few releases already.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.saved_model</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>SavedModels can now save custom gradients. Use the option
    <code>tf.saved_model.SaveOption(experimental_custom_gradients=True)</code> to
    enable this feature. The documentation in
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/advanced_autodiff#custom_gradients">Advanced autodiff</a>
    has been updated.</li>
<li>Object metadata has now been deprecated and no longer saved to the
    SavedModel.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>TF Core:</p>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>tf.config.experimental.reset_memory_stats</code> to reset the tracked
    peak memory returned by <code>tf.config.experimental.get_memory_info</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>target_workers</code> param to <code>data_service_ops.from_dataset_id</code> and
    <code>data_service_ops.distribute</code>. Users can specify <code>"AUTO"</code>, <code>"ANY"</code>, or
    <code>"LOCAL"</code> (case insensitive). If <code>"AUTO"</code>, tf.data service runtime
    decides which workers to read from. If <code>"ANY"</code>, TF workers read from any
    tf.data service workers. If <code>"LOCAL"</code>, TF workers will only read from
    local in-processs tf.data service workers. <code>"AUTO"</code> works well for most
    cases, while users can specify other targets. For example, <code>"LOCAL"</code>
    would help avoid RPCs and data copy if every TF worker colocates with a
    tf.data service worker. Currently, <code>"AUTO"</code> reads from any tf.data
    service workers to preserve existing behavior. The default value is
    <code>"AUTO"</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF Core:<ul>
<li>Added <code>tf.lookup.experimental.MutableHashTable</code>, which provides a
    generic mutable hash table implementation.<ul>
<li>Compared to <code>tf.lookup.experimental.DenseHashTable</code> this offers
    lower overall memory usage, and a cleaner API. It does not require
    specifying a <code>delete_key</code> and <code>empty_key</code> that cannot be inserted
    into the table.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added support for specifying number of subdivisions in all reduce host
    collective. This parallelizes work on CPU and speeds up the collective
    performance. Default behavior is unchanged.</li>
<li>Add an option <code>perturb_singular</code> to <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve</code> that
    allows solving linear systems with a numerically singular tridiagonal
    matrix, e.g. for use in inverse iteration.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.linalg.eigh_tridiagonal</code> that computes the eigenvalues of a
    Hermitian tridiagonal matrix.</li>
<li><code>tf.constant</code> now places its output on the current default device.</li>
<li>SavedModel<ul>
<li>Added <code>tf.saved_model.experimental.TrackableResource</code>, which allows
    the creation of custom wrapper objects for resource tensors.</li>
<li>Added a SavedModel load option to allow restoring partial
    checkpoints into the SavedModel. See
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/saved_model/LoadOptions"><code>tf.saved_model.LoadOptions</code></a>
    for details.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added a new op <code>SparseSegmentSumGrad</code> to match the other sparse segment
    gradient ops and avoid an extra gather operation that was in the
    previous gradient implementation.</li>
<li>Added a new session config setting <code>internal_fragmentation_fraction</code>,
    which controls when the BFC Allocator needs to split an oversized chunk
    to satisfy an allocation request.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.get_current_name_scope()</code> which returns the current full name
    scope string that will be prepended to op names.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.bucket_by_sequence_length</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.bucket_by_sequence_length</code> and deprecating the
    experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.get_single_element</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.get_single_element</code> and deprecating the experimental
    endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.group_by_window</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.group_by_window</code> and deprecating the experimental
    endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.RandomDataset</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.random</code> and deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.scan</code> API to <code>tf.data.Dataset.scan</code> and
    deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.snapshot</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.shapshot</code> and deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.take_while</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.take_while</code> and deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.ThreadingOptions</code> API to
    <code>tf.data.ThreadingOptions</code> and deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.unique</code> API to <code>tf.data.Dataset.unique</code>
    and deprecating the experimental endpoint.</li>
<li>Added <code>stop_on_empty_dataset</code> parameter to <code>sample_from_datasets</code> and
    <code>choose_from_datasets</code>. Setting <code>stop_on_empty_dataset=True</code> will stop
    sampling if it encounters an empty dataset. This preserves the sampling
    ratio throughout training. The prior behavior was to continue sampling,
    skipping over exhausted datasets, until all datasets are exhausted. By
    default, the original behavior (<code>stop_on_empty_dataset=False</code>) is
    preserved.</li>
<li>Removed previously deprecated tf.data statistics related APIs:<ul>
<li><code>tf.data.Options.experimental_stats</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.StatsAggregator</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.StatsOptions.*</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.bytes_produced_stats</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.latency_stats</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Removed the following experimental tf.data optimization APIs:<ul>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.MapVectorizationOptions.*</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions.filter_with_random_uniform_fusion</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions.hoist_random_uniform</code></li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions.map_vectorization</code> *
    <code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions.reorder_data_discarding_ops</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>Fix usage of <code>__getitem__</code> slicing in Keras Functional APIs when the
    inputs are <code>RaggedTensor</code> objects.</li>
<li>Add <code>keepdims</code> argument to all <code>GlobalPooling</code> layers.</li>
<li>Add <code>include_preprocessing</code> argument to <code>MobileNetV3</code> architectures to
    control the inclusion of <code>Rescaling</code> layer in the model.</li>
<li>Add optional argument (<code>force</code>) to <code>make_(train|test|predict)_funtion</code>
    methods to skip the cached function and generate a new one. This is
    useful to regenerate in a single call the compiled training function
    when any <code>.trainable</code> attribute of any model's layer has changed.</li>
<li>Models now have a <code>save_spec</code> property which contains the <code>TensorSpec</code>
    specs for calling the model. This spec is automatically saved when the
    model is called for the first time.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.linalg</code>:<ul>
<li>Add <code>CompositeTensor</code> as a base class to <code>LinearOperator</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.lite</code>:<ul>
<li>Fix mean op reference quantization rounding issue.</li>
<li>Added <code>framework_stable</code> BUILD target, which links in only the
    non-experimental TF Lite APIs.</li>
<li>Remove deprecated Java <code>Interpreter</code> methods:<ul>
<li><code>modifyGraphWithDelegate</code> - Use <code>Interpreter.Options.addDelegate</code></li>
<li><code>setNumThreads</code> - Use <code>Interpreter.Options.setNumThreads</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add Conv3DTranspose as a builtin op.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.summary</code>:<ul>
<li>Fix <code>tf.summary.should_record_summaries()</code> so it correctly reflects when
    summaries will be written, even when <code>tf.summary.record_if()</code> is not n
    effect, by returning True tensor if default writer is present.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Grappler:<ul>
<li>Disable default Grappler optimization timeout to make the optimization
    pipeline deterministic. This may lead to increased model loading time,
    because time spent in graph optimizations is now unbounded (was 20
    minutes).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Deterministic Op Functionality (enabled by setting <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> to
    <code>"true"</code> or <code>"1"</code>):<ul>
<li>Add a deterministic GPU implementation of
    <code>tf.nn.softmax_cross_entropy_with_logits</code>. See PR
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/49178">49178</a>.</li>
<li>Add a deterministic CPU implementation of <code>tf.image.crop_and_resize</code>.
    See PR <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/48905">48905</a>.</li>
<li>Add determinism-unimplemented exception-throwing to the following ops.
    When op-determinism is expected, an attempt to use the specified paths
    through the following ops on a GPU will cause
    <code>tf.errors.UnimplementedError</code> (with an understandable message) to be
    thrown.<ul>
<li><code>tf.nn.sparse_softmax_cross_entropy_with_logits</code> forwards and/or
    backwards. See PR
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/47925">47925</a>.</li>
<li><code>tf.image.crop_and_resize</code> gradient w.r.t. either <code>image</code> or
    <code>boxes</code>. See PR
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/48905">48905</a>.</li>
<li><code>tf.sparse.sparse_dense_matmul</code> forwards. See PR
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/pull/50355">50355</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Security</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a heap out of bounds access in sparse reduction operations
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37635">CVE-2021-37635</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a floating point exception in <code>SparseDenseCwiseDiv</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37636">CVE-2021-37636</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference in <code>CompressElement</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37637">CVE-2021-37637</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference in <code>RaggedTensorToTensor</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37638">CVE-2021-37638</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference and a heap OOB read arising from operations
    restoring tensors
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37639">CVE-2021-37639</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer division by 0 in sparse reshaping
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37640">CVE-2021-37640</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a division by 0 in <code>ResourceScatterDiv</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37642">CVE-2021-37642</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in <code>RaggedGather</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37641">CVE-2021-37641</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a <code>std::abort</code> raised from <code>TensorListReserve</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37644">CVE-2021-37644</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference in <code>MatrixDiagPartOp</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37643">CVE-2021-37643</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an integer overflow due to conversion to unsigned
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37645">CVE-2021-37645</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a bad allocation error in <code>StringNGrams</code> caused by integer conversion
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37646">CVE-2021-37646</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference in <code>SparseTensorSliceDataset</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37647">CVE-2021-37647</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an incorrect validation of <code>SaveV2</code> inputs
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37648">CVE-2021-37648</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference in <code>UncompressElement</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37649">CVE-2021-37649</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a segfault and a heap buffer overflow in
    <code>{Experimental,}DatasetToTFRecord</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37650">CVE-2021-37650</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap buffer overflow in <code>FractionalAvgPoolGrad</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37651">CVE-2021-37651</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a use after free in boosted trees creation
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37652">CVE-2021-37652</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a division by 0 in <code>ResourceGather</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37653">CVE-2021-37653</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB and a <code>CHECK</code> fail in <code>ResourceGather</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37654">CVE-2021-37654</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap OOB in <code>ResourceScatterUpdate</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37655">CVE-2021-37655</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an undefined behavior arising from reference binding to nullptr in
    <code>RaggedTensorToSparse</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-37656">CVE-2021-37656</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes an undefined behavior arising from reference binding to nullptr in
    <code>MatrixDiagV*</code> ops

<ul>

<h1>Release 2.3.3</h1>
<p>This release introduces several vulnerability fixes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a heap buffer overflow in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29512">CVE-2021-29512</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap out of bounds write in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29514">CVE-2021-29514</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a type confusion during tensor casts which leads to dereferencing null
    pointers
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29513">CVE-2021-29513</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a reference binding to null pointer in <code>MatrixDiag*</code> ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29515">CVE-2021-29515</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference via invalid Ragged Tensors
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29516">CVE-2021-29516</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a division by zero in <code>Conv3D</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29517">CVE-2021-29517</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes vulnerabilities where session operations in eager mode lead to null
    pointer dereferences
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29518">CVE-2021-29518</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a <code>CHECK</code>-fail in <code>SparseCross</code> caused by type confusion
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29519">CVE-2021-29519</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a segfault in <code>SparseCountSparseOutput</code>

<h1>Release 2.2.3</h1>
<p>This release introduces several vulnerability fixes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a heap buffer overflow in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29512">CVE-2021-29512</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap out of bounds write in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29514">CVE-2021-29514</a>)</li>

    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-8169">CVE-2020-8169</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-8177">CVE-2020-8177</a>,

    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-8284">CVE-2020-8284</a>,

    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-8286">CVE-2020-8286</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 2.1.4</h1>
<p>This release introduces several vulnerability fixes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a heap buffer overflow in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29512">CVE-2021-29512</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a heap out of bounds write in <code>RaggedBinCount</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29514">CVE-2021-29514</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a type confusion during tensor casts which leads to dereferencing null
    pointers
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29513">CVE-2021-29513</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a reference binding to null pointer in <code>MatrixDiag*</code> ops
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29515">CVE-2021-29515</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a null pointer dereference via invalid Ragged Tensors
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29516">CVE-2021-29516</a>)</li>
<li>Fixes a division by zero in <code>Conv3D</code>
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-29517">CVE-2021-29517</a>)</li>
