<h1>Release 2.3.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data</code> adds two new mechanisms to solve input pipeline bottlenecks and
    save resources:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/data/experimental/snapshot">snapshot</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/data/experimental/service">tf.data service</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p>In addition checkout the detailed
<a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/data_performance_analysis">guide</a> for
analyzing input pipeline performance with TF Profiler.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/TPUStrategy"><code>tf.distribute.TPUStrategy</code></a>
    is now a stable API and no longer considered experimental for TensorFlow.
    (earlier <code>tf.distribute.experimental.TPUStrategy</code>).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/profiler">TF Profiler</a> introduces two new
    tools: a memory profiler to visualize your model’s memory usage over time
    and a <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/profiler#events">python tracer</a>
    which allows you to trace python function calls in your model. Usability
    improvements include better diagnostic messages and
    <a href="https://tensorflow.org/guide/profiler#collect_performance_data">profile options</a>
    to customize the host and device trace verbosity level.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Introduces experimental support for Keras Preprocessing Layers API
    (<a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/keras/layers/experimental/preprocessing?version=nightly"><code>tf.keras.layers.experimental.preprocessing.*</code></a>)
    to handle data preprocessing operations, with support for composite tensor
    inputs. Please see below for additional details on these layers.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>TFLite now properly supports dynamic shapes during conversion and inference.
    We’ve also added opt-in support on Android and iOS for
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/master/tensorflow/lite/delegates/xnnpack">XNNPACK</a>,
    a highly optimized set of CPU kernels, as well as opt-in support for
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/lite/g3doc/performance/gpu_advanced.md#running-quantized-models-experimental">executing quantized models on the GPU</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Libtensorflow packages are available in GCS starting this release. We have
    also started to
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow#official-builds">release a nightly version of these packages</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The experimental Python API
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/debugging/experimental/enable_dump_debug_info"><code>tf.debugging.experimental.enable_dump_debug_info()</code></a>
    now allows you to instrument a TensorFlow program and dump debugging
    information to a directory on the file system. The directory can be read and
    visualized by a new interactive dashboard in TensorBoard 2.3 called
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/tensorboard/debugger_v2">Debugger V2</a>, which
    reveals the details of the TensorFlow program including graph structures,
    history of op executions at the Python (eager) and intra-graph levels, the
    runtime dtype, shape, and numerical composition of tensors, as well as their
    code locations.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Increases the <strong>minimum bazel version</strong> required to build TF to <strong>3.1.0</strong>.</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code><ul>
<li>Makes the following (breaking) changes to the <code>tf.data</code>.</li>
<li>C++ API: - <code>IteratorBase::RestoreInternal</code>,
    <code>IteratorBase::SaveInternal</code>, and <code>DatasetBase::CheckExternalState</code>
    become pure-virtual and subclasses are now expected to provide an
    implementation.</li>
<li>The deprecated <code>DatasetBase::IsStateful</code> method is removed in favor of
    <code>DatasetBase::CheckExternalState</code>.</li>
<li>Deprecated overrides of <code>DatasetBase::MakeIterator</code> and
    <code>MakeIteratorFromInputElement</code> are removed.</li>
<li>The signature of <code>tensorflow::data::IteratorBase::SaveInternal</code> and
    <code>tensorflow::data::IteratorBase::SaveInput</code> has been extended with
    <code>SerializationContext</code> argument to enable overriding the default policy
    for the handling external state during iterator checkpointing. This is
    not a backwards compatible change and all subclasses of <code>IteratorBase</code>
    <em>need to be updated</em> accordingly.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code><ul>
<li>Add a new <code>BackupAndRestore</code> callback for handling distributed training
    failures &amp; restarts. Please take a look at this
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/tutorials/distribute/multi_worker_with_keras">tutorial</a>
    for details on how to use the callback.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.image.extract_glimpse</code> has been updated to correctly process the case
    where <code>centered=False</code> and <code>normalized=False</code>. This is a breaking change as
    the output is different from (incorrect) previous versions. Note this
    breaking change only impacts <code>tf.image.extract_glimpse</code> and
    <code>tf.compat.v2.image.extract_glimpse</code> API endpoints. The behavior of
    <code>tf.compat.v1.image.extract_glimpse</code> does not change. The behavior of
    existing C++ kernel <code>ExtractGlimpse</code> does not change either, so saved models
    using <code>tf.raw_ops.ExtractGlimpse</code> will not be impacted.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Caveats</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.lite</code><ul>
<li>Keras-based LSTM models must be converted with an explicit batch size in
    the input layer.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<h3>TF Core:</h3>
<ul>
<li>Set <code>tf2_behavior</code> to 1 to enable V2 for early loading cases.</li>
<li>Add <code>execute_fn_for_device function</code> to dynamically choose the
    implementation based on underlying device placement.</li>
<li>Eager:<ul>
<li>Add <code>reduce_logsumexp</code> benchmark with experiment compile.</li>
<li>Give <code>EagerTensor</code>s a meaningful <code>__array__</code> implementation.</li>
<li>Add another version of defun matmul for performance analysis.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.function</code>/AutoGraph:<ul>
<li><code>AutoGraph</code> now includes into TensorFlow loops any variables that are
    closed over by local functions. Previously, such variables were
    sometimes incorrectly ignored.</li>
<li>functions returned by the <code>get_concrete_function</code> method of
    <code>tf.function</code> objects can now be called with arguments consistent with
    the original arguments or type specs passed to <code>get_concrete_function</code>.
    This calling convention is now the preferred way to use concrete
    functions with nested values and composite tensors. Please check the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/concrete_function">guide</a> for more
    details on <code>concrete_ function</code>.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.function</code>'s <code>experimental_relax_shapes</code> to handle composite
    tensors appropriately.</li>
<li>Optimize <code>tf.function</code> invocation, by removing redundant list converter.</li>
<li><code>tf.function</code> will retrace when called with a different variable instead
    of simply using the <code>dtype</code> &amp; <code>shape</code>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/issues/33862">Improve support</a>
    for dynamically-sized TensorArray inside <code>tf.function</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.math</code>:<ul>
<li>Narrow down <code>argmin</code>/<code>argmax</code> contract to always return the smallest
    index for ties.</li>
<li><code>tf.math.reduce_variance</code> and <code>tf.math.reduce_std</code> return correct
    computation for complex types and no longer support integer types.</li>
<li>Add Bessel functions of order 0,1 to <code>tf.math.special</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.divide</code> now always returns a tensor to be consistent with
    documentation and other APIs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.image</code>:<ul>
<li>Replaced
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/image/non_max_suppression_padded?hl=en"><code>tf.image.non_max_suppression_padded</code></a>
    with a new implementation that supports batched inputs, which is
    considerably faster on TPUs and GPUs. Boxes with area=0 will be ignored.
    Existing usage with single inputs should still work as before.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.linalg</code><ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.linalg.banded_triangular_solve</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.random</code>:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.random.stateless_parameterized_truncated_normal</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.ragged</code>:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.ragged.cross</code> and <code>tf.ragged.cross_hashed</code> operations.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.RaggedTensor</code>:<ul>
<li><code>RaggedTensor.to_tensor()</code> now preserves static shape.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.strings.format()</code> and <code>tf.print()</code> to support RaggedTensors.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.saved_model</code>:<ul>
<li><code>@tf.function</code> from SavedModel no longer ignores args after a
    <code>RaggedTensor</code> when selecting the concrete function to run.</li>
<li>Fix save model issue for ops with a list of functions.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.saved_model.LoadOptions</code> with
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/saved_model/LoadOptions?hl=en"><code>experimental_io_device</code></a>
    as arg with default value <code>None</code> to choose the I/O device for loading
    models and weights.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.saved_model.SaveOptions</code> with
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/saved_model/SaveOptions?hl=en"><code>experimental_io_device</code></a>
    as arg with default value <code>None</code> to choose the I/O device for saving
    models and weights.</li>
<li>Mutable tables now restore checkpointed values when loaded from
    SavedModel.</li>
<li>The user object metadata field in the SavedModel proto has been
    deprecated as part of the updates to Keras SavedModel. Keras was the
    only consumer of this field prior to the update.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>GPU<ul>
<li>TF 2.3 includes PTX kernels only for
    <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/cuda-gpus">compute capability</a> 7.0 to
    reduce the TF pip binary size. Earlier releases included PTX for a
    variety of older compute capabilities.</li>
<li>Remove environmental variable <code>TF_USE_CUDNN</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Others<ul>
<li>Retain parent namescope for ops added inside
    <code>tf.while_loop</code>/<code>tf.cond</code>/<code>tf.switch_case</code>.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.vectorized_map</code> to support vectorizing <code>tf.while_loop</code> and
    TensorList operations.</li>
<li><code>tf.custom_gradient</code> can now be applied to functions that accept nested
    structures of <code>tensors</code> as inputs (instead of just a list of tensors).
    Note that Python structures such as tuples and lists now won't be
    treated as tensors, so if you still want them to be treated that way,
    you need to wrap them with <code>tf.convert_to_tensor</code>.</li>
<li>No lowering on gradient case op when input is <code>DeviceIndex</code> op.</li>
<li>Extend the ragged version of <code>tf.gather</code> to support <code>batch_dims</code> and
    <code>axis</code> args.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.map_fn</code> to support RaggedTensors and SparseTensors.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tf.group</code>. It is not useful in eager mode.</li>
<li>Add CPU and GPU implementation of modified variation of
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/raw_ops/ApplyFtrl"><code>FTRL</code></a>/<a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/raw_ops/ApplyFtrlV2"><code>FTRLV2</code></a>
    that can triggerred by <code>multiply_linear_by_lr</code> allowing a learning rate
    of zero.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><code>tf.data</code>:</h3>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.dense_to_ragged_batch</code> works correctly with tuples.</li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.dense_to_ragged_batch</code> to output variable ragged rank.</li>
<li><code>tf.data.experimental.cardinality</code> is now a method on <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.data.Dataset</code> now supports <code>len(Dataset)</code> when the cardinality is
    finite.</li>
</ul>
<h3><code>tf.distribute</code>:</h3>
<ul>
<li>Expose experimental
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/DistributedDataset?hl=en"><code>tf.distribute.DistributedDataset</code></a>
    and
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/DistributedIterator"><code>tf.distribute.DistributedIterator</code></a>
    to distribute input data when using <code>tf.distribute</code> to scale training on
    multiple devices.<ul>
<li>Added a
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/DistributedIterator?hl=en#get_next_as_optional"><code>get_next_as_optional</code></a>
    method for
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/DistributedIterator?hl=en"><code>tf.distribute.DistributedIterator</code></a>
    class to return a <code>tf.experimental.Optional</code> instance that contains the
    next value for all replicas or none instead of raising an out of range
    error. Also see <em>new</em>
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/tutorials/distribute/input">guide on input distribution</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Allow var.assign on MirroredVariables with aggregation=NONE in replica
    context. Previously this would raise an error. We now allow this because
    many users and library writers find using <code>.assign</code> in replica context to be
    more convenient, instead of having to use <code>Strategy.extended.update</code> which
    was the previous way of updating variables in this situation.</li>
<li><code>tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code> adds support for
    partial batches. Workers running out of data now continue to participate in
    the training with empty inputs, instead of raising an error. Learn more
    about
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/tutorials/distribute/input#partial_batches">partial batches here</a>.</li>
<li>Improve the performance of reading metrics eagerly under
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code>.</li>
<li>Fix the issue that <code>strategy.reduce()</code> inside <code>tf.function</code> may raise
    exceptions when the values to reduce are from loops or if-clauses.</li>
<li>Fix the issue that <code>tf.distribute.MirroredStrategy</code> cannot be used together
    with <code>tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code>.</li>
<li>Add a <code>tf.distribute.cluster_resolver.TPUClusterResolver.connect</code> API to
    simplify TPU initialization.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.distribute.Strategy.gather</code> and
    <code>tf.distribute.ReplicaContext.all_gather</code> methods to gather and concatenate
    <code>tf.distribute.DistributedValues</code> across workers and devices.</li>
</ul>
<h3><code>tf.keras</code>:</h3>
<ul>
<li>Introduces experimental preprocessing layers API
    (<code>tf.keras.layers.experimental.preprocessing</code>) to handle data preprocessing
    operations such as categorical feature encoding, text vectorization, data
    normalization, and data discretization (binning). The newly added layers
    provide a replacement for the legacy feature column API, and support
    composite tensor inputs.</li>
<li>Added <strong>categorical data</strong> processing layers:<ul>
<li><code>IntegerLookup</code> &amp; <code>StringLookup</code>: build an index of categorical feature
    values</li>
<li><code>CategoryEncoding</code>: turn integer-encoded categories into one-hot,
    multi-hot, or tf-idf encoded representations</li>
<li><code>CategoryCrossing</code>: create new categorical features representing
    co-occurrences of previous categorical feature values</li>
<li><code>Hashing</code>: the hashing trick, for large-vocabulary categorical features</li>
<li><code>Discretization</code>: turn continuous numerical features into categorical
    features by binning their values</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Improved <strong>image preprocessing</strong> layers: <code>CenterCrop</code>, <code>Rescaling</code></li>
<li>Improved <strong>image augmentation</strong> layers: <code>RandomCrop</code>, <code>RandomFlip</code>,
    <code>RandomTranslation</code>, <code>RandomRotation</code>, <code>RandomHeight</code>, <code>RandomWidth</code>,
    <code>RandomZoom</code>, <code>RandomContrast</code></li>
<li>Improved <strong><code>TextVectorization</code></strong> layer, which handles string tokenization,
    n-gram generation, and token encoding<ul>
<li>The <code>TextVectorization</code> layer now accounts for the mask_token as part of
    the vocabulary size when output_mode='int'. This means that, if you have
    a max_tokens value of 5000, your output will have 5000 unique values
    (not 5001 as before).</li>
<li>Change the return value of <code>TextVectorization.get_vocabulary()</code> from
    <code>byte</code> to <code>string</code>. Users who previously were calling 'decode' on the
    output of this method should no longer need to do so.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Introduce new Keras dataset generation utilities :<ul>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/keras/preprocessing/image_dataset_from_directory"><code>image_dataset_from_directory</code></a></strong>
    is a utility based on <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>, meant to replace the legacy
    <code>ImageDataGenerator</code>. It takes you from a structured directory of images
    to a labeled dataset, in one function call. Note that it doesn't perform
    image data augmentation (which is meant to be done using preprocessing
    layers).</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/keras/preprocessing/text_dataset_from_directory"><code>text_dataset_from_directory</code></a></strong>
    takes you from a structured directory of text files to a labeled
    dataset, in one function call.</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/keras/preprocessing/timeseries_dataset_from_array"><code>timeseries_dataset_from_array</code></a></strong>
    is a <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>-based replacement of the legacy
    <code>TimeseriesGenerator</code>. It takes you from an array of timeseries data to
    a dataset of shifting windows with their targets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/keras/Model?hl=en#compile"><code>experimental_steps_per_execution</code></a>
    arg to <code>model.compile</code> to indicate the number of batches to run per
    <code>tf.function</code> call. This can speed up Keras Models on TPUs up to 3x.</li>
<li>Extends <code>tf.keras.layers.Lambda</code> layers to support multi-argument lambdas,
    and keyword arguments when calling the layer.</li>
<li>Functional models now get constructed if <em>any</em> tensor in a layer call's
    arguments/keyword arguments comes from a keras input. Previously the
    functional api would only work if all of the elements in the first argument
    to the layer came from a keras input.</li>
<li>Clean up <code>BatchNormalization</code> layer's <code>trainable</code> property to act like
    standard python state when it's used inside <code>tf.functions</code> (frozen at
    tracing time), instead of acting like a pseudo-variable whose updates <em>kind
    of sometimes</em> get reflected in already-traced <code>tf.function</code> traces.</li>
<li>Add the <code>Conv1DTranspose</code> layer.</li>
<li>Refine the semantics of <code>SensitivitySpecificityBase</code> derived metrics. See
    the updated API docstrings for
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/keras/metrics/SensitivityAtSpecificity"><code>tf.keras.metrics.SensitivityAtSpecificity</code></a>
    and
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r2.3/api_docs/python/tf/keras/metrics/SpecificityAtSensitivity"><code>tf.keras.metrics.SpecificityAtSensitivty</code></a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><code>tf.lite</code>:</h3>
<ul>
<li>Converter<ul>
<li>Restored <code>inference_input_type</code> and <code>inference_output_type</code> flags in TF
    2.x TFLiteConverter (backward compatible with TF 1.x) to support integer
    (tf.int8, tf.uint8) input and output types in post training full integer
    quantized models.</li>
<li>Added support for converting and resizing models with dynamic
    (placeholder) dimensions. Previously, there was only limited support for
    dynamic batch size, and even that did not guarantee that the model could
    be properly resized at runtime.<ul>
<li>Enabled experimental support for a new quantization mode with 16-bit
    activations and 8-bit weights. See
    <code>lite.OpsSet.EXPERIMENTAL_TFLITE_BUILTINS_ACTIVATIONS_INT16_WEIGHTS_INT8</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>CPU<ul>
<li>Fix an issue w/ dynamic weights and <code>Conv2D</code> on x86.</li>
<li>Add a runtime Android flag for enabling <code>XNNPACK</code> for optimized CPU
    performance.</li>
<li>Add a runtime iOS flag for enabling <code>XNNPACK</code> for optimized CPU
    performance.</li>
<li>Add a compiler flag to enable building a TFLite library that applies
    <code>XNNPACK</code> delegate automatically when the model has a <code>fp32</code> operation.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>GPU<ul>
<li>Allow GPU acceleration starting with internal graph nodes</li>
<li>Experimental support for quantized models with the Android GPU delegate</li>
<li>Add GPU delegate whitelist.</li>
<li>Rename GPU whitelist -&gt; compatibility (list).</li>
<li>Improve GPU compatibility list entries from crash reports.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>NNAPI<ul>
<li>Set default value for
    <code>StatefulNnApiDelegate::Options::max_number_delegated_partitions</code> to 3.</li>
<li>Add capability to disable <code>NNAPI</code> CPU and check <code>NNAPI</code> Errno.</li>
<li>Fix crashes when using <code>NNAPI</code> with target accelerator specified with
    model containing Conv2d or FullyConnected or LSTM nodes with quantized
    weights.</li>
<li>Fix <code>ANEURALNETWORKS_BAD_DATA</code> execution failures with
    <code>sum</code>/<code>max</code>/<code>min</code>/<code>reduce</code> operations with <code>scalar</code> inputs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Hexagon<ul>
<li>TFLite Hexagon Delegate out of experimental.</li>
<li>Experimental <code>int8</code> support for most hexagon ops.</li>
<li>Experimental per-channel quant support for <code>conv</code> in Hexagon delegate.</li>
<li>Support dynamic batch size in C++ API.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>CoreML<ul>
<li>Opensource CoreML delegate</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Misc<ul>
<li>Enable building Android TFLite targets on Windows</li>
<li>Add support for <code>BatchMatMul</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for <code>half_pixel_centers</code> with <code>ResizeNearestNeighbor</code>.</li>
<li>Add 3D support for <code>BatchToSpaceND</code>.</li>
<li>Add 5D support for <code>BroadcastSub</code>, <code>Maximum</code>, <code>Minimum</code>, <code>Transpose</code> and
    <code>BroadcastDiv</code>.</li>
<li>Rename <code>kTfLiteActRelu1</code> to <code>kTfLiteActReluN1To1</code>.</li>
<li>Enable flex delegate on tensorflow.lite.Interpreter Python package.</li>
<li>Add <code>Buckettize</code>, <code>SparseCross</code> and <code>BoostedTreesBucketize</code> to the flex
    whitelist.</li>
<li>Add support for selective registration of flex ops.</li>
<li>Add missing kernels for flex delegate whitelisted ops.</li>
<li>Fix issue when using direct <code>ByteBuffer</code> inputs with graphs that have
    dynamic shapes.</li>
<li>Fix error checking supported operations in a model containing
    <code>HardSwish</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3>Packaging Support</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>tf.sysconfig.get_build_info()</code>. Returns a dict that describes the
    build environment of the currently installed TensorFlow package, e.g. the
    NVIDIA CUDA and NVIDIA CuDNN versions used when TensorFlow was built.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Profiler</h3>
<ul>
<li>Fix a subtle use-after-free issue in <code>XStatVisitor::RefValue()</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h3>TPU Enhancements</h3>
<ul>
<li>Adds 3D mesh support in TPU configurations ops.</li>
<li>Added TPU code for <code>FTRL</code> with <code>multiply_linear_by_lr</code>.</li>
<li>Silently adds a new file system registry at <code>gstpu</code>.</li>
<li>Support <code>restartType</code> in cloud tpu client.</li>
<li>Depend on a specific version of google-api-python-client.</li>
<li>Fixes apiclient import.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Tracing and Debugging</h3>
<ul>
<li>Add a <code>TFE_Py_Execute</code> traceme.</li>
</ul>
<h3>XLA Support</h3>
<ul>
<li>Implement stable <code>argmin</code> and <code>argmax</code></li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 2.2.0</h1>
<p>TensorFlow 2.2 discontinues support for Python 2,
<a href="https://groups.google.com/a/tensorflow.org/d/msg/announce/gVwS5RC8mds/dCt1ka2XAAAJ">previously announced</a>
as following
<a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0373/#update">Python 2's EOL on January 1, 2020</a>.</p>
<p>Coinciding with this change, new releases of
<a href="https://hub.docker.com/r/tensorflow/tensorflow/">TensorFlow's Docker images</a>
provide Python 3 exclusively. Because all images now use Python 3, Docker tags
containing <code>-py3</code> will no longer be provided and existing <code>-py3</code> tags like
<code>latest-py3</code> will not be updated.</p>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Replaced the scalar type for string tensors from <code>std::string</code> to
    <code>tensorflow::tstring</code> which is now ABI stable.</li>
<li>A new Profiler for TF 2 for CPU/GPU/TPU. It offers both device and host
    performance analysis, including input pipeline and TF Ops. Optimization
    advisory is provided whenever possible. Please see
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/tensorboard/tensorboard_profiling_keras">this tutorial</a>
    and <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/profiler">guide</a> for usage guidelines.</li>
<li>Export C++ functions to Python using <code>pybind11</code> as opposed to <code>SWIG</code> as a
    part of our
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/community/blob/master/rfcs/20190208-pybind11.md">deprecation of swig efforts</a>.</li>
<li><code>tf.distribute</code>:<ul>
<li>Support added for global sync <code>BatchNormalization</code> by using the newly
    added <code>tf.keras.layers.experimental.SyncBatchNormalization</code> layer. This
    layer will sync <code>BatchNormalization</code> statistics every step across all
    replicas taking part in sync training.</li>
<li>Performance improvements for GPU multi-worker distributed training using
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code></li>
<li>Update NVIDIA <code>NCCL</code> to <code>2.5.7-1</code> for better performance and performance
    tuning. Please see
    <a href="https://docs.nvidia.com/deeplearning/sdk/nccl-developer-guide/docs/env.html">nccl developer guide</a>
    for more information on this.</li>
<li>Support gradient <code>allreduce</code> in <code>float16</code>. See this
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/models/blob/master/official/modeling/grad_utils.py">example</a>
    usage.</li>
<li>Experimental support of
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/distribute/experimental/CollectiveHints">all reduce gradient packing</a>
    to allow overlapping gradient aggregation with backward path
    computation.</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>experimental_run_v2</code> method for distribution strategies and
    renamed the method <code>run</code> as it is no longer experimental.</li>
<li>Add CompositeTensor support for DistributedIterators. This should help
    prevent unnecessary function retracing and memory leaks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>Model.fit</code> major improvements:<ul>
<li>You can now use custom training logic with <code>Model.fit</code> by overriding
    <code>Model.train_step</code>.</li>
<li>Easily write state-of-the-art training loops without worrying about
    all of the features <code>Model.fit</code> handles for you (distribution
    strategies, callbacks, data formats, looping logic, etc)</li>
<li>See the default
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/1381fc8e15e22402417b98e3881dfd409998daea/tensorflow/python/keras/engine/training.py#L540"><code>Model.train_step</code></a>
    for an example of what this function should look like. Same applies
    for validation and inference via <code>Model.test_step</code> and
    <code>Model.predict_step</code>.</li>
<li>SavedModel uses its own <code>Model._saved_model_inputs_spec</code> attr now
    instead of relying on <code>Model.inputs</code> and <code>Model.input_names</code>, which
    are no longer set for subclass Models. This attr is set in eager,
    <code>tf.function</code>, and graph modes. This gets rid of the need for users
    to manually call <code>Model._set_inputs</code> when using Custom Training
    Loops(CTLs).</li>
<li>Dynamic shapes are supported for generators by calling the Model on
    the first batch we "peek" from the generator. This used to happen
    implicitly in <code>Model._standardize_user_data</code>. Long-term, a solution
    where the <code>DataAdapter</code> doesn't need to call the Model is probably
    preferable.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The SavedModel format now supports all Keras built-in layers (including
    metrics, preprocessing layers, and stateful RNN layers)</li>
<li>Update Keras batch normalization layer to use the running mean and
    average computation in the <code>fused_batch_norm</code>. You should see
    significant performance improvements when using <code>fused_batch_norm</code> in
    Eager mode.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Enable TFLite experimental new converter by default.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>XLA</p>
<ul>
<li>XLA now builds and works on windows. All prebuilt packages come with XLA
    available.</li>
<li>XLA can be
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/xla#explicit_compilation_with_tffunction">enabled for a <code>tf.function</code></a>
    with “compile or throw exception” semantics on CPU and GPU.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>In <code>tf.keras.applications</code> the name of the "top" layer has been
    standardized to "predictions". This is only a problem if your code
    relies on the exact name of the layer.</li>
<li>Huber loss function has been updated to be consistent with other Keras
    losses. It now computes mean over the last axis of per-sample losses
    before applying the reduction function.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>AutoGraph no longer converts functions passed to <code>tf.py_function</code>,
    <code>tf.py_func</code> and <code>tf.numpy_function</code>.</li>
<li>Deprecating <code>XLA_CPU</code> and <code>XLA_GPU</code> devices with this release.</li>
<li>Increasing the minimum bazel version to build TF to 2.0.0 to use Bazel's
    <code>cc_experimental_shared_library</code>.</li>
<li>Keras compile/fit behavior for functional and subclassed models have been
    unified. Model properties such as <code>metrics</code>, <code>metrics_names</code> will now be
    available only after <strong>training/evaluating the model on actual data</strong> for
    functional models. <code>metrics</code> will <strong>now include</strong> model <code>loss</code> and output
    losses.<code>loss_functions</code> property has been removed from the model. This was
    an undocumented property that was accidentally public and has now been
    removed.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Caveats</h2>
<ul>
<li>The current TensorFlow release now <strong>requires</strong>
    <a href="https://pypi.org/project/gast/">gast</a> version 0.3.3.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li>Removed <code>autotune_algorithm</code> from experimental optimization options.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TF Core:<ul>
<li><code>tf.constant</code> always creates CPU tensors irrespective of the current
    device context.</li>
<li>Eager <code>TensorHandles</code> maintain a list of mirrors for any copies to local
    or remote devices. This avoids any redundant copies due to op execution.</li>
<li>For <code>tf.Tensor</code> &amp; <code>tf.Variable</code>, <code>.experimental_ref()</code> is no longer
    experimental and is available as simply <code>.ref()</code>.</li>
<li><code>pfor/vectorized_map</code>: Added support for vectorizing 56 more ops.
    Vectorizing <code>tf.cond</code> is also supported now.</li>
<li>Set as much partial shape as we can infer statically within the gradient
    impl of the gather op.</li>
<li>Gradient of <code>tf.while_loop</code> emits <code>StatelessWhile</code> op if <code>cond</code> and body
    functions are stateless. This allows multiple gradients while ops to run
    in parallel under distribution strategy.</li>
<li>Speed up <code>GradientTape</code> in eager mode by auto-generating list of op
    inputs/outputs which are unused and hence not cached for gradient
    functions.</li>
<li>Support <code>back_prop=False</code> in <code>while_v2</code> but mark it as deprecated.</li>
<li>Improve error message when attempting to use <code>None</code> in data-dependent
    control flow.</li>
<li>Add <code>RaggedTensor.numpy()</code>.</li>
<li>Update <code>RaggedTensor.__getitem__</code> to preserve uniform dimensions &amp; allow
    indexing into uniform dimensions.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.expand_dims</code> to always insert the new dimension as a
    non-ragged dimension.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.embedding_lookup</code> to use <code>partition_strategy</code> and <code>max_norm</code>
    when <code>ids</code> is ragged.</li>
<li>Allow <code>batch_dims==rank(indices)</code> in <code>tf.gather</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for bfloat16 in <code>tf.print</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.distribute</code>:<ul>
<li>Support <code>embedding_column</code> with variable-length input features for
    <code>MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>Added <code>experimental_aggregate_gradients</code> argument to
    <code>tf.keras.optimizer.Optimizer.apply_gradients</code>. This allows custom
    gradient aggregation and processing aggregated gradients in custom
    training loop.</li>
<li>Allow <code>pathlib.Path</code> paths for loading models via Keras API.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.function</code>/AutoGraph:<ul>
<li>AutoGraph is now available in <code>ReplicaContext.merge_call</code>,
    <code>Strategy.extended.update</code> and <code>Strategy.extended.update_non_slot</code>.</li>
<li>Experimental support for shape invariants has been enabled in
    <code>tf.function</code>. See the API docs for
    <code>tf.autograph.experimental.set_loop_options</code> for additional info.</li>
<li>AutoGraph error messages now exclude frames corresponding to APIs
    internal to AutoGraph.</li>
<li>Improve shape inference for <code>tf.function</code> input arguments to unlock more
    Grappler optimizations in TensorFlow 2.x.</li>
<li>Improve automatic control dependency management of resources by allowing
    resource reads to occur in parallel and synchronizing only on writes.</li>
<li>Fix execution order of multiple stateful calls to <code>experimental_run_v2</code>
    in <code>tf.function</code>.</li>
<li>You can now iterate over <code>RaggedTensors</code> using a for loop inside
    <code>tf.function</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.lite</code>:<ul>
<li>Migrated the <code>tf.lite</code> C inference API out of experimental into lite/c.</li>
<li>Add an option to disallow <code>NNAPI</code> CPU / partial acceleration on Android
    10</li>
<li>TFLite Android AARs now include the C headers and APIs are required to
    use TFLite from native code.</li>
<li>Refactors the delegate and delegate kernel sources to allow usage in the
    linter.</li>
<li>Limit delegated ops to actually supported ones if a device name is
    specified or <code>NNAPI</code> CPU Fallback is disabled.</li>
<li>TFLite now supports <code>tf.math.reciprocal1</code> op by lowering to <code>tf.div op</code>.</li>
<li>TFLite's unpack op now supports boolean tensor inputs.</li>
<li>Microcontroller and embedded code moved from experimental to main
    TensorFlow Lite folder</li>
<li>Check for large TFLite tensors.</li>
<li>Fix GPU delegate crash with C++17.</li>
<li>Add 5D support to TFLite <code>strided_slice</code>.</li>
<li>Fix error in delegation of <code>DEPTH_TO_SPACE</code> to <code>NNAPI</code> causing op not to
    be accelerated.</li>
<li>Fix segmentation fault when running a model with LSTM nodes using
    <code>NNAPI</code> Delegate</li>
<li>Fix <code>NNAPI</code> delegate failure when an operand for Maximum/Minimum
    operation is a scalar.</li>
<li>Fix <code>NNAPI</code> delegate failure when Axis input for reduce operation is a
    scalar.</li>
<li>Expose option to limit the number of partitions that will be delegated
    to <code>NNAPI</code>.</li>
<li>If a target accelerator is specified, use its feature level to determine
    operations to delegate instead of SDK version.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.random</code>:<ul>
<li>Various random number generation improvements:</li>
<li>Add a fast path for default <code>random_uniform</code></li>
<li><code>random_seed</code> documentation improvement.</li>
<li><code>RandomBinomial</code> broadcasts and appends the sample shape to the left
    rather than the right.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.random.stateless_binomial</code>, <code>tf.random.stateless_gamma</code>,
    <code>tf.random.stateless_poisson</code></li>
<li><code>tf.random.stateless_uniform</code> now supports unbounded sampling of <code>int</code>
    types.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Math and Linear Algebra:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.linalg.LinearOperatorTridiag</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>LinearOperatorBlockLowerTriangular</code></li>
<li>Add broadcasting support to
    tf.linalg.triangular_solve<a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/issues/26204">#26204</a>,
    tf.math.invert_permutation.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.sobol_sample</code> op.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.xlog1py</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.special.{dawsn,expi,fresnel_cos,fresnel_sin,spence}</code>.</li>
<li>Add a Modified Discrete Cosine Transform (MDCT) and its inverse to
    <code>tf.signal</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TPU Enhancements:<ul>
<li>Refactor <code>TpuClusterResolver</code> to move shared logic to a separate pip
    package.</li>
<li>Support configuring TPU software version from cloud tpu client.</li>
<li>Allowed TPU embedding weight decay factor to be multiplied by learning
    rate.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>XLA Support:<ul>
<li>Add standalone XLA AOT runtime target + relevant .cc sources to pip
    package.</li>
<li>Add check for memory alignment to MemoryAllocation::MemoryAllocation()
    on 32-bit ARM. This ensures a deterministic early exit instead of a hard
    to debug bus error later.</li>
<li><code>saved_model_cli aot_compile_cpu</code> allows you to compile saved models to
    XLA header+object files and include them in your C++ programs.</li>
<li>Enable <code>Igamma</code>, <code>Igammac</code> for XLA.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Deterministic Op Functionality:<ul>
<li>XLA reduction emitter is deterministic when the environment variable
    <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> is set to "true" or "1". This extends
    deterministic <code>tf.nn.bias_add</code> back-prop functionality (and therefore
    also deterministic back-prop of bias-addition in Keras layers) to
    include when XLA JIT compilation is enabled.</li>
<li>Fix problem, when running on a CUDA GPU and when either environment
    variable <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> or environment variable
    <code>TF_CUDNN_DETERMINISTIC</code> is set to "true" or "1", in which some layer
    configurations led to an exception with the message "No algorithm
    worked!"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Tracing and Debugging:<ul>
<li>Add source, destination name to <code>_send</code> traceme to allow easier
    debugging.</li>
<li>Add traceme event to <code>fastpathexecute</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Fix an issue with AUC.reset_states for multi-label AUC
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/issues/35852">#35852</a></li>
<li>Fix the TF upgrade script to not delete files when there is a parsing
    error and the output mode is <code>in-place</code>.</li>
<li>Move <code>tensorflow/core:framework/*_pyclif</code> rules to
    <code>tensorflow/core/framework:*_pyclif</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 2.0.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a security vulnerability where converting a Python string to a
    <code>tf.float16</code> value produces a segmentation fault
    (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2020-5215">CVE-2020-5215</a>)</li>
<li>Updates <code>curl</code> to <code>7.66.0</code> to handle
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2019-5482">CVE-2019-5482</a>
    and
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2019-5481">CVE-2019-5481</a></li>
<li>Updates <code>sqlite3</code> to <code>3.30.01</code> to handle
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2019-19646">CVE-2019-19646</a>,
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2019-19645">CVE-2019-19645</a>
    and
    <a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2019-16168">CVE-2019-16168</a></li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 2.1.0</h1>
<p>TensorFlow 2.1 will be the last TF release supporting Python 2. Python 2 support
<a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0373/#update">officially ends an January 1, 2020</a>.
<a href="https://groups.google.com/a/tensorflow.org/d/msg/announce/gVwS5RC8mds/dCt1ka2XAAAJ">As announced earlier</a>,
TensorFlow will also stop supporting Python 2 starting January 1, 2020, and no
more releases are expected in 2019.</p>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>The <code>tensorflow</code> pip package now includes GPU support by default (same as
    <code>tensorflow-gpu</code>) for both Linux and Windows. This runs on machines with and
    without NVIDIA GPUs. <code>tensorflow-gpu</code> is still available, and CPU-only
    packages can be downloaded at <code>tensorflow-cpu</code> for users who are concerned
    about package size.</li>
<li><strong>Windows users:</strong> Officially-released <code>tensorflow</code> Pip packages are now
    built with Visual Studio 2019 version 16.4 in order to take advantage of the
    new <code>/d2ReducedOptimizeHugeFunctions</code> compiler flag. To use these new
    packages, you must install "Microsoft Visual C++ Redistributable for Visual
    Studio 2015, 2017 and 2019", available from Microsoft's website
    <a href="https://support.microsoft.com/help/2977003/the-latest-supported-visual-c-downloads">here</a>.<ul>
<li>This does not change the minimum required version for building
    TensorFlow from source on Windows, but builds enabling
    <code>EIGEN_STRONG_INLINE</code> can take over 48 hours to compile without this
    flag. Refer to <code>configure.py</code> for more information about
    <code>EIGEN_STRONG_INLINE</code> and <code>/d2ReducedOptimizeHugeFunctions</code>.</li>
<li>If either of the required DLLs, <code>msvcp140.dll</code> (old) or <code>msvcp140_1.dll</code>
    (new), are missing on your machine, <code>import tensorflow</code> will print a
    warning message.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <code>tensorflow</code> pip package is built with CUDA 10.1 and cuDNN 7.6.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code><ul>
<li>Experimental support for mixed precision is available on GPUs and Cloud
    TPUs. See
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/keras/mixed_precision">usage guide</a>.</li>
<li>Introduced the <code>TextVectorization</code> layer, which takes as input raw
    strings and takes care of text standardization, tokenization, n-gram
    generation, and vocabulary indexing. See this
    <a href="https://colab.research.google.com/drive/1RvCnR7h0_l4Ekn5vINWToI9TNJdpUZB3">end-to-end text classification example</a>.</li>
<li>Keras <code>.compile</code> <code>.fit</code> <code>.evaluate</code> and <code>.predict</code> are allowed to be
    outside of the DistributionStrategy scope, as long as the model was
    constructed inside of a scope.</li>
<li>Experimental support for Keras <code>.compile</code>, <code>.fit</code>, <code>.evaluate</code>, and
    <code>.predict</code> is available for Cloud TPUs, Cloud TPU, for all types of
    Keras models (sequential, functional and subclassing models).</li>
<li>Automatic outside compilation is now enabled for Cloud TPUs. This allows
    <code>tf.summary</code> to be used more conveniently with Cloud TPUs.</li>
<li>Dynamic batch sizes with DistributionStrategy and Keras are supported on
    Cloud TPUs.</li>
<li>Support for <code>.fit</code>, <code>.evaluate</code>, <code>.predict</code> on TPU using numpy data, in
    addition to <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>.</li>
<li>Keras reference implementations for many popular models are available in
    the TensorFlow
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/models/tree/master/official">Model Garden</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code><ul>
<li>Changes rebatching for <code>tf.data datasets</code> + DistributionStrategy for
    better performance. Note that the dataset also behaves slightly
    differently, in that the rebatched dataset cardinality will always be a
    multiple of the number of replicas.</li>
<li><code>tf.data.Dataset</code> now supports automatic data distribution and sharding
    in distributed environments, including on TPU pods.</li>
<li>Distribution policies for <code>tf.data.Dataset</code> can now be tuned with 1.
    <code>tf.data.experimental.AutoShardPolicy(OFF, AUTO, FILE, DATA)</code> 2.
    <code>tf.data.experimental.ExternalStatePolicy(WARN, IGNORE, FAIL)</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.debugging</code><ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.debugging.enable_check_numerics()</code> and
    <code>tf.debugging.disable_check_numerics()</code> to help debugging the root
    causes of issues involving infinities and <code>NaN</code>s.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.distribute</code><ul>
<li>Custom training loop support on TPUs and TPU pods is available through
    <code>strategy.experimental_distribute_dataset</code>,
    <code>strategy.experimental_distribute_datasets_from_function</code>,
    <code>strategy.experimental_run_v2</code>, <code>strategy.reduce</code>.</li>
<li>Support for a global distribution strategy through
    <code>tf.distribute.experimental_set_strategy(),</code> in addition to
    <code>strategy.scope()</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>TensorRT</code><ul>
<li><a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/tensorrt#tensorrt-whats-new">TensorRT 6.0</a>
    is now supported and enabled by default. This adds support for more
    TensorFlow ops including Conv3D, Conv3DBackpropInputV2, AvgPool3D,
    MaxPool3D, ResizeBilinear, and ResizeNearestNeighbor. In addition, the
    TensorFlow-TensorRT python conversion API is exported as
    <code>tf.experimental.tensorrt.Converter</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Environment variable <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> has been added. When set to
    "true" or "1", this environment variable makes <code>tf.nn.bias_add</code> operate
    deterministically (i.e. reproducibly), but currently only when XLA JIT
    compilation is <em>not</em> enabled. Setting <code>TF_DETERMINISTIC_OPS</code> to "true" or
    "1" also makes cuDNN convolution and max-pooling operate deterministically.
    This makes Keras Conv*D and MaxPool*D layers operate deterministically in
    both the forward and backward directions when running on a CUDA-enabled GPU.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Deletes <code>Operation.traceback_with_start_lines</code> for which we know of no
    usages.</li>
<li>Removed <code>id</code> from <code>tf.Tensor.__repr__()</code> as <code>id</code> is not useful other than
    internal debugging.</li>
<li>Some <code>tf.assert_*</code> methods now raise assertions at operation creation time
    if the input tensors' values are known at that time, not during the
    <code>session.run()</code>. This only changes behavior when the graph execution would
    have resulted in an error. When this happens, a noop is returned and the
    input tensors are marked non-feedable. In other words, if they are used as
    keys in <code>feed_dict</code> argument to <code>session.run()</code>, an error will be raised.
    Also, because some assert ops don't make it into the graph, the graph
    structure changes. A different graph can result in different per-op random
    seeds when they are not given explicitly (most often).</li>
<li>The following APIs are not longer experimental:
    <code>tf.config.list_logical_devices</code>, <code>tf.config.list_physical_devices</code>,
    <code>tf.config.get_visible_devices</code>, <code>tf.config.set_visible_devices</code>,
    <code>tf.config.get_logical_device_configuration</code>,
    <code>tf.config.set_logical_device_configuration</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.config.experimentalVirtualDeviceConfiguration</code> has been renamed to
    <code>tf.config.LogicalDeviceConfiguration</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.config.experimental_list_devices</code> has been removed, please use
    <code>tf.config.list_logical_devices</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.data</code><ul>
<li>Fixes concurrency issue with <code>tf.data.experimental.parallel_interleave</code>
    with <code>sloppy=True</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.data.experimental.dense_to_ragged_batch()</code>.</li>
<li>Extend <code>tf.data</code> parsing ops to support <code>RaggedTensors</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.distribute</code><ul>
<li>Fix issue where GRU would crash or give incorrect output when a
    <code>tf.distribute.Strategy</code> was used.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.estimator</code><ul>
<li>Added option in <code>tf.estimator.CheckpointSaverHook</code> to not save the
    <code>GraphDef</code>.</li>
<li>Moving the checkpoint reader from swig to pybind11.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code><ul>
<li>Export <code>depthwise_conv2d</code> in <code>tf.keras.backend</code>.</li>
<li>In Keras Layers and Models, Variables in <code>trainable_weights</code>,
    <code>non_trainable_weights</code>, and <code>weights</code> are explicitly deduplicated.</li>
<li>Keras <code>model.load_weights</code> now accepts <code>skip_mismatch</code> as an argument.
    This was available in external Keras, and has now been copied over to
    <code>tf.keras</code>.</li>
<li>Fix the input shape caching behavior of Keras convolutional layers.</li>
<li><code>Model.fit_generator</code>, <code>Model.evaluate_generator</code>,
    <code>Model.predict_generator</code>, <code>Model.train_on_batch</code>,
    <code>Model.test_on_batch</code>, and <code>Model.predict_on_batch</code> methods now respect
    the <code>run_eagerly</code> property, and will correctly run using <code>tf.function</code>
    by default. Note that <code>Model.fit_generator</code>, <code>Model.evaluate_generator</code>,
    and <code>Model.predict_generator</code> are deprecated endpoints. They are
    subsumed by <code>Model.fit</code>, <code>Model.evaluate</code>, and <code>Model.predict</code> which now
    support generators and Sequences.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.lite</code><ul>
<li>Legalization for <code>NMS</code> ops in TFLite.</li>
<li>add <code>narrow_range</code> and <code>axis</code> to <code>quantize_v2</code> and <code>dequantize</code> ops.</li>
<li>Added support for <code>FusedBatchNormV3</code> in converter.</li>
<li>Add an <code>errno</code>-like field to <code>NNAPI</code> delegate for detecting <code>NNAPI</code>
    errors for fallback behaviour.</li>
<li>Refactors <code>NNAPI</code> Delegate to support detailed reason why an operation
    is not accelerated.</li>
<li>Converts hardswish subgraphs into atomic ops.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other<ul>
<li>Critical stability updates for TPUs, especially in cases where the XLA
    compiler produces compilation errors.</li>
<li>TPUs can now be re-initialized multiple times, using
    <code>tf.tpu.experimental.initialize_tpu_system</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>RaggedTensor.merge_dims()</code>.</li>
<li>Added new <code>uniform_row_length</code> row-partitioning tensor to
    <code>RaggedTensor</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>shape</code> arg to <code>RaggedTensor.to_tensor</code>; Improve speed of
    <code>RaggedTensor.to_tensor</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.io.parse_sequence_example</code> and <code>tf.io.parse_single_sequence_example</code>
    now support ragged features.</li>
<li>Fix <code>while_v2</code> with variables in custom gradient.</li>
<li>Support taking gradients of V2 <code>tf.cond</code> and <code>tf.while_loop</code> using
    <code>LookupTable</code>.</li>
<li>Fix bug where <code>vectorized_map</code> failed on inputs with unknown static
    shape.</li>
<li>Add preliminary support for sparse CSR matrices.</li>
<li>Tensor equality with <code>None</code> now behaves as expected.</li>
<li>Make calls to <code>tf.function(f)()</code>, <code>tf.function(f).get_concrete_function</code>
    and <code>tf.function(f).get_initialization_function</code> thread-safe.</li>
<li>Extend <code>tf.identity</code> to work with CompositeTensors (such as
    SparseTensor)</li>
<li>Added more <code>dtypes</code> and zero-sized inputs to <code>Einsum</code> Op and improved
    its performance</li>
<li>Enable multi-worker <code>NCCL</code> <code>all-reduce</code> inside functions executing
    eagerly.</li>
<li>Added complex128 support to <code>RFFT</code>, <code>RFFT2D</code>, <code>RFFT3D</code>, <code>IRFFT</code>,
    <code>IRFFT2D</code>, and <code>IRFFT3D</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>pfor</code> converter for <code>SelfAdjointEigV2</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.ndtri</code> and <code>tf.math.erfinv</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.config.experimental.enable_mlir_bridge</code> to allow using MLIR
    compiler bridge in eager model.</li>
<li>Added support for MatrixSolve on Cloud TPU / XLA.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.autodiff.ForwardAccumulator</code> for forward-mode autodiff</li>
<li>Add <code>LinearOperatorPermutation</code>.</li>
<li>A few performance optimizations on <code>tf.reduce_logsumexp</code>.</li>
<li>Added multilabel handling to <code>AUC</code> metric</li>
<li>Optimization on <code>zeros_like</code>.</li>
<li>Dimension constructor now requires <code>None</code> or types with an <code>__index__</code>
    method.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.random.uniform</code> microbenchmark.</li>
<li>Use <code>_protogen</code> suffix for proto library targets instead of
    <code>_cc_protogen</code> suffix.</li>
<li>Moving the checkpoint reader from <code>swig</code> to <code>pybind11</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.device</code> &amp; <code>MirroredStrategy</code> now supports passing in a
    <code>tf.config.LogicalDevice</code></li>
<li>If you're building Tensorflow from source, consider using
    <a href="https://github.com/bazelbuild/bazelisk">bazelisk</a> to automatically
    download and use the correct Bazel version. Bazelisk reads the
    <code>.bazelversion</code> file at the root of the project directory.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.15.0</h1>
<p>This is the last 1.x release for TensorFlow. We do not expect to update the 1.x
branch with features, although we will issue patch releases to fix
vulnerabilities for at least one year.</p>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>As
    <a href="https://groups.google.com/a/tensorflow.org/forum/#!topic/developers/iRCt5m4qUz0">announced</a>,
    <code>tensorflow</code> pip package will by default include GPU support (same as
    <code>tensorflow-gpu</code> now) for the platforms we currently have GPU support (Linux
    and Windows). It will work on machines with and without Nvidia GPUs.
    <code>tensorflow-gpu</code> will still be available, and CPU-only packages can be
    downloaded at <code>tensorflow-cpu</code> for users who are concerned about package
    size.</li>
<li>TensorFlow 1.15 contains a complete implementation of the 2.0 API in its
    <code>compat.v2</code> module. It contains a copy of the 1.15 main module (without
    <code>contrib</code>) in the <code>compat.v1</code> module. TensorFlow 1.15 is able to emulate 2.0
    behavior using the <code>enable_v2_behavior()</code> function. This enables writing
    forward compatible code: by explicitly importing either
    <code>tensorflow.compat.v1</code> or <code>tensorflow.compat.v2</code>, you can ensure that your
    code works without modifications against an installation of 1.15 or 2.0.</li>
<li>EagerTensor now supports numpy buffer interface for tensors.</li>
<li>Add toggles <code>tf.enable_control_flow_v2()</code> and <code>tf.disable_control_flow_v2()</code>
    for enabling/disabling v2 control flow.</li>
<li>Enable v2 control flow as part of <code>tf.enable_v2_behavior()</code> and
    <code>TF2_BEHAVIOR=1</code>.</li>
<li>AutoGraph translates Python control flow into TensorFlow expressions,
    allowing users to write regular Python inside <code>tf.function</code>-decorated
    functions. AutoGraph is also applied in functions used with <code>tf.data</code>,
    <code>tf.distribute</code> and <code>tf.keras</code> APIS.</li>
<li>Adds <code>enable_tensor_equality()</code>, which switches the behavior such that:<ul>
<li>Tensors are no longer hashable.</li>
<li>Tensors can be compared with <code>==</code> and <code>!=</code>, yielding a Boolean Tensor
    with element-wise comparison results. This will be the default behavior
    in 2.0.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Tensorflow code now produces 2 different pip packages: <code>tensorflow_core</code>
    containing all the code (in the future it will contain only the private
    implementation) and <code>tensorflow</code> which is a virtual pip package doing
    forwarding to <code>tensorflow_core</code> (and in the future will contain only the
    public API of tensorflow). We don't expect this to be breaking, unless you
    were importing directly from the implementation.</li>
<li>TensorFlow 1.15 is built using devtoolset7 (GCC7) on Ubuntu 16. This may
    lead to ABI incompatibilities with extensions built against earlier versions
    of TensorFlow.</li>
<li>Deprecated the use of <code>constraint=</code> and <code>.constraint</code> with ResourceVariable.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li><code>OMP_NUM_THREADS</code> is no longer used by the default Keras config. To
    configure the number of threads, use <code>tf.config.threading</code> APIs.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.model.save_model</code> and <code>model.save</code> now defaults to saving a
    TensorFlow SavedModel.</li>
<li><code>keras.backend.resize_images</code> (and consequently,
    <code>keras.layers.Upsampling2D</code>) behavior has changed, a bug in the resizing
    implementation was fixed.</li>
<li>Layers now default to <code>float32</code>, and automatically cast their inputs to
    the layer's dtype. If you had a model that used <code>float64</code>, it will
    probably silently use <code>float32</code> in TensorFlow2, and a warning will be
    issued that starts with Layer "layer-name" is casting an input tensor
    from dtype float64 to the layer's dtype of float32. To fix, either set
    the default dtype to float64 with
    <code>tf.keras.backend.set_floatx('float64')</code>, or pass <code>dtype='float64'</code> to
    each of the Layer constructors. See <code>tf.keras.layers.Layer</code> for more
    information.</li>
<li>Some <code>tf.assert_*</code> methods now raise assertions at operation creation
    time (i.e. when this Python line executes) if the input tensors' values
    are known at that time, not during the session.run(). When this happens,
    a noop is returned and the input tensors are marked non-feedable. In
    other words, if they are used as keys in <code>feed_dict</code> argument to
    <code>session.run()</code>, an error will be raised. Also, because some assert ops
    don't make it into the graph, the graph structure changes. A different
    graph can result in different per-op random seeds when they are not
    given explicitly (most often).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.estimator</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras.estimator.model_to_estimator</code> now supports exporting to
    <code>tf.train.Checkpoint</code> format, which allows the saved checkpoints to be
    compatible with <code>model.load_weights</code>.</li>
<li>Fix tests in canned estimators.</li>
<li>Expose Head as public API.</li>
<li>Fixes critical bugs that help with <code>DenseFeatures</code> usability in TF2</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li>Promoting <code>unbatch</code> from experimental to core API.</li>
<li>Adding support for datasets as inputs to <code>from_tensors</code> and
    <code>from_tensor_slices</code> and batching and unbatching of nested datasets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras.estimator.model_to_estimator</code> now supports exporting to
    tf.train.Checkpoint format, which allows the saved checkpoints to be
    compatible with <code>model.load_weights</code>.</li>
<li>Saving a Keras Model using <code>tf.saved_model.save</code> now saves the list of
    variables, trainable variables, regularization losses, and the call
    function.</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>tf.keras.experimental.export_saved_model</code> and
    <code>tf.keras.experimental.function</code>. Please use
    <code>tf.keras.models.save_model(..., save_format='tf')</code> and
    <code>tf.keras.models.load_model</code> instead.</li>
<li>Add an <code>implementation=3</code> mode for <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected2D</code>
    and <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected1D</code> layers using <code>tf.SparseTensor</code>
    to store weights, allowing a dramatic speedup for large sparse models.</li>
<li>Enable the Keras compile API <code>experimental_run_tf_function</code> flag by
    default. This flag enables single training/eval/predict execution path.
    With this 1. All input types are converted to <code>Dataset</code>. 2. When
    distribution strategy is not specified this goes through the no-op
    distribution strategy path. 3. Execution is wrapped in tf.function
    unless <code>run_eagerly=True</code> is set in compile.</li>
<li>Raise error if <code>batch_size</code> argument is used when input is
    dataset/generator/keras sequence.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.lite</code><ul>
<li>Add <code>GATHER</code> support to NN API delegate.</li>
<li>tflite object detection script has a debug mode.</li>
<li>Add delegate support for <code>QUANTIZE</code>.</li>
<li>Added evaluation script for COCO minival.</li>
<li>Add delegate support for <code>QUANTIZED_16BIT_LSTM</code>.</li>
<li>Converts hardswish subgraphs into atomic ops.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add support for defaulting the value of <code>cycle_length</code> argument of
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.interleave</code> to the number of schedulable CPU cores.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: Add converter for <code>MatrixDiag</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>narrow_range</code> attribute to <code>QuantizeAndDequantizeV2</code> and V3.</li>
<li>Added new op: <code>tf.strings.unsorted_segment_join</code>.</li>
<li>Add HW acceleration support for <code>topK_v2</code>.</li>
<li>Add new <code>TypeSpec</code> classes.</li>
<li>CloudBigtable version updated to v0.10.0.</li>
<li>Expose <code>Head</code> as public API.</li>
<li>Update docstring for gather to properly describe the non-empty <code>batch_dims</code>
    case.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.sparse.from_dense</code> utility function.</li>
<li>Improved ragged tensor support in <code>TensorFlowTestCase</code>.</li>
<li>Makes the a-normal form transformation in Pyct configurable as to which
    nodes are converted to variables and which are not.</li>
<li><code>ResizeInputTensor</code> now works for all delegates.</li>
<li>Add <code>EXPAND_DIMS</code> support to NN API delegate TEST: expand_dims_test</li>
<li><code>tf.cond</code> emits a StatelessIf op if the branch functions are stateless and
    do not touch any resources.</li>
<li><code>tf.cond</code>, <code>tf.while</code> and <code>if</code> and <code>while</code> in AutoGraph now accept a
    nonscalar predicate if has a single element. This does not affect non-V2
    control flow.</li>
<li><code>tf.while_loop</code> emits a StatelessWhile op if the cond and body functions are
    stateless and do not touch any resources.</li>
<li>Refactors code in Quant8 LSTM support to reduce TFLite binary size.</li>
<li>Add support of local soft device placement for eager op.</li>
<li>Add HW acceleration support for <code>LogSoftMax</code>.</li>
<li>Added a function <code>nested_value_rowids</code> for ragged tensors.</li>
<li>Add guard to avoid acceleration of L2 Normalization with input rank != 4</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.cumulative_logsumexp operation</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.ragged.stack</code>.</li>
<li>Fix memory allocation problem when calling <code>AddNewInputConstantTensor</code>.</li>
<li>Delegate application failure leaves interpreter in valid state.</li>
<li>Add check for correct memory alignment to
    <code>MemoryAllocation::MemoryAllocation()</code>.</li>
<li>Extracts <code>NNAPIDelegateKernel</code> from nnapi_delegate.cc</li>
<li>Added support for <code>FusedBatchNormV3</code> in converter.</li>
<li>A ragged to dense op for directly calculating tensors.</li>
<li>Fix accidental quadratic graph construction cost in graph-mode
    <code>tf.gradients()</code>.</li>
</ul>
