<h1>Release 2.0.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<p>TensorFlow 2.0 focuses on <strong>simplicity</strong> and <strong>ease of use</strong>, featuring updates
like:</p>
<ul>
<li>Easy model building with Keras and eager execution.</li>
<li>Robust model deployment in production on any platform.</li>
<li>Powerful experimentation for research.</li>
<li>API simplification by reducing duplication and removing deprecated
    endpoints.</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on best practices with 2.0, see
<a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta/guide/effective_tf2">the Effective 2.0 guide</a></p>
<p>For information on upgrading your existing TensorFlow 1.x models, please refer
to our
<a href="https://medium.com/tensorflow/upgrading-your-code-to-tensorflow-2-0-f72c3a4d83b5">Upgrade</a>
and <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta/guide/migration_guide">Migration</a> guides.
We have also released a collection of
<a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta">tutorials and getting started guides</a>.</p>
<h2>Highlights</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF 2.0 delivers Keras as the central high level API used to build and train
    models. Keras provides several model-building APIs such as Sequential,
    Functional, and Subclassing along with eager execution, for immediate
    iteration and intuitive debugging, and <code>tf.data</code>, for building scalable
    input pipelines. Checkout
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta/guide/keras/overview">guide</a> for additional
    details.</li>
<li>Distribution Strategy: TF 2.0 users will be able to use the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta/guide/distribute_strategy"><code>tf.distribute.Strategy</code></a>
    API to distribute training with minimal code changes, yielding great
    out-of-the-box performance. It supports distributed training with Keras
    model.fit, as well as with custom training loops. Multi-GPU support is
    available, along with experimental support for multi worker and Cloud TPUs.
    Check out the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/beta/guide/distribute_strategy">guide</a> for more
    details.</li>
<li>Functions, not Sessions. The traditional declarative programming model of
    building a graph and executing it via a <code>tf.Session</code> is discouraged, and
    replaced with by writing regular Python functions. Using the <code>tf.function</code>
    decorator, such functions can be turned into graphs which can be executed
    remotely, serialized, and optimized for performance.</li>
<li>Unification of <code>tf.train.Optimizers</code> and <code>tf.keras.Optimizers</code>. Use
    <code>tf.keras.Optimizers</code> for TF2.0. <code>compute_gradients</code> is removed as public
    API, use <code>GradientTape</code> to compute gradients.</li>
<li>AutoGraph translates Python control flow into TensorFlow expressions,
    allowing users to write regular Python inside <code>tf.function</code>-decorated
    functions. AutoGraph is also applied in functions used with tf.data,
    tf.distribute and tf.keras APIs.</li>
<li>Unification of exchange formats to SavedModel. All TensorFlow ecosystem
    projects (TensorFlow Lite, TensorFlow JS, TensorFlow Serving, TensorFlow
    Hub) accept SavedModels. Model state should be saved to and restored from
    SavedModels.</li>
<li>API Changes: Many API symbols have been renamed or removed, and argument
    names have changed. Many of these changes are motivated by consistency and
    clarity. The 1.x API remains available in the compat.v1 module. A list of
    all symbol changes can be found
    <a href="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1FLFJLzg7WNP6JHODX5q8BDgptKafq_slHpnHVbJIteQ/edit#gid=0">here</a>.<ul>
<li>API clean-up, included removing <code>tf.app</code>, <code>tf.flags</code>, and <code>tf.logging</code>
    in favor of <a href="https://github.com/abseil/abseil-py">absl-py</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>No more global variables with helper methods like
    <code>tf.global_variables_initializer</code> and <code>tf.get_global_step</code>.</li>
<li>Add toggles <code>tf.enable_control_flow_v2()</code> and <code>tf.disable_control_flow_v2()</code>
    for enabling/disabling v2 control flow.</li>
<li>Enable v2 control flow as part of <code>tf.enable_v2_behavior()</code> and
    <code>TF2_BEHAVIOR=1</code>.</li>
<li>Fixes autocomplete for most TensorFlow API references by switching to use
    relative imports in API <code>__init__.py</code> files.</li>
<li>Auto Mixed-Precision graph optimizer simplifies converting models to
    <code>float16</code> for acceleration on Volta and Turing Tensor Cores. This feature
    can be enabled by wrapping an optimizer class with
    <code>tf.train.experimental.enable_mixed_precision_graph_rewrite()</code>.</li>
<li>Add environment variable <code>TF_CUDNN_DETERMINISTIC</code>. Setting to "true" or "1"
    forces the selection of deterministic cuDNN convolution and max-pooling
    algorithms. When this is enabled, the algorithm selection procedure itself
    is also deterministic.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Many backwards incompatible API changes have been made to clean up the APIs
    and make them more consistent.</li>
<li>
<p>Toolchains:</p>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow 2.0.0 is built using devtoolset7 (GCC7) on Ubuntu 16. This
    may lead to ABI incompatibilities with extensions built against earlier
    versions of TensorFlow.</li>
<li>Tensorflow code now produces 2 different pip packages: tensorflow_core
    containing all the code (in the future it will contain only the private
    implementation) and tensorflow which is a virtual pip package doing
    forwarding to tensorflow_core (and in the future will contain only the
    public API of tensorflow). We don't expect this to be breaking, unless
    you were importing directly from the implementation. Removed the
    <code>freeze_graph</code> command line tool; <code>SavedModel</code> should be used in place
    of frozen graphs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.contrib</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code> has been deprecated, and functionality has been either
    migrated to the core TensorFlow API, to an ecosystem project such as
    <a href="https://www.github.com/tensorflow/addons">tensorflow/addons</a> or
    <a href="https://www.github.com/tensorflow/io">tensorflow/io</a>, or removed
    entirely.</li>
<li>Remove <code>tf.contrib.timeseries</code> dependency on TF distributions.</li>
<li>Replace contrib references with <code>tf.estimator.experimental.*</code> for apis
    in <code>early_stopping.py</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.estimator</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Premade estimators in the tf.estimator.DNN/Linear/DNNLinearCombined
    family have been updated to use <code>tf.keras.optimizers</code> instead of the
    <code>tf.compat.v1.train.Optimizer</code>s. If you do not pass in an <code>optimizer=</code>
    arg or if you use a string, the premade estimator will use the Keras
    optimizer. This is checkpoint breaking, as the optimizers have separate
    variables. A checkpoint converter tool for converting optimizers is
    included with the release, but if you want to avoid any change, switch
    to the v1 version of the estimator:
    <code>tf.compat.v1.estimator.DNN/Linear/DNNLinearCombined*</code>.</li>
<li>Default aggregation for canned Estimators is now <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code>.
    To maintain previous default behavior, please pass <code>SUM</code> as the loss
    aggregation method.</li>
<li>Canned Estimators don’t support <code>input_layer_partitioner</code> arg in the
    API. If you have this arg, you will have to switch to <code>tf.compat.v1
    canned Estimators</code>.</li>
<li><code>Estimator.export_savedmodel</code> has been renamed to <code>export_saved_model</code>.</li>
<li>When saving to SavedModel, Estimators will strip default op attributes.
    This is almost always the correct behavior, as it is more forwards
    compatible, but if you require that default attributes to be saved with
    the model, please use <code>tf.compat.v1.Estimator</code>.</li>
<li>Feature Columns have been upgraded to be more Eager-friendly and to work
    with Keras. As a result, <code>tf.feature_column.input_layer</code> has been
    deprecated in favor of <code>tf.keras.layers.DenseFeatures</code>. v1 feature
    columns have direct analogues in v2 except for
    <code>shared_embedding_columns</code>, which are not cross-compatible with v1 and
    v2. Use <code>tf.feature_column.shared_embeddings</code> instead.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>OMP_NUM_THREADS</code> is no longer used by the default Keras config. To
    configure the number of threads, use <code>tf.config.threading</code> APIs.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.model.save_model</code> and <code>model.save</code> now defaults to saving a
    TensorFlow SavedModel. HDF5 files are still supported.</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>tf.keras.experimental.export_saved_model</code> and
    <code>tf.keras.experimental.function</code>. Please use
    <code>tf.keras.models.save_model(..., save_format='tf')</code> and
    <code>tf.keras.models.load_model</code> instead.</li>
<li>Layers now default to float32, and automatically cast their inputs to
    the layer's dtype. If you had a model that used float64, it will
    probably silently use float32 in TensorFlow 2, and a warning will be
    issued that starts with <code>Layer &lt;layer-name&gt;</code> is casting an input tensor
    from dtype float64 to the layer's dtype of float32. To fix, either set
    the default dtype to float64 with
    <code>tf.keras.backend.set_floatx('float64')</code>, or pass <code>dtype='float64'</code> to
    each of the Layer constructors. See <code>tf.keras.layers.Layer</code> for more
    information.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Removed <code>lite.OpHint</code>, <code>lite.experimental</code>, and <code>lite.constant</code> from 2.0
    API.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Tensors are no longer hashable, but instead compare element-wise with <code>==</code>
    and <code>!=</code>. Use <code>tf.compat.v1.disable_tensor_equality()</code> to return to the
    previous behavior.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Performing equality operations on Tensors or Variables with incompatible
    shapes an exception is no longer thrown. Instead <code>__eq__</code> returns False and
    <code>__ne__</code> returns True.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Removed <code>tf.string_split</code> from v2 API.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Deprecated the use of <code>constraint=</code> and <code>.constraint</code> with ResourceVariable.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Add <code>UnifiedGRU</code> as the new GRU implementation for tf2.0. Change the default
    recurrent activation function for GRU from <code>hard_sigmoid</code> to <code>sigmoid</code>, and
    <code>reset_after</code> to True in 2.0. Historically recurrent activation is
    <code>hard_sigmoid</code> since it is fast than 'sigmoid'. With new unified backend
    between CPU and GPU mode, since the CuDNN kernel is using sigmoid, we change
    the default for CPU mode to sigmoid as well. With that, the default GRU will
    be compatible with both CPU and GPU kernel. This will enable user with GPU
    to use CuDNN kernel by default and get a 10x performance boost in training.
    Note that this is checkpoint breaking change. If user want to use their 1.x
    pre-trained checkpoint, please construct the layer with
    GRU(recurrent_activation='hard_sigmoid', reset_after=False) to fallback to
    1.x behavior.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>CUDNN_INSTALL_PATH</code>, <code>TENSORRT_INSTALL_PATH</code>, <code>NCCL_INSTALL_PATH</code>,
    <code>NCCL_HDR_PATH</code> are deprecated. Use <code>TF_CUDA_PATHS</code> instead which supports a
    comma-separated list of base paths that are searched to find CUDA libraries
    and headers.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Refer to our
<a href="https://github.com/orgs/tensorflow/projects/4">public project status tracker</a>
and
<a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/issues?q=is%3Aopen+is%3Aissue+label%3A2.0">issues tagged with <code>2.0</code></a>
on GitHub for insight into recent issues and development progress.</p>
<p>If you experience any snags when using TF 2.0, please let us know at the
<a href="https://groups.google.com/a/tensorflow.org/forum/?utm_medium=email&amp;utm_source=footer#!forum/testing">TF 2.0 Testing User Group</a>.
We have a support mailing list as well as weekly testing meetings, and would
love to hear your migration feedback and questions.</p>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.contrib</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Expose <code>tf.contrib.proto.*</code> ops in <code>tf.io</code> (they will exist in TF2)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.data</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Add support for TensorArrays to <code>tf.data Dataset</code>.</li>
<li>Integrate Ragged Tensors with <code>tf.data</code>.</li>
<li>All core and experimental tf.data transformations that input
    user-defined functions can span multiple devices now.</li>
<li>Extending the TF 2.0 support for <code>shuffle(...,
    reshuffle_each_iteration=True)</code> and <code>cache()</code> to work across different
    Python iterators for the same dataset.</li>
<li>Removing the <code>experimental_numa_aware</code> option from <code>tf.data.Options</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>num_parallel_reads</code> and passing in a Dataset containing filenames
    into <code>TextLineDataset</code> and <code>FixedLengthRecordDataset</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for defaulting the value of <code>cycle_length</code> argument of
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.interleave</code> to the number of schedulable CPU cores.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.enumerate_dataset</code> to core as
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.enumerate</code>.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>tf.data.experimental.unbatch</code> to core as
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.unbatch</code>.</li>
<li>Adds option for introducing slack in the pipeline to reduce CPU
    contention, via <code>tf.data.Options().experimental_slack = True</code></li>
<li>Added experimental support for parallel batching to <code>batch()</code> and
    <code>padded_batch()</code>. This functionality can be enabled through
    <code>tf.data.Options()</code>.</li>
<li>Support cancellation of long-running <code>reduce</code>.</li>
<li>Now we use <code>dataset</code> node name as prefix instead of the op name, to
    identify the component correctly in metrics, for pipelines with repeated
    components.</li>
<li>Improve the performance of datasets using <code>from_tensors()</code>.</li>
<li>Promoting <code>unbatch</code> from experimental to core API.</li>
<li>Adding support for datasets as inputs to <code>from_tensors</code> and
    <code>from_tensor_slices</code> and batching and unbatching of nested datasets.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.distribute</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Enable <code>tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code> working
    in eager mode.</li>
<li>Callbacks are supported in <code>MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code>.</li>
<li>Disable <code>run_eagerly</code> and distribution strategy if there are symbolic
    tensors added to the model using <code>add_metric</code> or <code>add_loss</code>.</li>
<li>Loss and gradients should now more reliably be correctly scaled w.r.t.
    the global batch size when using a <code>tf.distribute.Strategy</code>.</li>
<li>Set default loss reduction as <code>AUTO</code> for improving reliability of loss
    scaling with distribution strategy and custom training loops. <code>AUTO</code>
    indicates that the reduction option will be determined by the usage
    context. For almost all cases this defaults to <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code>.
    When used in distribution strategy scope, outside of built-in training
    loops such as <code>tf.keras</code> <code>compile</code> and <code>fit</code>, we expect reduction value
    to be 'None' or 'SUM'. Using other values will raise an error.</li>
<li>Support for multi-host <code>ncclAllReduce</code> in Distribution Strategy.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.estimator</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Replace <code>tf.contrib.estimator.add_metrics</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.add_metrics</code></li>
<li>Use <code>tf.compat.v1.estimator.inputs</code> instead of <code>tf.estimator.inputs</code></li>
<li>Replace contrib references with <code>tf.estimator.experimental.*</code> for apis
    in early_s in Estimator</li>
<li>Canned Estimators will now use keras optimizers by default. An error
    will be raised if tf.train.Optimizers are used, and you will have to
    switch to tf.keras.optimizers or tf.compat.v1 canned Estimators.</li>
<li>A checkpoint converter for canned Estimators has been provided to
    transition canned Estimators that are warm started from
    <code>tf.train.Optimizers</code> to <code>tf.keras.optimizers</code>.</li>
<li>Losses are scaled in canned estimator v2 and not in the optimizers
    anymore. If you are using Estimator + distribution strategy + optimikzer
    v1 then the behavior does not change. This implies that if you are using
    custom estimator with optimizer v2, you have to scale losses. We have
    new utilities to help scale losses <code>tf.nn.compute_average_loss</code>,
    <code>tf.nn.scale_regularization_loss</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.keras</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Premade models (including Linear and WideDeep) have been introduced for
    the purpose of replacing Premade estimators.</li>
<li>Model saving changes</li>
<li><code>model.save</code> and <code>tf.saved_model.save</code> may now save to the TensorFlow
    SavedModel format. The model can be restored using
    <code>tf.keras.models.load_model</code>. HDF5 files are still supported, and may be
    used by specifying <code>save_format="h5"</code> when saving.</li>
<li>Raw TensorFlow functions can now be used in conjunction with the Keras
    Functional API during model creation. This obviates the need for users
    to create Lambda layers in most cases when using the Functional API.
    Like Lambda layers, TensorFlow functions that result in Variable
    creation or assign ops are not supported.</li>
<li>Add support for passing list of lists to the <code>metrics</code> argument in Keras
    <code>compile</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.keras.layers.AbstractRNNCell</code> as the preferred implementation
    for RNN cells in TF v2. User can use it to implement RNN cells with
    custom behavior.</li>
<li>Keras training and validation curves are shown on the same plot when
    using the TensorBoard callback.</li>
<li>Switched Keras <code>fit/evaluate/predict</code> execution to use only a single
    unified path by default unless eager execution has been explicitly
    disabled, regardless of input type. This unified path places an
    eager-friendly training step inside of a <code>tf.function</code>. With this</li>
<li>All input types are converted to <code>Dataset</code>.</li>
<li>The path assumes there is always a distribution strategy. when
    distribution strategy is not specified the path uses a no-op
    distribution strategy.</li>
<li>The training step is wrapped in <code>tf.function</code> unless <code>run_eagerly=True</code>
    is set in compile. The single path execution code does not yet support
    all use cases. We fallback to the existing v1 execution paths if your
    model contains the following:<ol>
<li><code>sample_weight_mode</code> in compile</li>
<li><code>weighted_metrics</code> in compile</li>
<li>v1 optimizer</li>
<li>target tensors in compile If you are experiencing any issues because
    of this change, please inform us (file an issue) about your use case
    and you can unblock yourself by setting
    <code>experimental_run_tf_function=False</code> in compile meanwhile. We have
    seen couple of use cases where the model usage pattern is not as
    expected and would not work with this change.</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>output tensors of one layer is used in the constructor of another.</li>
<li>symbolic tensors outside the scope of the model are used in custom loss
    functions. The flag can be disabled for these cases and ideally the
    usage pattern will need to be fixed.</li>
<li>Mark Keras <code>set_session</code> as <code>compat.v1</code> only.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.estimator.model_to_estimator</code> now supports exporting to
    <code>tf.train.Checkpoint format</code>, which allows the saved checkpoints to be
    compatible with <code>model.load_weights</code>.</li>
<li><code>keras.backend.resize_images</code> (and consequently,
    <code>keras.layers.Upsampling2D</code>) behavior has changed, a bug in the resizing
    implementation was fixed.</li>
<li>Add an <code>implementation=3</code> mode for <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected2D</code>
    and <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected1D</code> layers using <code>tf.SparseTensor</code>
    to store weights, allowing a dramatic speedup for large sparse models.</li>
<li>Raise error if <code>batch_size</code> argument is used when input is
    dataset/generator/keras sequence.</li>
<li>Update TF 2.0 <code>keras.backend.name_scope</code> to use TF 2.0 <code>name_scope</code>.</li>
<li>Add v2 module aliases for losses, metrics, initializers and optimizers:
    <code>tf.losses = tf.keras.losses</code> &amp; <code>tf.metrics = tf.keras.metrics</code> &amp;
    <code>tf.initializers = tf.keras.initializers</code> &amp; <code>tf.optimizers =
    tf.keras.optimizers</code>.</li>
<li>Updates binary cross entropy logic in Keras when input is probabilities.
    Instead of converting probabilities to logits, we are using the cross
    entropy formula for probabilities.</li>
<li>Added public APIs for <code>cumsum</code> and <code>cumprod</code> keras backend functions.</li>
<li>Add support for temporal sample weight mode in subclassed models.</li>
<li>Raise <code>ValueError</code> if an integer is passed to the training APIs.</li>
<li>Added fault-tolerance support for training Keras model via <code>model.fit()</code>
    with <code>MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy</code>, tutorial available.</li>
<li>Custom Callback tutorial is now available.</li>
<li>To train with <code>tf.distribute</code>, Keras API is recommended over estimator.</li>
<li><code>steps_per_epoch</code> and <code>steps</code> arguments are supported with numpy arrays.</li>
<li>New error message when unexpected keys are used in
    sample_weight/class_weight dictionaries</li>
<li>Losses are scaled in Keras compile/fit and not in the optimizers
    anymore. If you are using custom training loop, we have new utilities to
    help scale losses <code>tf.nn.compute_average_loss</code>,
    <code>tf.nn.scale_regularization_loss</code>.</li>
<li><code>Layer</code> apply and add_variable APIs are deprecated.</li>
<li>Added support for channels first data format in cross entropy losses
    with logits and support for tensors with unknown ranks.</li>
<li>Error messages will be raised if <code>add_update</code>, <code>add_metric</code>, <code>add_loss</code>,
    activity regularizers are used inside of a control flow branch.</li>
<li>New loss reduction types:</li>
<li><code>AUTO</code>: Indicates that the reduction option will be determined by the
    usage context. For almost all cases this defaults to
    <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code>. When used with <code>tf.distribute.Strategy</code>, outside
    of built-in training loops such as <code>tf.keras</code> <code>compile</code> and <code>fit</code>, we
    expect reduction value to be <code>SUM</code> or <code>NONE</code>. Using <code>AUTO</code> in that case
    will raise an error.</li>
<li><code>NONE</code>: Weighted losses with one dimension reduced (axis=-1, or axis
    specified by loss function). When this reduction type used with built-in
    Keras training loops like <code>fit</code>/<code>evaluate</code>, the unreduced vector loss is
    passed to the optimizer but the reported loss will be a scalar value.</li>
<li><code>SUM</code>: Scalar sum of weighted losses. 4. <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code>: Scalar
    <code>SUM</code> divided by number of elements in losses. This reduction type is
    not supported when used with <code>tf.distribute.Strategy</code> outside of
    built-in training loops like <code>tf.keras</code> <code>compile</code>/<code>fit</code>.</li>
<li>Wraps losses passed to the <code>compile</code> API (strings and v1 losses) which
    are not instances of v2 <code>Loss</code> class in <code>LossWrapper</code> class. =&gt; All
    losses will now use <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code> reduction as default.</li>
<li><code>model.add_loss(symbolic_tensor)</code> should work in ambient eager.</li>
<li>Update metric name to always reflect what the user has given in compile.
    Affects following cases</li>
<li>When name is given as 'accuracy'/'crossentropy'</li>
<li>When an aliased function name is used eg. 'mse'</li>
<li>Removing the <code>weighted</code> prefix from weighted metric names.</li>
<li>Allow non-Tensors through v2 losses.</li>
<li>Add v2 sparse categorical crossentropy metric.</li>
<li>Add v2 APIs for <code>AUCCurve</code> and <code>AUCSummationMethod</code> enums.</li>
<li><code>add_update</code> can now be passed a zero-arg callable in order to support
    turning off the update when setting <code>trainable=False</code> on a Layer of a
    Model compiled with <code>run_eagerly=True</code>.</li>
<li>Standardize the LayerNormalization API by replacing the args <code>norm_axis</code>
    and <code>params_axis</code> with <code>axis</code>.</li>
<li>Fixed critical bugs that help with DenseFeatures usability in TF2</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>tf.lite</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Added evaluation script for <code>COCO</code> minival</li>
<li>Add delegate support for <code>QUANTIZE</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>GATHER</code> support to NN API delegate.</li>
<li>Added support for TFLiteConverter Python API in 2.0. Contains functions
    from_saved_model, from_keras_file, and from_concrete_functions.</li>
<li>Add <code>EXPAND_DIMS</code> support to NN API delegate TEST.</li>
<li>Add <code>narrow_range</code> attribute to QuantizeAndDequantizeV2 and V3.</li>
<li>Added support for <code>tflite_convert</code> command line tool in 2.0.</li>
<li>Post-training quantization tool supports quantizing weights shared by
    multiple operations. The models made with versions of this tool will use
    INT8 types for weights and will only be executable interpreters from
    this version onwards.</li>
<li>Post-training quantization tool supports fp16 weights and GPU delegate
    acceleration for fp16.</li>
<li>Add delegate support for <code>QUANTIZED_16BIT_LSTM</code>.</li>
<li>Extracts <code>NNAPIDelegateKernel</code> from nnapi_delegate.cc</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>TensorRT</p>
<ul>
<li>Add TensorFlow 2.0-compatible <code>TrtGraphConverterV2</code> API for TensorRT
    conversion. TensorRT initialization arguments are now passed wrapped in
    a named-tuple, <code>TrtConversionParams</code>, rather than as separate arguments
    as in <code>TrtGraphConverter</code>.</li>
<li>Changed API to optimize TensorRT engines during graph optimization. This
    is now done by calling <code>converter.build()</code> where previously
    <code>is_dynamic_op=False</code> would be set.</li>
<li><code>converter.convert()</code> no longer returns a <code>tf.function</code>. Now the
    function must be accessed from the saved model.</li>
<li>The <code>converter.calibrate()</code> method has been removed. To trigger
    calibration, a <code>calibration_input_fn</code> should be provided to
    <code>converter.convert()</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Other:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fix accidental quadratic graph construction cost in graph-mode
    <code>tf.gradients()</code>.</li>
<li>ResourceVariable's gather op supports batch dimensions.</li>
<li>ResourceVariable support for <code>gather_nd</code>.</li>
<li><code>ResourceVariable</code> and <code>Variable</code> no longer accepts <code>constraint</code> in the
    constructor, nor expose it as a @property.</li>
<li>Added gradient for <code>SparseToDense</code> op.</li>
<li>Expose a flag that allows the number of threads to vary across Python
    benchmarks.</li>
<li><code>image.resize</code> in 2.0 now supports gradients for the new resize kernels.</li>
<li><code>image.resize</code> now considers proper pixel centers and has new kernels
    (incl. anti-aliasing).</li>
<li>Renamed <code>tf.image</code> functions to remove duplicate "image" where it is
    redundant.</li>
<li>Variadic reduce is supported on CPU Variadic reduce is supported on CPU</li>
<li>Remove unused <code>StringViewVariantWrapper</code>.</li>
<li>Delete unused <code>Fingerprint64Map</code> op registration</li>
<li>Add broadcasting support to <code>tf.matmul</code>.</li>
<li>Add C++ Gradient for <code>BatchMatMulV2</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.cumulative_logsumexp</code> operation.</li>
<li>Add ellipsis (...) support for <code>tf.einsum()</code>.</li>
<li>Add expand_composites argument to all <code>nest.*</code> methods.</li>
<li>Added <code>strings.byte_split</code>.</li>
<li>Add a new "result_type" parameter to <code>tf.strings.split</code>.</li>
<li>Add name argument to <code>tf.string_split</code> and <code>tf.strings_split</code>.</li>
<li>Extend <code>tf.strings.split</code> to support inputs with any rank.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.random.binomial</code>.</li>
<li>Added <code>key</code> and <code>skip</code> methods to <code>random.experimental.Generator</code>.</li>
<li>Extend <code>tf.function</code> with basic support for CompositeTensors arguments
    (such as <code>SparseTensor</code> and <code>RaggedTensor</code>).</li>
<li><code>parallel_for.pfor</code>: add converters for Softmax, LogSoftmax, IsNaN, All,
    Any, and MatrixSetDiag.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: add converters for LowerTriangularSolve and Cholesky.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: add converters for <code>LogMatrixDeterminant</code> and
    <code>MatrixBandPart</code>.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: Add converter for <code>MatrixDiag</code>.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: Add converters for <code>OneHot</code>, <code>LowerBound</code>, <code>UpperBound</code>.</li>
<li><code>parallel_for</code>: add converter for <code>BroadcastTo</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>pfor</code> converter for <code>Squeeze</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>RaggedTensor.placeholder()</code>.</li>
<li>Add ragged tensor support to <code>tf.squeeze</code>.</li>
<li>Update RaggedTensors to support int32 row_splits.</li>
<li>Allow <code>LinearOperator.solve</code> to take a <code>LinearOperator</code>.</li>
<li>Allow all dtypes for <code>LinearOperatorCirculant</code>.</li>
<li>Introduce MaxParallelism method</li>
<li>Add <code>LinearOperatorHouseholder</code>.</li>
<li>Adds Philox support to new stateful RNG's XLA path.</li>
<li>Added <code>TensorSpec</code> support for CompositeTensors.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve</code> op.</li>
<li>Added partial_pivoting input parameter to <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve</code>.</li>
<li>Added gradient to <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve</code>.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_mul op</code>.</li>
<li>Added GPU implementation of <code>tf.linalg.tridiagonal_matmul</code>.</li>
<li>Added <code>LinearOperatorToeplitz</code>.</li>
<li>Upgraded LIBXSMM to version 1.11.</li>
<li>Uniform processing of quantized embeddings by Gather and EmbeddingLookup
    Ops.</li>
<li>Correct a misstatement in the documentation of the sparse softmax cross
    entropy logit parameter.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.ragged.boolean_mask</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.switch_case</code> added, which selects a branch_fn based on a
    branch_index.</li>
<li>The C++ kernel of gather op supports batch dimensions.</li>
<li>Fixed default value and documentation for <code>trainable</code> arg of
    tf.Variable.</li>
<li><code>EagerTensor</code> now supports numpy buffer interface for tensors.</li>
<li>This change bumps the version number of the <code>FullyConnected</code> Op to 5.</li>
<li>Added new op: <code>tf.strings.unsorted_segment_join</code>.</li>
<li>Added HW acceleration support for <code>topK_v2</code>.</li>
<li>CloudBigtable version updated to v0.10.0 BEGIN_PUBLIC CloudBigtable
    version updated to v0.10.0.</li>
<li>Expose <code>Head</code> as public API.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.sparse.from_dense</code> utility function.</li>
<li>Improved ragged tensor support in <code>TensorFlowTestCase</code>.</li>
<li>Added a function <code>nested_value_rowids</code> for ragged tensors.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.ragged.stack</code>.</li>
<li>Makes the a-normal form transformation in Pyct configurable as to which
    nodes are converted to variables and which are not.</li>
<li><code>ResizeInputTensor</code> now works for all delegates.</li>
<li><code>tf.cond</code> emits a StatelessIf op if the branch functions are stateless
    and do not touch any resources.</li>
<li>Add support of local soft device placement for eager op.</li>
<li>Pass partial_pivoting to the <code>_TridiagonalSolveGrad</code>.</li>
<li>Add HW acceleration support for <code>LogSoftMax</code>.</li>
<li>Add guard to avoid acceleration of L2 Normalization with input rank != 4</li>
<li>Fix memory allocation problem when calling <code>AddNewInputConstantTensor</code>.</li>
<li>Delegate application failure leaves interpreter in valid state</li>
<li><code>tf.while_loop</code> emits a StatelessWhile op if the cond and body functions
    are stateless and do not touch any resources.</li>
<li><code>tf.cond</code>, <code>tf.while</code> and if and while in AutoGraph now accept a
    nonscalar predicate if has a single element. This does not affect non-V2
    control flow.</li>
<li>Fix potential security vulnerability where decoding variant tensors from
    proto could result in heap out of bounds memory access.</li>
<li>Only create a GCS directory object if the object does not already exist.</li>
<li>Introduce <code>dynamic</code> constructor argument in Layer and Model, which
    should be set to <code>True</code> when using imperative control flow in the <code>call</code>
    method.</li>
<li>Begin adding Go wrapper for C Eager API.</li>
<li>XLA HLO graphs can be inspected with interactive_graphviz tool now.</li>
<li>Add dataset ops to the graph (or create kernels in Eager execution)
    during the python Dataset object creation instead doing it during
    Iterator creation time.</li>
<li>Add <code>batch_dims</code> argument to <code>tf.gather</code>.</li>
<li>The behavior of <code>tf.gather</code> is now correct when <code>axis=None</code> and
    <code>batch_dims&lt;0</code>.</li>
<li>Update docstring for gather to properly describe the non-empty
    <code>batch_dims</code> case.</li>
<li>Removing of dtype in the constructor of initializers and partition_info
    in call.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.math.nextafter</code> op.</li>
<li>Turn on MKL-DNN contraction kernels by default. MKL-DNN dynamically
    dispatches the best kernel implementation based on CPU vector
    architecture. To disable them, build with
    <code>--define=tensorflow_mkldnn_contraction_kernel=0</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.linspace(start, stop, num)</code> now always uses "stop" as last value
    (for num &gt; 1)</li>
<li>Added top-k to precision and recall to keras metrics.</li>
<li>Add a ragged size op and register it to the op dispatcher</li>
<li>Transitive dependencies on :<code>pooling_ops</code> were removed. Some users may
    need to add explicit dependencies on :<code>pooling_ops</code> if they reference
    the operators from that library.</li>
<li>Add <code>CompositeTensor</code> base class.</li>
<li>Malformed gif images could result in an access out of bounds in the
    color palette of the frame. This has been fixed now</li>
<li>Add templates and interfaces for creating lookup tables</li>
<li><code>Tensor::UnsafeCopyFromInternal</code> deprecated in favor
    <code>Tensor::BitcastFrom</code>.</li>
<li>In <code>map_vectorization</code> optimization, reduce the degree of parallelism in
    the vectorized map node.</li>
<li>Add variant wrapper for <code>absl::string_view</code>.</li>
<li>Add OpKernels for some stateless maps.</li>
<li>DType is no longer convertible to an int. Use <code>dtype.as_datatype_enum</code>
    instead of <code>int(dtype)</code> to get the same result.</li>
<li>Support both binary and -1/1 label input in v2 hinge and squared hinge
    losses.</li>
<li>Added <code>LinearOperator.adjoint</code> and <code>LinearOperator.H</code> (alias).</li>
<li>Expose CriticalSection in core as <code>tf.CriticalSection</code>.</li>
<li>Enhanced graphviz output.</li>
<li>Add opkernel templates for common table operations.</li>
<li>Fix callbacks do not log values in eager mode when a deferred build
    model is used.</li>
<li><code>SignatureDef</code> util functions have been deprecated.</li>
<li>Update <code>Fingerprint64Map</code> to use aliases</li>
<li>Add legacy string flat hash map op kernels.</li>
<li>Add support for <code>add_metric</code> in the graph function mode.</li>
<li>Updating cosine similarity loss - removed the negate sign from cosine
    similarity.</li>
<li>Changed default for gradient accumulation for TPU embeddings to true.</li>
<li>Adds summary trace API for collecting graph and profile information.</li>
<li>The <code>precision_mode</code> argument to <code>TrtGraphConverter</code> is now case
    insensitive.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.14.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>The 1.14.1 whl package is built with ROCm2.7 user-bit environment</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.14.0</h1>
<h2>ROCm specific features</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF-ROCm integrates the ROCm RCCL library as the collective communication
    routines for mGPU computation</li>
<li>TF-ROCm enables the XLA backend starting 1.14.0 release, currently, it's
    functionality-complete, performance optimization in progress.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known issues</h2>
<ul>
<li>We recommend to disable MIOpen 2.0 ASM kernels for GFX803 GPUs using the
    environment variable: <code>export MIOPEN_DEBUG_GCN_ASM_KERNELS=0</code></li>
</ul>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>This is the first 1.x release containing the compat.v2 module. This module
    is required to allow libraries to publish code which works in both 1.x and
    2.x. After this release, no backwards incompatible changes are allowed in
    the 2.0 Python API.</li>
<li>Turn on MKL-DNN contraction kernels by default. MKL-DNN dynamically
    dispatches the best kernel implementation based on CPU vector architecture.
    To disable them, build with --define=tensorflow_mkldnn_contraction_kernel=0.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Behavioral changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Set default loss reduction as <code>AUTO</code> for improving reliability of loss
    scaling with distribution strategy and custom training loops. <code>AUTO</code>
    indicates that the reduction option will be determined by the usage context.
    For almost all cases this defaults to <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code>. When used in
    distribution strategy scope, outside of built-in training loops such as
    <code>tf.keras</code> <code>compile</code> and <code>fit</code>, we expect reduction value to be 'None' or
    'SUM'. Using other values will raise an error.</li>
<li>Wraps losses passed to the <code>compile</code> API (strings and v1 losses) which are
    not instances of v2 <code>Loss</code> class in <code>LossWrapper</code> class. =&gt; All losses will
    now use <code>SUM_OVER_BATCH_SIZE</code> reduction as default.</li>
<li>Disable <code>run_eagerly</code> and distribution strategy if there are symbolic
    tensors added to the model using <code>add_metric</code> or <code>add_loss</code>.</li>
<li>tf.linspace(start, stop, num) now always uses "stop" as last value (for
    num &gt; 1)</li>
<li><code>ResourceVariable</code> and <code>Variable</code> no longer accepts <code>constraint</code> in the
    constructor, nor expose it as a @property.</li>
<li>The behavior of tf.gather is now correct when axis=None and batch_dims&lt;0.</li>
<li>Only create a GCS directory object if the object does not already exist.</li>
<li>In <code>map_vectorization</code> optimization, reduce the degree of parallelism in the
    vectorized map node.</li>
<li>Bug fix: loss and gradients should now more reliably be correctly scaled
    w.r.t. the global batch size when using a tf.distribute.Strategy.</li>
<li>Updating cosine similarity loss - removed the negate sign from cosine
    similarity.</li>
<li>DType is no longer convertible to an int. Use dtype.as_datatype_enum instead
    of int(dtype) to get the same result.</li>
<li>Changed default for gradient accumulation for TPU embeddings to true.</li>
<li>Callbacks now log values in eager mode when a deferred build model is used.</li>
<li>Transitive dependencies on :pooling_ops were removed. Some users may need to
    add explicit dependencies on :pooling_ops if they reference the operators
    from that library.</li>
<li>tf.keras.optimizers default learning rate changes:<ul>
<li>Adadelta: 1.000 to 0.001</li>
<li>Adagrad: 0.01 to 0.001</li>
<li>Adamax: 0.002 to 0.001</li>
<li>NAdam: 0.002 to 0.001</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Documentation</li>
<li>Deprecations and Symbol renames.<ul>
<li>Remove unused StringViewVariantWrapper</li>
<li>Delete unused Fingerprint64Map op registration</li>
<li>SignatureDef util functions have been deprecated.</li>
<li>Renamed tf.image functions to remove duplicate "image" where it is
    redundant.</li>
<li>tf.keras.experimental.export renamed to
    tf.keras.experimental.export_saved_model</li>
<li>Standardize the LayerNormalization API by replacing the args <code>norm_axis</code>
    and <code>params_axis</code> with <code>axis</code>.</li>
<li>Tensor::UnsafeCopyFromInternal deprecated in favor Tensor::BitcastFrom</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Keras &amp; Python API<ul>
<li>Add v2 module aliases for:</li>
<li>tf.initializers =&gt; tf.keras.initializers</li>
<li>tf.losses =&gt; tf.keras.losses &amp; tf.metrics =&gt; tf.keras.metrics</li>
<li>tf.optimizers =&gt; tf.keras.optimizers</li>
<li>Add tf.keras.layers.AbstractRNNCell as the preferred implementation of
    RNN cell for TF v2. User can use it to implement RNN cell with custom
    behavior.</li>
<li>Adding <code>clear_losses</code> API to be able to clear losses at the end of
    forward pass in a custom training loop in eager.</li>
<li>Add support for passing list of lists to the <code>metrics</code> param in Keras
    <code>compile</code>.</li>
<li>Added top-k to precision and recall to keras metrics.</li>
<li>Adding public APIs for <code>cumsum</code> and <code>cumprod</code> keras backend functions.</li>
<li>Fix: model.add_loss(symbolic_tensor) should work in ambient eager.</li>
<li>Add name argument to tf.string_split and tf.strings_split</li>
<li>Minor change to SavedModels exported from Keras using
    tf.keras.experimental.export. (SignatureDef key for evaluation mode is
    now "eval" instead of "test"). This will be reverted back to "test" in
    the near future.</li>
<li>Updates binary cross entropy logic in Keras when input is probabilities.
    Instead of converting probabilities to logits, we are using the cross
    entropy formula for probabilities.</li>
<li>Raw TensorFlow functions can now be used in conjunction with the Keras
    Functional API during model creation. This obviates the need for users
    to create Lambda layers in most cases when using the Functional API.
    Like Lambda layers, TensorFlow functions that result in Variable
    creation or assign ops are not supported.</li>
<li>Keras training and validation curves are shown on the same plot.</li>
<li>Introduce <code>dynamic</code> constructor argument in Layer and Model, which
    should be set to True when using imperative control flow in the <code>call</code>
    method.</li>
<li>Removing of dtype in the constructor of initializers and partition_info
    in call.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>New ops and improved op functionality<ul>
<li>Add OpKernels for some stateless maps</li>
<li>Add v2 APIs for AUCCurve and AUCSummationMethod
    enums. #tf-metrics-convergence</li>
<li>Add tf.math.nextafter op.</li>
<li>Add CompositeTensor base class.</li>
<li>Add tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve op.</li>
<li>Add opkernel templates for common table operations.</li>
<li>Added support for TFLite in TensorFlow 2.0.</li>
<li>Adds summary trace API for collecting graph and profile information.</li>
<li>Add batch_dims argument to tf.gather.</li>
<li>Add support for <code>add_metric</code> in the graph function mode.</li>
<li>Add C++ Gradient for BatchMatMulV2.</li>
<li>Added tf.random.binomial</li>
<li>Added gradient for SparseToDense op.</li>
<li>Add legacy string flat hash map op kernels</li>
<li>Add a ragged size op and register it to the op dispatcher</li>
<li>Add broadcasting support to tf.matmul.</li>
<li>Add ellipsis (...) support for tf.einsum()</li>
<li>Added LinearOperator.adjoint and LinearOperator.H (alias).</li>
<li>Added GPU implementation of tf.linalg.tridiagonal_solve.</li>
<li>Added strings.byte_split</li>
<li>Add RaggedTensor.placeholder()</li>
<li>Add a new "result_type" parameter to tf.strings.split</li>
<li><code>add_update</code> can now be passed a zero-arg callable in order to support
    turning off the update when setting <code>trainable=False</code> on a Layer of a
    Model compiled with <code>run_eagerly=True</code>.</li>
<li>Add variant wrapper for absl::string_view</li>
<li>Add expand_composites argument to all nest.* methods.</li>
<li>Add pfor converter for Squeeze.</li>
<li>Bug fix for tf.tile gradient</li>
<li>Expose CriticalSection in core as tf.CriticalSection.</li>
<li>Update Fingerprint64Map to use aliases</li>
<li>ResourceVariable support for gather_nd.</li>
<li>ResourceVariable's gather op supports batch dimensions.</li>
<li>Variadic reduce is supported on CPU</li>
<li>Extend tf.function with basic support for CompositeTensors arguments
    (such as SparseTensor and RaggedTensor).</li>
<li>Add templates and interfaces for creating lookup tables</li>
<li>Post-training quantization tool supports quantizing weights shared by
    multiple operations. The models made with versions of this tool will use
    INT8 types for weights and will only be executable interpreters from
    this version onwards.</li>
<li>Malformed gif images could result in an access out of bounds in the
    color palette of the frame. This has been fixed now</li>
<li>image.resize now considers proper pixel centers and has new kernels
    (incl. anti-aliasing).</li>
<li>Added an isotonic regression solver (tf.nn.isotonic_regression).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Performance<ul>
<li>Turn on MKL-DNN contraction kernels by default. MKL-DNN dynamically
    dispatches the best kernel implementation based on CPU vector
    architecture. To disable them, build with
    --define=tensorflow_mkldnn_contraction_kernel=0.</li>
<li>Support for multi-host ncclAllReduce in Distribution Strategy.</li>
<li>Expose a flag that allows the number of threads to vary across Python
    benchmarks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow 2.0 Development<ul>
<li>Add v2 sparse categorical crossentropy metric.</li>
<li>Allow non-Tensors through v2 losses.</li>
<li>Add UnifiedGRU as the new GRU implementation for tf2.0. Change the
    default recurrent activation function for GRU from 'hard_sigmoid' to
    'sigmoid', and 'reset_after' to True in 2.0. Historically recurrent
    activation is 'hard_sigmoid' since it is fast than 'sigmoid'. With new
    unified backend between CPU and GPU mode, since the CuDNN kernel is
    using sigmoid, we change the default for CPU mode to sigmoid as well.
    With that, the default GRU will be compatible with both CPU and GPU
    kernel. This will enable user with GPU to use CuDNN kernel by default
    and get a 10x performance boost in training. Note that this is
    checkpoint breaking change. If user want to use their 1.x pre-trained
    checkpoint, please construct the layer with
    GRU(recurrent_activation='hard_sigmoid', reset_after=False) to fallback
    to 1.x behavior.</li>
<li>TF 2.0 - Update metric name to always reflect what the user has given in
    compile. Affects following cases 1. When name is given as
    'accuracy'/'crossentropy' 2. When an aliased function name is used eg.
    'mse' 3. Removing the <code>weighted</code> prefix from weighted metric names.</li>
<li>Begin adding Go wrapper for C Eager API</li>
<li>image.resize in 2.0 now supports gradients for the new resize kernels.</li>
<li>removed tf.string_split from v2 API</li>
<li>Expose tf.contrib.proto.* ops in tf.io (they will exist in TF2)</li>
<li>"Updates the TFLiteConverter API in 2.0. Changes from_concrete_function
    to from_concrete_functions."</li>
<li>Enable tf.distribute.experimental.MultiWorkerMirroredStrategy working in
    eager mode.</li>
<li>Support both binary and -1/1 label input in v2 hinge and squared hinge
    losses.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow Lite<ul>
<li>"Adds support for tflite_convert in 2.0."</li>
<li>"Remove lite.OpHint, lite.experimental, and lite.constant from 2.0 API."</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>tf.contrib<ul>
<li>Added Neural Turing Implementation as described in
    https://arxiv.org/abs/1807.08518.</li>
<li>Remove tf.contrib.timeseries dependency on TF distributions.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>tf.data<ul>
<li>Add num_parallel_reads and passing in a Dataset containing filenames
    into TextLineDataset and FixedLengthRecordDataset</li>
<li>Going forward we operate in TF 2.0, this change is part of the effort to
    slowly converting XYZDataset to DatasetV2 type which is the official
    version going to be used in TF 2.0 and motivated by some compatibility
    issue found, _BigtableXYZDataset (of type DatasetV2) does not implement
    the _as_variant_tensor() of DatasetV1, when moving contrib.bigtable to
    tensorflow_io. Converting into DatasetV2 removes the overheads to
    maintain V1 while we are moving into TF 2.0.</li>
<li>Add dataset ops to the graph (or create kernels in Eager execution)
    during the python Dataset object creation instead doing it during
    Iterator creation time.</li>
<li>Add support for TensorArrays to tf.data Dataset.</li>
<li>Switching tf.data functions to use <code>defun</code>, providing an escape hatch to
    continue using the legacy <code>Defun</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Toolchains<ul>
<li>CUDNN_INSTALL_PATH, TENSORRT_INSTALL_PATH, NCCL_INSTALL_PATH,
    NCCL_HDR_PATH are deprecated. Use TF_CUDA_PATHS instead which supports a
    comma-separated list of base paths that are searched to find CUDA
    libraries and headers.</li>
<li>TF code now resides in <code>tensorflow_core</code> and <code>tensorflow</code> is just a
    virtual pip package. No code changes are needed for projects using
    TensorFlow, the change is transparent</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>XLA<ul>
<li>XLA HLO graphs can be inspected with interactive_graphviz tool now.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Estimator<ul>
<li>Use tf.compat.v1.estimator.inputs instead of tf.estimator.inputs</li>
<li>Replace contrib references with tf.estimator.experimental.* for apis in
    early_stopping.py</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</ul>
<h1>Release 1.12.3</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Updates <code>png_archive</code> dependency to 1.6.37 to not be affected by
    CVE-2019-7317, CVE-2018-13785, and CVE-2018-14048.</li>
<li>Updates <code>sqlite</code> dependency to 3.28.0 to not be affected by CVE-2018-20506,
    CVE-2018-20346, and CVE-2018-20505.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.12.2</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes a potential security vulnerability where carefully crafted GIF images
    can produce a null pointer dereference during decoding.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.13.2</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>TF-RCCL path fix for issue#370</li>
<li>The 1.13.2 whl package is built the ROCm2.3 user-bit environment</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.13.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow Lite has moved from contrib to core. This means that Python
    modules are under <code>tf.lite</code> and source code is now under <code>tensorflow/lite</code>
    rather than <code>tensorflow/contrib/lite</code>.</li>
<li>TensorFlow GPU binaries are now built against CUDA 10 and TensorRT 5.0.</li>
<li>Support for Python3.7 on all operating systems.</li>
<li>Moved NCCL to core.</li>
</ul>
<h2>ROCm Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>MIOpen v1.7.1 integration</li>
<li>Tensorflow VERBS support is enabled, details in: <a href="https://github.com/ROCmSoftwarePlatform/tensorflow-upstream/blob/r1.13-rocm/rocm_docs/tensorflow-verbs.md">TensorFlow Verbs Quick-Start</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Behavioral changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Disallow conversion of python floating types to uint32/64 (matching behavior
    of other integer types) in <code>tf.constant</code>.</li>
<li>Make the <code>gain</code> argument of convolutional orthogonal initializers
    (<code>convolutional_delta_orthogonal</code>, <code>convolutional_orthogonal_1D</code>,
    <code>convolutional_orthogonal_2D</code>, <code>convolutional_orthogonal_3D</code>) have
    consistent behavior with the <code>tf.initializers.orthogonal</code> initializer, i.e.
    scale the output l2-norm by <code>gain</code> and NOT by <code>sqrt(gain)</code>. (Note that these
    functions are currently in <code>tf.contrib</code> which is not guaranteed backward
    compatible).</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Documentation<ul>
<li>Update the doc with the details about the rounding mode used in
    quantize_and_dequantize_v2.</li>
<li>Clarify that tensorflow::port::InitMain() <em>should</em> be called before
    using the TensorFlow library. Programs failing to do this are not
    portable to all platforms.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Deprecations and Symbol renames.<ul>
<li>Removing deprecations for the following endpoints: <code>tf.acos</code>,
    <code>tf.acosh</code>, <code>tf.add</code>, <code>tf.as_string</code>, <code>tf.asin</code>, <code>tf.asinh</code>, <code>tf.atan</code>,
    <code>tf.atan2</code>, <code>tf.atanh</code>, <code>tf.cos</code>, <code>tf.cosh</code>, <code>tf.equal</code>, <code>tf.exp</code>,
    <code>tf.floor</code>, <code>tf.greater</code>, <code>tf.greater_equal</code>, <code>tf.less</code>,
    <code>tf.less_equal</code>, <code>tf.log</code>, <code>tf.logp1</code>, <code>tf.logical_and</code>,
    <code>tf.logical_not</code>, <code>tf.logical_or</code>, <code>tf.maximum</code>, <code>tf.minimum</code>,
    <code>tf.not_equal</code>, <code>tf.sin</code>, <code>tf.sinh</code>, <code>tf.tan</code></li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tf.data.Dataset.shard</code>.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>saved_model.loader.load</code> which is replaced by
    <code>saved_model.load</code> and <code>saved_model.main_op</code>, which will be replaced by
    <code>saved_model.main_op</code> in V2.</li>
<li>Deprecate tf.QUANTIZED_DTYPES. The official new symbol is
    tf.dtypes.QUANTIZED_DTYPES.</li>
<li>Update sklearn imports for deprecated packages.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>Variable.count_up_to</code> and <code>tf.count_up_to</code> in favor of
    <code>Dataset.range</code>.</li>
<li>Export <code>confusion_matrix</code> op as <code>tf.math.confusion_matrix</code> instead of
    <code>tf.train.confusion_matrix</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.dtypes.</code> endpoint for every constant in dtypes.py. Moving
    endpoints in versions.py to corresponding endpoints in <code>tf.sysconfig.</code>
    and <code>tf.version.</code>. Moving all constants under <code>tf.saved_model</code>
    submodules to <code>tf.saved_model</code> module. New endpoints are added in V1 and
    V2 but existing endpoint removals are only applied in V2.</li>
<li>Deprecates behavior where device assignment overrides collocation
    constraints inside a collocation context manager.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Keras &amp; Python API<ul>
<li>Add to Keras functionality analogous to
    <code>tf.register_tensor_conversion_function</code>.</li>
<li>Subclassed Keras models can now be saved through
    <code>tf.contrib.saved_model.save_keras_model</code>.</li>
<li><code>LinearOperator.matmul</code> now returns a new <code>LinearOperator</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>New ops and improved op functionality<ul>
<li>Add a Nearest Neighbor Resize op.</li>
<li>Add an <code>ignore_unknown</code> argument to <code>parse_values</code> which suppresses
    ValueError for unknown hyperparameter types. Such * Add
    <code>tf.linalg.matvec</code> convenience function.</li>
<li><code>tf.einsum()</code>raises <code>ValueError</code> for unsupported equations like
    <code>"ii-&gt;"</code>.</li>
<li>Add DCT-I and IDCT-I in <code>tf.signal.dct</code> and <code>tf.signal.idct</code>.</li>
<li>Add LU decomposition op.</li>
<li>Add quantile loss to gradient boosted trees in estimator.</li>
<li>Add <code>round_mode</code> to <code>QuantizeAndDequantizeV2</code> op to select rounding
    algorithm.</li>
<li>Add <code>unicode_encode</code>, <code>unicode_decode</code>, <code>unicode_decode_with_offsets</code>,
    <code>unicode_split</code>, <code>unicode_split_with_offset</code>, and <code>unicode_transcode</code>
    ops. Amongst other things, this Op adds the ability to encode, decode,
    and transcode a variety of input text encoding formats into the main
    Unicode encodings (UTF-8, UTF-16-BE, UTF-32-BE)</li>
<li>Add "unit" attribute to the substr op, which allows obtaining the
    substring of a string containing unicode characters.</li>
<li>Broadcasting support for Ragged Tensors.</li>
<li><code>SpaceToDepth</code> supports uint8 data type.</li>
<li>Support multi-label quantile regression in estimator.</li>
<li>We now use "div" as the default partition_strategy in
    <code>tf.nn.safe_embedding_lookup_sparse</code>, <code>tf.nn.sampled_softmax</code> and
    <code>tf.nn.nce_loss</code>. hyperparameter are ignored.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Performance<ul>
<li>Improve performance of GPU cumsum/cumprod by up to 300x.</li>
<li>Added support for weight decay in most TPU embedding optimizers,
    including AdamW and MomentumW.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow 2.0 Development<ul>
<li>Add a command line tool to convert to TF2.0, tf_upgrade_v2</li>
<li>Merge <code>tf.spectral</code> into <code>tf.signal</code> for TensorFlow 2.0.</li>
<li>Change the default recurrent activation function for LSTM from
    'hard_sigmoid' to 'sigmoid' in 2.0. Historically recurrent activation is
    'hard_sigmoid' since it is fast than 'sigmoid'. With new unified backend
    between CPU and GPU mode, since the CuDNN kernel is using sigmoid, we
    change the default for CPU mode to sigmoid as well. With that, the
    default LSTM will be compatible with both CPU and GPU kernel. This will
    enable user with GPU to use CuDNN kernel by default and get a 10x
    performance boost in training. Note that this is checkpoint breaking
    change. If user want to use their 1.x pre-trained checkpoint, please
    construct the layer with LSTM(recurrent_activation='hard_sigmoid') to
    fallback to 1.x behavior.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow Lite<ul>
<li>Move from <code>tensorflow/contrib/lite</code> to <code>tensorflow/lite</code>.</li>
<li>Add experimental Java API for injecting TensorFlow Lite delegates</li>
<li>Add support for strings in TensorFlow Lite Java API.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li>Add Apache Ignite Filesystem plugin to support accessing Apache IGFS.</li>
<li>Dropout now takes <code>rate</code> argument, <code>keep_prob</code> is deprecated.</li>
<li>Estimator occurrences references <code>tf.contrib.estimator</code> were changed to
    <code>tf.estimator</code>:</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.BaselineEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.BaselineEstimator</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.DNNLinearCombinedEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.DNNLinearCombinedEstimator</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.DNNEstimator</code> with <code>tf.estimator.DNNEstimator</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.LinearEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.LinearEstimator</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.InMemoryEvaluatorHook</code> and
    tf.estimator.experimental.InMemoryEvaluatorHook`.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.estimator.make_stop_at_checkpoint_step_hook</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.experimental.make_stop_at_checkpoint_step_hook</code>.</li>
<li>Expose `tf.distribute.Strategy as the new name for
    tf.contrib.distribute.DistributionStrategy.</li>
<li>Migrate linear optimizer from contrib to core.</li>
<li>Move <code>tf.contrib.signal</code> to <code>tf.signal</code> (preserving aliases in
    tf.contrib.signal).</li>
<li>Users of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.export_all_saved_models</code> and related
    should switch to
    <code>tf.estimator.Estimator.experimental_export_all_saved_models</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>tf.data:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.data.experimental.StatsOptions()</code>, to configure options to
    collect statistics from <code>tf.data.Dataset</code> pipeline using
    <code>StatsAggregator</code>. Add nested option, <code>experimental_stats</code> (which takes
    a <code>tf.data.experimen tal.StatsOptions</code> object), to <code>tf.data.Options</code>.
    Deprecates <code>tf.data.experimental.set_stats_agregator</code>.</li>
<li>Performance optimizations:</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions()</code>, to configure options
    to enable <code>tf.data</code> performance optimizations. Add nested option,
    <code>experimental_optimization</code> (which takes a
    <code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions</code> object), to
    <code>tf.data.Options</code>. Remove performance optimization options from
    <code>tf.data.Options</code>, and add them under
    <code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions</code> instead.</li>
<li>Enable <code>map_and_batch_fusion</code> and <code>noop_elimination</code> optimizations by
    default. They can be disabled by configuring
    <code>tf.data.experimental.OptimizationOptions</code> to set <code>map_and_batch =
    False</code> or <code>noop_elimination = False</code> respectively. To disable all
    default optimizations, set <code>apply_default_optimizations = False</code>.</li>
<li>Support parallel map in <code>map_and_filter_fusion</code>.</li>
<li>Disable static optimizations for input pipelines that use non-resource
    <code>tf.Variable</code>s.</li>
<li>Add NUMA-aware MapAndBatch dataset.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tf.data.Dataset.make_one_shot_iterator()</code> in V1, removed it
    from V2, and added tf.compat.v1.data.make_one_shot_iterator()`.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tf.data.Dataset.make_initializable_iterator()</code> in V1, removed
    it from V2, and added <code>tf.compat.v1.data.make_initializable_iterator()</code>.</li>
<li>Enable nested dataset support in core <code>tf.data</code> transformations.</li>
<li>For <code>tf.data.Dataset</code> implementers: Added
    <code>tf.data.Dataset._element_structured property</code> to replace
    <code>Dataset.output_{types,shapes,classes}</code>.</li>
<li>Make <code>num_parallel_calls</code> of <code>tf.data.Dataset.interleave</code> and
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.map</code> work in Eager mode.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Toolchains<ul>
<li>Fixed OpenSSL compatibility by avoiding <code>EVP_MD_CTX_destroy</code>.</li>
<li>Added bounds checking to printing deprecation warnings.</li>
<li>Upgraded CUDA dependency to 10.0</li>
<li>To build with Android NDK r14b, add "#include <linux/compiler.h>" to
    android-ndk-r14b/platforms/android-14/arch-*/usr/include/linux/futex.h</li>
<li>Removed <code>:android_tensorflow_lib_selective_registration*</code> targets, use
    <code>:android_tensorflow_lib_lite*</code> targets instead.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>XLA<ul>
<li>Move <code>RoundToEven</code> function to xla/client/lib/math.h.</li>
<li>A new environment variable <code>TF_XLA_DEBUG_OPTIONS_PASSTHROUGH</code> set to "1"
    or "true" allows the debug options passed within an XRTCompile op to be
    passed directly to the XLA compilation backend. If such variable is not
    set (service side), only a restricted set will be passed through.</li>
<li>Allow the XRTCompile op to return the ProgramShape resulted form the XLA
    compilation as a second return argument.</li>
<li>XLA HLO graphs can now be rendered as SVG/HTML.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Estimator<ul>
<li>Replace all occurrences of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.BaselineEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.BaselineEstimator</code></li>
<li>Replace all occurrences of
    <code>tf.contrib.estimator.DNNLinearCombinedEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.DNNLinearCombinedEstimator</code></li>
<li>Replace all occurrences of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.DNNEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.DNNEstimator</code></li>
<li>Replace all occurrences of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.LinearEstimator</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.LinearEstimator</code></li>
<li>Users of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.export_all_saved_models</code> and related
    should switch to
    <code>tf.estimator.Estimator.experimental_export_all_saved_models</code>.</li>
<li>Update <code>regression_head</code> to the new Head API for Canned Estimator V2.</li>
<li>Switch <code>multi_class_head</code> to Head API for Canned Estimator V2.</li>
<li>Replace all occurrences of <code>tf.contrib.estimator.InMemoryEvaluatorHook</code>
    and <code>tf.contrib.estimator.make_stop_at_checkpoint_step_hook</code> with
    <code>tf.estimator.experimental.InMemoryEvaluatorHook</code> and
    <code>tf.estimator.experimental.make_stop_at_checkpoint_step_hook</code></li>
<li>Migrate linear optimizer from contrib to core.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.12.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Keras models can now be directly exported to the SavedModel
    format(<code>tf.contrib.saved_model.save_keras_model()</code>) and used with Tensorflow
    Serving.</li>
<li>Keras models now support evaluating with a <code>tf.data.Dataset</code>.</li>
<li>TensorFlow binaries are built with XLA support linked in by default.</li>
<li>Ignite Dataset added to contrib/ignite that allows to work with Apache
    Ignite.</li>
</ul>
<h2>ROCm Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>MIOpenv1.6 integration</li>
<li>Training in fp16 is fully supported</li>
<li>Performance improvements in TF CNN benchmarks</li>
<li>Layer fusion is supported, details in: <a href="https://github.com/ROCmSoftwarePlatform/tensorflow-upstream/blob/r1.12-rocm/rocm_docs/rocm-port-overview.md">TensorFlow ROCm port high-level design document</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>tf.data:<ul>
<li>tf.data users can now represent, get, and set options of TensorFlow
    input pipelines using <code>tf.data.Options()</code>, <code>tf.data.Dataset.options()</code>,
    and <code>tf.data.Dataset.with_options()</code> respectively.</li>
<li>New <code>tf.data.Dataset.reduce()</code> API allows users to reduce a finite
    dataset to a single element using a user-provided reduce function.</li>
<li>New <code>tf.data.Dataset.window()</code> API allows users to create finite windows
    of input dataset; when combined with the <code>tf.data.Dataset.reduce()</code> API,
    this allows users to implement customized batching.</li>
<li>All C++ code moves to the <code>tensorflow::data</code> namespace.</li>
<li>Add support for <code>num_parallel_calls</code> to <code>tf.data.Dataset.interleave</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li>Remove <code>tf.contrib.linalg</code>. <code>tf.linalg</code> should be used instead.</li>
<li>Replace any calls to <code>tf.contrib.get_signature_def_by_key(metagraph_def,
    signature_def_key)</code> with
    <code>meta_graph_def.signature_def[signature_def_key]</code>. Catching a ValueError
    exception thrown by <code>tf.contrib.get_signature_def_by_key</code> should be
    replaced by catching a KeyError exception.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data</code><ul>
<li>Deprecate, and replace by tf.data.experimental.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Instead of jemalloc, revert back to using system malloc since it
    simplifies build and has comparable performance.</li>
<li>Remove integer types from <code>tf.nn.softplus</code> and <code>tf.nn.softsign</code> OpDefs.
    This is a bugfix; these ops were never meant to support integers.</li>
<li>Allow subslicing Tensors with a single dimension.</li>
<li>Add option to calculate string length in Unicode characters.</li>
<li>Add functionality to SubSlice a tensor.</li>
<li>Add searchsorted (ie lower/upper_bound) op.</li>
<li>Add model explainability to Boosted Trees.</li>
<li>Support negative positions for tf.substr.</li>
<li>There was previously a bug in the bijector_impl where the
    _reduce_jacobian_det_over_event does not handle scalar ILDJ
    implementations properly.</li>
<li>In tf eager execution, allow re-entering a GradientTape context.</li>
<li>Add tf_api_version flag. If --define=tf_api_version=2 flag is passed in,
    then bazel will build TensorFlow API version 2.0. Note that TensorFlow
    2.0 is under active development and has no guarantees at this point.</li>
<li>Add additional compression options to TfRecordWriter.</li>
<li>Performance improvements for regex full match operations.</li>
<li>Replace tf.GraphKeys.VARIABLES with <code>tf.GraphKeys.GLOBAL_VARIABLES</code>.</li>
<li>Remove unused dynamic learning rate support.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.11.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Nvidia GPU:<ul>
<li>Prebuilt binaries are now (as of TensorFlow 1.11) built against cuDNN
    7.2 and TensorRT 4. See updated install guides:
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/install/install_linux#tensorflow_gpu_support">Installing TensorFlow on Ubuntu</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Google Cloud TPU:<ul>
<li>Experimental tf.data integration for Keras on Google Cloud TPUs.</li>
<li>Experimental / preview support for eager execution on Google Cloud TPUs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>DistributionStrategy:<ul>
<li>Add multi-GPU DistributionStrategy support in tf.keras. Users can now
    use <code>fit</code>, <code>evaluate</code> and <code>predict</code> to distribute their model on
    multiple GPUs.</li>
<li>Add multi-worker DistributionStrategy and standalone client support in
    Estimator. See
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/master/tensorflow/contrib/distribute">README</a>
    for more details.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add C, C++, and Python functions for querying kernels.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Keras:<ul>
<li>The default values for tf.keras <code>RandomUniform</code>, <code>RandomNormal</code>, and
    <code>TruncatedNormal</code> initializers have been changed to match those in
    external Keras.</li>
<li>Breaking change: <code>model.get_config()</code> on a Sequential model now returns
    a config dictionary (consistent with other Model instances) instead of a
    list of configs for the underlying layers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>C++:<ul>
<li>Changed the signature of SessionFactory::NewSession so that it can
    return a meaningful error message on failure.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>tf.data:<ul>
<li>Remove <code>num_parallel_parser_calls</code> argument from
    <code>tf.contrib.data.make_csv_dataset()</code>. [tf.data] Remove
    <code>num_parallel_parser_calls</code> argument from
    <code>tf.contrib.data.make_csv_dataset()</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.data.Dataset.list_files()</code> raises an exception at initialization
    time if the argument matches no files.</li>
<li>Renamed BigTable class to BigtableTable for clarity</li>
<li>Document use of the Cloud Bigtable API</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.reduce_dataset</code> which can be used to reduce a
    dataset to a single element.</li>
<li>Generalization of <code>tf.contrib.data.sliding_window_batch</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>INC:<ul>
<li>Runtime improvements to triangular solve.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li>Add an <code>implementation</code> argument to <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected2D</code>
    and <code>tf.keras.layers.LocallyConnected1D</code>. The new mode
    (<code>implementation=2</code>) performs forward pass as a single dense matrix
    multiplication, allowing dramatic speedups in certain scenarios (but
    worse performance in others - see docstring). The option also allows to
    use <code>padding=same</code>.</li>
<li>Add documentation clarifying the differences between tf.fill and
    tf.constant.</li>
<li>Add experimental IndexedDatasets.</li>
<li>Add selective registration target using the lite proto runtime.</li>
<li>Add simple Tensor and DataType classes to TensorFlow Lite Java</li>
<li>Add support for bitcasting to/from uint32 and uint64.</li>
<li>Added a subclass of Estimator that can be created from a SavedModel
    (SavedModelEstimator).</li>
<li>Adds leaf index modes as an argument.</li>
<li>Allow a different output shape from the input in
    tf.contrib.image.transform.</li>
<li>Change the state_size order of the StackedRNNCell to be natural order.
    To keep the existing behavior, user can add reverse_state_order=True
    when constructing the StackedRNNCells.</li>
<li>Deprecate self.test_session() in favor of self.session() or
    self.cached_session().</li>
<li>Directly import tensor.proto.h (the transitive import will be removed
    from tensor.h soon).</li>
<li>Estimator.train() now supports tf.contrib.summary.* summaries out of
    the box; each call to .train() will now create a separate tfevents file
    rather than re-using a shared one.</li>
<li>Fix FTRL L2-shrinkage behavior: the gradient from the L2 shrinkage term
    should not end up in the accumulator.</li>
<li>Fix toco compilation/execution on Windows.</li>
<li>GoogleZoneProvider class added to detect which Google Cloud Engine zone
    tensorflow is running in.</li>
<li>It is now safe to call any of the C API's TF_Delete* functions on
    nullptr.</li>
<li>Log some errors on Android to logcat.</li>
<li>Match FakeQuant numerics in TFLite to improve accuracy of TFLite
    quantized inference models.</li>
<li>Optional bucket location check for the GCS Filesystem.</li>
<li>Performance enhancements for StringSplitOp &amp; StringSplitV2Op.</li>
<li>Performance improvements for regex replace operations.</li>
<li>TFRecordWriter now raises an error if .write() fails.</li>
<li>TPU: More helpful error messages in TPUClusterResolvers.</li>
<li>The legacy_init_op argument to SavedModelBuilder methods for adding
    MetaGraphs has been deprecated. Please use the equivalent main_op
    argument instead. As part of this, we now explicitly check for a single
    main_op or legacy_init_op at the time of SavedModel building, whereas
    the check on main_op was previously only done at load time.</li>
<li>The protocol used for Estimator training is now configurable in
    RunConfig.</li>
<li>Triangular solve performance improvements.</li>
<li>Unify RNN cell interface between TF and Keras. Add new
    get_initial_state() to Keras and TF RNN cell, which will use to replace
    the existing zero_state() method.</li>
<li>Update initialization of variables in Keras.</li>
<li>Updates to "constrained_optimization" in tensorflow/contrib.</li>
<li>boosted trees: adding pruning mode.</li>
<li>tf.train.Checkpoint does not delete old checkpoints by default.</li>
<li>tfdbg: Limit the total disk space occupied by dumped tensor data to 100
    GBytes. Add environment variable <code>TFDBG_DISK_BYTES_LIMIT</code> to allow
    adjustment of this upper limit.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
