<h1>Release 1.10.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>Fixing keras on Cloud TPUs. No new binaries will be built for Windows.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.10.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>The <code>tf.lite</code> runtime now supports <code>complex64</code>.</li>
<li>Initial
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/r1.10/tensorflow/contrib/bigtable">Google Cloud Bigtable integration</a>
    for <code>tf.data</code>.</li>
<li>Improved local run behavior in <code>tf.estimator.train_and_evaluate</code> which does
    not reload checkpoints for evaluation.</li>
<li><code>RunConfig</code> now sets device_filters to restrict how workers and PS can
    communicate. This can speed up training and ensure clean shutdowns in some
    situations. But if you have jobs that require communication between workers,
    you will have to set custom session_options in your <code>RunConfig</code>.</li>
<li>Moved Distributions and Bijectors from <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code> to
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/probability">Tensorflow Probability (TFP)</a>.
    <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code> is now deprecated and will be removed by the end
    of 2018.</li>
<li>Adding new endpoints for existing tensorflow symbols. These endpoints are
    going to be the preferred endpoints going forward and may replace some of
    the existing endpoints in the future. See below for the complete list. New
    symbols have been added to the following modules:
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/debugging"><code>tf.debugging</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/dtypes"><code>tf.dtypes</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/image"><code>tf.image</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/io"><code>tf.io</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/linalg"><code>tf.linalg</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/manip"><code>tf.manip</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/math"><code>tf.math</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/quantization"><code>tf.quantization</code></a>,
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/api_docs/python/tf/strings"><code>tf.strings</code></a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Prebuilt binaries are now (as of TensorFlow 1.10) built against NCCL 2.2 and
    no longer include NCCL in the binary install. TensorFlow usage with multiple
    GPUs and NCCL requires upgrade to
    <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/nccl">NCCL 2.2</a>. See updated install guides:
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/install/gpu">TensorFlow GPU support</a> and
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/install/source">Build TensorFlow from source</a>.</li>
<li>Starting from TensorFlow 1.11, Windows builds will use Bazel. Therefore, we
    will drop official support for cmake.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data.group_by_reducer()</code> is now available via the public
    API.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data.choose_from_datasets()</code> is now available via the public
    API.</li>
<li>Adding <code>drop_remainder</code> argument to <code>tf.data.Dataset.batch()</code> and
    <code>tf.data.Dataset.padded_batch()</code>, deprecating
    <code>tf.contrib.data.batch_and_drop_remainder()</code> and
    <code>tf.contrib.data.padded_batch_and_drop_remainder()</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.estimator</code>:<ul>
<li><code>Estimator</code>s now use custom savers included in <code>EstimatorSpec</code> scaffolds
    for saving SavedModels during export.</li>
<li><code>EstimatorSpec</code> will now add a default prediction output for export if
    no <code>export_output</code> is provided, eliminating the need to explicitly
    include a <code>PredictOutput</code> object in the <code>model_fn</code> for simple use-cases.</li>
<li>Support sparse_combiner in canned Linear Estimators.</li>
<li>Added batch normalization to <code>DNNClassifier</code>, <code>DNNRegressor</code>, and
    <code>DNNEstimator</code>.</li>
<li>Adding ranking support for boosted trees.</li>
<li>Adding center bias option for boosted trees.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add <code>synchronization</code> and <code>aggregation</code> args to get_variable(). These args
    will be used for distributed variables.</li>
<li>Add <code>synchronization</code> and <code>aggregation</code> args to the layer <code>add_weight()</code>
    API. These args will be used for distributed variables.</li>
<li><code>tf.losses.*</code> do not add to the global collection when executing eagerly (to
    avoid leaking memory).</li>
<li>Support different summary and checkpoint directories in
    <code>tf.train.MonitoredTrainingSession()</code>.</li>
<li>Added IndRNN, IndyGRU, and IndyLSTM cells to <code>tf.contrib.rnn</code>.</li>
<li>Add safe static factory functions for SparseTensor and convert all CHECKs to
    DCHECKs. Using the constructor directly is unsafe and deprecated.</li>
<li>Make the Bigtable client connection pool configurable &amp; increase the
    default # of connections for performance.</li>
<li>Added derivative of <code>tf.random_gamma</code> with respect to the alpha parameter.</li>
<li>Added derivative of <code>tf.igamma(a, x)</code> and <code>tf.igammac(a, x)</code> with respect to
    a.</li>
<li>Modified Bessel functions of order zero and one.</li>
<li>Add FillTriangular Bijector to create triangular matrices.</li>
<li>Added support for Type III DCT, and <code>tf.spectral.idct(type=2|3)</code>.</li>
<li>Correctly handle CuDNN RNN weight loaded when nest in <code>TimeDistributed</code>.</li>
<li>Adding per-element weight support for <code>WALSComputePartialLhsAndRhsOp</code>.</li>
<li>ZerosLike and OnesLike ops treated as constants by Graph Transform Tool.</li>
<li>Gamma distribution and the derived distributions (Beta, Dirichlet, Student's
    t, inverse Gamma) now fully reparameterized.</li>
<li>Java: Experimental wrapper classes to make graph generation easier. Thanks
    @karllessard and @kbsriram</li>
<li>Build &amp; link in secure gRPC components (switch from the insecure grpc
    dependency to secure grpc dependency).</li>
<li>Adding new endpoints for existing tensorflow symbols. These endpoints are
    going to be the preferred endpoints going forward and may replace some of
    the existing endpoints in the future. List of new endpoints:<ul>
<li>New endpoints in <code>tf.image</code> namespace: <code>tf.image.extract_image_patches</code></li>
<li>New endpoints in <code>tf.debugging</code> namespace:
    <code>tf.debugging.check_numerics</code>, <code>tf.debugging.is_finite</code>,
    <code>tf.debugging.is_inf</code>, <code>tf.debugging.is_nan</code>.</li>
<li>New endpoints in <code>tf.dtypes</code> namespace: <code>tf.dtypes.as_string</code>.</li>
<li>New endpoints in <code>tf.io</code> namespace: <code>tf.io.decode_base64</code>,
    <code>tf.io.decode_compressed</code>, <code>tf.io.decode_json_example</code>,
    <code>tf.io.decode_raw</code>, <code>tf.io.encode_base64</code>, <code>tf.io.matching_files</code>,
    <code>tf.io.parse_tensor</code>, <code>tf.io.read_file,</code>tf.io.write_file`.</li>
<li>New endpoints in tf.linalg namespace: <code>tf.linalg.cross</code>,
    <code>tf.linalg.tensor_diag</code> (corresponds to <code>tf.diag</code>),
    <code>tf.linalg.tensor_diag_part</code> (corresponds to <code>tf.diag_part</code>).</li>
<li>New endpoints in tf.manip namespace: <code>tf.manip.batch_to_space_nd</code>,
    <code>tf.manip.gather_nd</code>, <code>tf.manip.reshape</code>, <code>tf.manip.reverse</code>,
    <code>tf.manip.scatter_nd</code>, <code>tf.manip.space_to_batch_nd</code>, <code>tf.manip.tile</code></li>
<li>New endpoints in tf.math namespace: <code>tf.math.acos</code>, <code>tf.math.acosh</code>,
    <code>tf.math.add</code>, <code>tf.math.asin</code>, <code>tf.math.asinh</code>, <code>tf.math.atan</code>,
    <code>tf.math.atan2</code>, <code>tf.math.atanh</code>, <code>tf.math.betainc</code>, <code>tf.math.ceil</code>,
    <code>tf.math.cos</code>, <code>tf.math.cosh</code>, <code>tf.math.digamma</code>, <code>tf.math.equal</code>,
    <code>tf.math.erfc</code>, <code>tf.math.exp</code>, <code>tf.math.expm1</code>, <code>tf.math.floor</code>,
    <code>tf.math.greater</code>, <code>tf.math.greater_equal</code>, <code>tf.math.igamma</code>,
    <code>tf.math.igammac</code>, <code>tf.math.invert_permutation</code>, <code>tf.math.less</code>,
    <code>tf.math.less_equal</code>, <code>tf.math.lgamma</code>, <code>tf.math.log</code>, <code>tf.math.log1p</code>,
    <code>tf.math.logical_and</code>, <code>tf.math.logical_not</code>, <code>tf.math.logical_or</code>,
    <code>tf.math.maximum</code>, <code>tf.math.minimum</code>, <code>tf.math.not_equal</code>,
    <code>tf.math.polygamma</code>, <code>tf.math.reciprocal</code>, <code>tf.math.rint</code>,
    <code>tf.math.rsqrt</code>, <code>tf.math.segment_max</code>, <code>tf.math.segment_mean</code>,
    <code>tf.math.segment_min</code>, <code>tf.math.segment_prod</code>, <code>tf.math.segment_sum</code>,
    <code>tf.math.sin</code>, <code>tf.math.sinh</code>, <code>tf.math.softplus</code>, <code>tf.math.softsign</code>,
    <code>tf.math.squared_difference</code>, <code>tf.math.tan</code>,
    <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_max</code>, <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_min</code>,
    <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_prod</code>, <code>tf.math.unsorted_segment_sum</code>,
    <code>tf.math.zeta</code>.</li>
<li>New endpoints in <code>tf.quantization</code> namespace:
    <code>tf.quantization.dequantize</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_args</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_args_gradient</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_vars</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_vars_gradient</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_vars_per_channel</code>,
    <code>tf.quantization.fake_quant_with_min_max_vars_per_channel_gradient</code>.</li>
<li>New endpoints in tf.strings namespace: <code>tf.strings.join</code> (corresponds to
    <code>tf.string_join</code>), <code>tf.strings.regex_replace</code>, <code>tf.strings.to_number</code>
    (corresponds to <code>tf.string_to_number</code>), <code>tf.strings.strip</code> (corresponds
    to <code>tf.string_strip</code>), <code>tf.strings.substr</code>, <code>tf.strings.to_hash_bucket</code>
    (corresponds to <code>tf.string_to_hash_bucket</code>),
    <code>tf.strings.to_hash_bucket_fast</code> (corresponds to
    <code>tf.string_to_hash_bucket_fast</code>), <code>tf.strings.to_hash_bucket_strong</code>
    (corresponds to <code>tf.string_to_hash_bucket_strong</code>).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.9.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Updated docs for <code>tf.keras</code>: New Keras-based
    <a href="http://tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/get_started">get started</a>, and
    <a href="http://tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/programmers_guide/keras">programmers guide page</a>.</li>
<li>Update <code>tf.keras</code> to the Keras 2.1.6 API.</li>
<li>Added
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/keras/layers/CuDNNGRU"><code>tf.keras.layers.CuDNNGRU</code></a>
    and
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/keras/layers/CuDNNLSTM"><code>tf.keras.layers.CuDNNLSTM</code></a>
    layers.
    <a href="https://colab.sandbox.google.com/github/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/contrib/eager/python/examples/nmt_with_attention/nmt_with_attention.ipynb?linkId=53292082">Try it</a>.</li>
<li>Adding support of core
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/get_started/feature_columns">feature columns</a>
    and <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/api_docs/python/tf/losses">losses</a> to
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/models/tree/master/official/r1/boosted_trees">gradient boosted trees estimators</a>.</li>
<li>The
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/lite">python interface</a>
    for the
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/lite/toco/README.md">TFLite Optimizing Converter</a>
    has been expanded, and the command line interface (AKA: <code>toco</code>,
    <code>tflite_convert</code>) is once again included in the standard <code>pip</code> installation.</li>
<li>Improved data-loading and text processing with:<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/decode_compressed"><code>tf.decode_compressed</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/string_strip"><code>tf.string_strip</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/strings/regex_full_match"><code>tf.strings.regex_full_match</code></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Added experimental support for new pre-made Estimators:<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/contrib/estimator/BaselineEstimator"><code>tf.contrib.estimator.BaselineEstimator</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/contrib/estimator/RNNEstimator"><code>tf.contrib.estimator.RNNClassifier</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/contrib/estimator/RNNClassifier"><code>tf.contrib.estimator.RNNEstimator</code></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/contrib/distributions/bijectors/Bijector">distributions.Bijector</a>
    API supports broadcasting for Bijectors with new API changes.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>If you're opening empty variable scopes; replace <code>variable_scope('', ...)</code>
    by <code>variable_scope(tf.get_variable_scope(), ...)</code>.</li>
<li>Headers used for building custom ops have been moved from
    site-packages/external into site-packages/tensorflow/include/external.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tfe.Network</code> is deprecated. Please inherit from <code>tf.keras.Model</code>.</li>
<li>Layered variable names have changed in the following conditions:<ul>
<li>Using <code>tf.keras.layers</code> with custom variable scopes.</li>
<li>Using <code>tf.layers</code> in a subclassed <code>tf.keras.Model</code> class. See
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/r1.9/api_docs/python/tf/layers">here</a>
    for more details</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li><code>Dataset.from_generator()</code> now accepts an <code>args</code> list, in order to
    create nested generators.</li>
<li><code>Dataset.list_files()</code> now produces deterministic results when
    <code>shuffle=False</code> or a <code>seed</code> is passed.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data.sample_from_datasets()</code> and
    <code>tf.contrib.data.choose_from_datasets()</code> make it easier to sample or
    deterministically choose elements from multiple datasets.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data.make_csv_dataset()</code> now supports line breaks in quoted
    strings, and two infrequently used arguments removed.</li>
<li>(C++) <code>DatasetBase::DebugString()</code> is now <code>const</code>.</li>
<li>(C++) <code>DatasetBase::MakeIterator()</code> has been renamed to
    <code>DatasetBase::MakeIteratorInternal()</code>.</li>
<li>(C++) <code>IteratorBase::Initialize()</code> method was added to support raising
    errors during iterator construction.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Eager Execution:<ul>
<li>Added the ability to pause recording operations for gradient computation
    via <code>tf.GradientTape.stop_recording</code>.</li>
<li>Updated documentation, introductory notebooks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>Move Keras code out of _impl folder and remove API files.</li>
<li><code>tf.keras.Model.save_weights</code> now saves in TensorFlow format by default.</li>
<li>Enable dataset iterators to be passed to <code>tf.keras.Model</code> training/eval
    methods.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg) CLI: fix an issue in which the TensorBoard
    Debugger Plugin could not handle total source file size exceeding gRPC
    message size limit (4 MB).</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib.framework.zero_initializer</code> supports ResourceVariable.</li>
<li>Adding "constrained_optimization" to tensorflow/contrib.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Add GCS Configuration Ops.</li>
<li>Changing signature of <code>MakeIterator</code> to enable propagating error status.</li>
<li>KL divergence for two Dirichlet distributions.</li>
<li>More consistent GcsFileSystem behavior for certain reads past EOF.</li>
<li>Update benchmark for tf.scan to match ranges across eager and graph
    modes.</li>
<li>Fixed bug in <code>tf.reduce_prod gradient</code> for complex dtypes.</li>
<li>Allow the use of '.' in variables (e.g. "hparams.parse('a.b=1.0')"),
    which would previously raise an error. This will correspond to an
    attribute name with an embedded '.' symbol (e.g. 'a.b'), which can only
    be accessed indirectly (e.g. through getattr and setattr). To set this
    up the user will first need to explicitly add the variable to the hparam
    object (e.g. "hparams.add_hparam(name='a.b', value=0.0)").</li>
<li>Benchmark for tf.scan in graph and eager modes.</li>
<li>Added complex128 support to FFT, FFT2D, FFT3D, IFFT, IFFT2D, and IFFT3D.</li>
<li>Making ids unique in <code>nn.embedding_lookup_sparse</code>. This helps to reduce
    RPC calls for looking up the embeddings when there are repeated ids in
    the batch.</li>
<li>Support indicator column in boosted trees.</li>
<li>Prevent <code>tf.gradients()</code> from backpropagating through integer tensors.</li>
<li>LinearOperator[1D,2D,3D]Circulant added to <code>tensorflow.linalg</code>.</li>
<li>Conv3D, Conv3DBackpropInput, Conv3DBackpropFilter now supports
    arbitrary.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.train.Checkpoint</code> for reading/writing object-based
    checkpoints.</li>
<li>Added LinearOperatorKronecker, a dense-free implementation of the
    Kronecker Product.</li>
<li>Allow LinearOperator to broadcast.</li>
<li>SavedModelBuilder will now deduplicate asset names that point to files
    with the same basename and the same contents. Note that this may result
    in new asset files included in SavedModels in cases where assets with
    the same name but different contents were previously overwriting each
    other.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.8.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Can now pass <code>tf.contrib.distribute.MirroredStrategy()</code> to
    <code>tf.estimator.RunConfig()</code> to run an Estimator model on multiple GPUs on one
    machine.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.prefetch_to_device()</code>, which supports prefetching to
    GPU memory.</li>
<li>Added Gradient Boosted Trees as pre-made Estimators: BoostedTreesClassifier,
    BoostedTreesRegressor.</li>
<li>Add 3rd generation pipeline config for Cloud TPUs which improves performance
    and usability.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.bayesflow</code> is moving out to it's own repo.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.{proto,rpc}</code> to allow generic proto parsing and RPC
    communication<sup><a href="#rpc-issue">1</a></sup>.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.prefetch_to_device</code>, which enables prefetching
    dataset elements to GPU memory.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.AUTOTUNE</code>, which allows the tf.data runtime to
    automatically tune the prefetch buffer sizes based on your system and
    environment.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.make_csv_dataset</code> for building datasets of CSV
    files.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Eager Execution:<ul>
<li>With eager execution Datasets can now be used as standard python
    iterators (<code>for batch in dataset:</code>). Both <code>Dataset.__iter__()</code> and
    <code>Dataset.make_one_shot_iterator()</code> can now be used to create iterators
    when eager execution is enabled.</li>
<li>Automatic device placement has been enabled (i.e., use a GPU if
    available automatically, without requiring an explicit <code>with
    tf.device(“/gpu:0”)</code>) (Fixes #14133)</li>
<li><code>tf.GradientTape</code> has moved out of contrib.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.keras</code>:<ul>
<li>Added the fashion mnist dataset.</li>
<li>New data preprocessing functions: <code>image/random_brightness</code>,
    <code>sequence/TimeseriesGenerator</code>, and <code>text/hashing_trick</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Accelerated Linear Algebra (XLA):<ul>
<li>Select and scatter in reference util and evaluator now use
    lexicographical order to break ties.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg) CLI:<ul>
<li>During tensor-filter operations, allow exclusion of nodes by regular
    expressions.</li>
<li>Fix spurious background colors in some text terminals.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li>Add meta-distribution BatchReshape which reshapes batch dimensions.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.layers.recompute_grad</code> works for explicit gradient
    checkpointing on TPU.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.framework.argsort</code>.</li>
<li>Allow <code>DNNBoostedTreeCombinedEstimator</code> to work with core versions of
    feature columns and losses.</li>
<li>Add non-linear image warping ops: <code>tf.contrib.image.sparse_image_warp</code>,
    <code>tf.contrib.image.dense_image_warp</code>, and
    <code>tf.contrib.image.interpolate_spline</code>.</li>
<li>Fix bug in <code>tf.contrib.opt.MultitaskOptimizerWrapper</code> where types of
    tensors were mismatched.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Low-level graph construction now calls the TensorFlow C API. This change
    should be invisible to most users, but can be disabled by setting the
    environment variable <code>TF_C_API_GRAPH_CONSTRUCTION=0</code> in this release.
    Future releases will remove the ability to disable this change. Please
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/issues/new">file a bug</a> if you
    find yourself using this escape hatch.</li>
<li>Add description of shapes and a pointer to tutorial notebook in
    <code>tf.distributions.Distribution</code>.</li>
<li>Update scatter operations:</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.scatter_min</code> and <code>tf.scatter_max</code></li>
<li>Extend scatter operations to work with a scalar update parameter.</li>
<li>Move cuDNN RNN ops to core for use in TensorFlow codebase only.</li>
<li>Add <code>float64</code> support for <code>Conv2d</code>, <code>Conv2dBackpropInput</code>, and
    <code>Conv2dBackpropFilter</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>float64</code> support for <code>AvgPool</code>/<code>AvgPoolGrad</code>.</li>
<li>Make graph name scope thread local so that they work correctly in
    multi-threaded environments.</li>
<li>Update nsync synchronization library to avoid slow primitives on Linux.</li>
<li>Removed need to put nsync/public on C include path when building custom
    ops.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.image.psnr</code>, <code>tf.image.ssim</code>, <code>tf.image.ssim_multiscale</code>,
    <code>tf.image.image_gradients</code>, <code>tf.image.sobel_edges</code>.</li>
<li>Add links to https://js.tensorflow.org.</li>
<li>Fix non-uniformity of orthogonal matrices.</li>
<li>Fix bug where multi-image Estimator eval summaries were not displayed
    correctly.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="rpc-issue"><sup>1</sup></a> The cancellation logic of the RPC op
contains a concurrency error. A fix has been submitted to master and will be
part of the next release.</p>

<h1>Release 1.7.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Eager mode is moving out of contrib, try <code>tf.enable_eager_execution()</code>.</li>
<li>Graph rewrites emulating fixed-point quantization compatible with TensorFlow
    Lite, supported by new <code>tf.contrib.quantize</code> package.</li>
<li>Easily customize gradient computation with <code>tf.custom_gradient</code>.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorboard/blob/master/tensorboard/plugins/debugger/README.md">TensorBoard Debugger Plugin</a>,
    the graphical user interface (GUI) of TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg), is now in
    alpha.</li>
<li>Experimental support for reading a sqlite database as a <code>Dataset</code> with new
    <code>tf.contrib.data.SqlDataset</code>.</li>
<li>Distributed Mutex / CriticalSection added to
    <code>tf.contrib.framework.CriticalSection</code>.</li>
<li>Better text processing with <code>tf.regex_replace</code>.</li>
<li>Easy, efficient sequence input with
    <code>tf.contrib.data.bucket_by_sequence_length</code></li>
<li>Initial support for <code>tf.contrib.tensorrt</code> that enables native TensorRT in
    TensorFlow.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Accelerated Linear Algebra (XLA):<ul>
<li>Add <code>MaxPoolGradGrad</code> support for XLA</li>
<li>CSE pass from Tensorflow is now disabled in XLA.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.data.Dataset</code></li>
<li>Add support for building C++ Dataset op kernels as external libraries,
    using the <code>tf.load_op_library()</code> mechanism.</li>
<li><code>Dataset.list_files()</code> now shuffles its output by default.</li>
<li><code>Dataset.shuffle(..., seed=tf.constant(0, dtype=tf.int64))</code> now yields
    the same sequence of elements as <code>Dataset.shuffle(..., seed=0)</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>num_parallel_reads</code> argument to <code>tf.data.TFRecordDataset</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.halton_sequence</code> now supports randomization.</li>
<li>Add support for scalars in <code>tf.contrib.all_reduce</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>effective_sample_size</code> to <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.mcmc_diagnostics</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>potential_scale_reduction</code> to
    <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.mcmc_diagnostics</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>BatchNormalization</code>, <code>Kumaraswamy</code> bijectors.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>tf.contrib.learn</code>. Please check contrib/learn/README.md for
    instructions on how to convert existing code.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.data</code></li>
<li>Remove deprecated <code>tf.contrib.data.Dataset</code>, <code>tf.contrib.data.Iterator</code>,
    <code>tf.contrib.data.FixedLengthRecordDataset</code>,
    <code>tf.contrib.data.TextLineDataset</code>, and <code>tf.contrib.data.TFRecordDataset</code>
    classes.</li>
<li>Added <code>bucket_by_sequence_length</code>, <code>sliding_window_batch</code>, and
    <code>make_batched_features_dataset</code></li>
<li>Remove unmaintained <code>tf.contrib.ndlstm</code>. You can find it externally at
    https://github.com/tmbarchive/tfndlstm.</li>
<li>Moved most of <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow</code> to its own repo: <code>tfp</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>tf.py_func now reports the full stack trace if an exception occurs.</li>
<li>Integrate <code>TPUClusterResolver</code> with GKE's integration for Cloud TPUs.</li>
<li>Add a library for statistical testing of samplers.</li>
<li>Add Helpers to stream data from the GCE VM to a Cloud TPU.</li>
<li>Integrate ClusterResolvers with TPUEstimator.</li>
<li>Unify metropolis_hastings interface with HMC kernel.</li>
<li>Move LIBXSMM convolutions to a separate --define flag so that they are
    disabled by default.</li>
<li>Fix <code>MomentumOptimizer</code> lambda.</li>
<li>Reduce <code>tfp.layers</code> boilerplate via programmable docstrings.</li>
<li>Add <code>auc_with_confidence_intervals</code>, a method for computing the AUC and
    confidence interval with linearithmic time complexity.</li>
<li><code>regression_head</code> now accepts customized link function, to satisfy the
    usage that user can define their own link function if the
    <code>array_ops.identity</code> does not meet the requirement.</li>
<li>Fix <code>initialized_value</code> and <code>initial_value</code> behaviors for
    <code>ResourceVariables</code> created from <code>VariableDef</code> protos.</li>
<li>Add TensorSpec to represent the specification of Tensors.</li>
<li>Constant folding pass is now deterministic.</li>
<li>Support <code>float16</code> <code>dtype</code> in <code>tf.linalg.*</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.estimator.export.TensorServingInputReceiver</code> that allows
    <code>tf.estimator.Estimator.export_savedmodel</code> to pass raw tensors to model
    functions.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Deprecations</h2>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow 1.7 may be the last time we support Cuda versions below 8.0.
    Starting with TensorFlow 1.8 release, 8.0 will be the minimum supported
    version.</li>
<li>TensorFlow 1.7 may be the last time we support cuDNN versions below 6.0.
    Starting with TensorFlow 1.8 release, 6.0 will be the minimum supported
    version.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.6.0</h1>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Prebuilt binaries are now built against CUDA 9.0 and cuDNN 7.</li>
<li>Prebuilt binaries will use AVX instructions. This may break TF on older
    CPUs.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>New Optimizer internal API for non-slot variables. Descendants of
    AdamOptimizer that access _beta[12]_power will need to be updated.</li>
<li><code>tf.estimator.{FinalExporter,LatestExporter}</code> now export stripped
    SavedModels. This improves forward compatibility of the SavedModel.</li>
<li>FFT support added to XLA CPU/GPU.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Documentation updates:<ul>
<li>Added a second version of Getting Started, which is aimed at ML
    newcomers.</li>
<li>Clarified documentation on <code>resize_images.align_corners</code> parameter.</li>
<li>Additional documentation for TPUs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Google Cloud Storage (GCS):<ul>
<li>Add client-side throttle.</li>
<li>Add a <code>FlushCaches()</code> method to the FileSystem interface, with an
    implementation for GcsFileSystem.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.Kumaraswamy</code>.</li>
<li><code>RetryingFileSystem::FlushCaches()</code> calls the base FileSystem's
    <code>FlushCaches()</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>auto_correlation</code> to distributions.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.Autoregressive</code>.</li>
<li>Add SeparableConv1D layer.</li>
<li>Add convolutional Flipout layers.</li>
<li>When both inputs of <code>tf.matmul</code> are bfloat16, it returns bfloat16,
    instead of float32.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.image.connected_components</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.framework.CriticalSection</code> that allows atomic variable
    access.</li>
<li>Output variance over trees predictions for classifications tasks.</li>
<li>For <code>pt</code> and <code>eval</code> commands, allow writing tensor values to filesystem
    as numpy files.</li>
<li>gRPC: Propagate truncated errors (instead of returning gRPC internal
    error).</li>
<li>Augment <code>parallel_interleave</code> to support 2 kinds of prefetching.</li>
<li>Improved XLA support for C64-related ops log, pow, atan2, tanh.</li>
<li>Add probabilistic convolutional layers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>API Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Introducing <code>prepare_variance</code> boolean with default setting to False for
    backward compatibility.</li>
<li>Move <code>layers_dense_variational_impl.py</code> to <code>layers_dense_variational.py</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Bugs</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Using XLA:GPU with CUDA 9 and CUDA 9.1 results in garbage results and/or
    <code>CUDA_ILLEGAL_ADDRESS</code> failures.</p>
<p>Google discovered in mid-December 2017 that the PTX-to-SASS compiler in CUDA
9 and CUDA 9.1 sometimes does not properly compute the carry bit when
decomposing 64-bit address calculations with large offsets (e.g. <code>load [x +
large_constant]</code>) into 32-bit arithmetic in SASS.</p>
<p>As a result, these versions of <code>ptxas</code> miscompile most XLA programs which
use more than 4GB of temp memory. This results in garbage results and/or
<code>CUDA_ERROR_ILLEGAL_ADDRESS</code> failures.</p>
<p>A fix in CUDA 9.1.121 is expected in late February 2018. We do not expect a
fix for CUDA 9.0.x. Until the fix is available, the only workaround is to
<a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/cuda-toolkit-archive">downgrade</a> to CUDA 8.0.x
or disable XLA:GPU.</p>
<p>TensorFlow will print a warning if you use XLA:GPU with a known-bad version
of CUDA; see e00ba24c4038e7644da417ddc639169b6ea59122.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.5.0</h1>
<h2>Breaking Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Prebuilt binaries are now built against CUDA 9.0 and cuDNN 7.</li>
<li>Starting from 1.6 release, our prebuilt binaries will use AVX instructions.
    This may break TF on older CPUs.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/r1.5/tensorflow/contrib/eager">Eager execution</a>
    preview version is now available.</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/r1.5/tensorflow/lite">TensorFlow Lite</a>
    dev preview is now available.</li>
<li>CUDA 9.0 and cuDNN 7 support.</li>
<li>Accelerated Linear Algebra (XLA):<ul>
<li>Add <code>complex64</code> support to XLA compiler.</li>
<li><code>bfloat</code> support is now added to XLA infrastructure.</li>
<li>Make <code>ClusterSpec</code> propagation work with XLA devices.</li>
<li>Use a deterministic executor to generate XLA graph.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib</code>:<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions</code>:</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.Autoregressive</code>.</li>
<li>Make <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code> QuadratureCompound classes support batch</li>
<li>Infer <code>tf.contrib.distributions.RelaxedOneHotCategorical</code> <code>dtype</code> from
    arguments.</li>
<li>Make <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code> quadrature family parameterized by
    <code>quadrature_grid_and_prob</code> vs <code>quadrature_degree</code>.</li>
<li><code>auto_correlation</code> added to <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code></li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.layers</code>, a collection of probabilistic
    (neural) layers.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.halton_sequence</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.make_saveable_from_iterator.</code></li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.data.shuffle_and_repeat</code>.</li>
<li>Add new custom transformation: <code>tf.contrib.data.scan()</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijectors</code>:</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijectors.MaskedAutoregressiveFlow</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijectors.Permute</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijectors.Gumbel</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijectors.Reshape</code>.</li>
<li>Support shape inference (i.e., shapes containing -1) in the Reshape
    bijector.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add <code>streaming_precision_recall_at_equal_thresholds,</code> a method for computing
    streaming precision and recall with <code>O(num_thresholds + size of
    predictions)</code> time and space complexity.</li>
<li>Change <code>RunConfig</code> default behavior to not set a random seed, making random
    behavior independently random on distributed workers. We expect this to
    generally improve training performance. Models that do rely on determinism
    should set a random seed explicitly.</li>
<li>Replaced the implementation of <code>tf.flags</code> with <code>absl.flags</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for <code>CUBLAS_TENSOR_OP_MATH</code> in fp16 GEMM</li>
<li>Add support for CUDA on NVIDIA Tegra devices</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Documentation updates:<ul>
<li>Clarified that you can only install TensorFlow on 64-bit machines.</li>
<li>Added a short doc explaining how <code>Estimator</code>s save checkpoints.</li>
<li>Add documentation for ops supported by the <code>tf2xla</code> bridge.</li>
<li>Fix minor typos in the doc of <code>SpaceToDepth</code> and <code>DepthToSpace</code>.</li>
<li>Updated documentation comments in <code>mfcc_mel_filterbank.h</code> and <code>mfcc.h</code>
    to clarify that the input domain is squared magnitude spectra and the
    weighting is done on linear magnitude spectra (sqrt of inputs).</li>
<li>Change <code>tf.contrib.distributions</code> docstring examples to use <code>tfd</code> alias
    rather than <code>ds</code>, <code>bs</code>.</li>
<li>Fix docstring typos in <code>tf.distributions.bijectors.Bijector</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.assert_equal</code> no longer raises <code>ValueError.</code> It now raises
    <code>InvalidArgumentError,</code> as documented.</li>
<li>Update Getting Started docs and API intro.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Google Cloud Storage (GCS):<ul>
<li>Add userspace DNS caching for the GCS client.</li>
<li>Customize request timeouts for the GCS filesystem.</li>
<li>Improve GCS filesystem caching.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Bug Fixes:<ul>
<li>Fix bug where partitioned integer variables got their wrong shapes.
    Before</li>
<li>Fix correctness bug in CPU and GPU implementations of Adadelta.</li>
<li>Fix a bug in <code>import_meta_graph</code>'s handling of partitioned variables
    when importing into a scope. WARNING: This may break loading checkpoints
    of graphs with partitioned variables saved after using
    <code>import_meta_graph</code> with a non-empty <code>import_scope</code> argument.</li>
<li>Fix bug in offline debugger which prevented viewing events.</li>
<li>Added the <code>WorkerService.DeleteWorkerSession</code> method to the gRPC
    interface, to fix a memory leak. Ensure that your master and worker
    servers are running the same version of TensorFlow to avoid
    compatibility issues.</li>
<li>Fix bug in peephole implementation of BlockLSTM cell.</li>
<li>Fix bug by casting dtype of <code>log_det_jacobian</code> to match <code>log_prob</code> in
    <code>TransformedDistribution</code>.</li>
<li>Fix a bug in <code>import_meta_graph</code>'s handling of partitioned variables
    when</li>
<li>Ensure <code>tf.distributions.Multinomial</code> doesn't underflow in <code>log_prob</code>.
    Before this change, all partitions of an integer variable were
    initialized with the shape of the unpartitioned variable; after this
    change they are initialized correctly.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Other:<ul>
<li>Add necessary shape util support for bfloat16.</li>
<li>Add a way to run ops using a step function to MonitoredSession.</li>
<li>Add <code>DenseFlipout</code> probabilistic layer.</li>
<li>A new flag <code>ignore_live_threads</code> is available on train. If set to
    <code>True</code>, it will ignore threads that remain running when tearing down
    infrastructure after successfully completing training, instead of
    throwing a RuntimeError.</li>
<li>Restandardize <code>DenseVariational</code> as simpler template for other
    probabilistic layers.</li>
<li><code>tf.data</code> now supports <code>tf.SparseTensor</code> components in dataset elements.</li>
<li>It is now possible to iterate over <code>Tensor</code>s.</li>
<li>Allow <code>SparseSegmentReduction</code> ops to have missing segment IDs.</li>
<li>Modify custom export strategy to account for multidimensional sparse
    float splits.</li>
<li><code>Conv2D</code>, <code>Conv2DBackpropInput</code>, <code>Conv2DBackpropFilter</code> now supports
    arbitrary dilations with GPU and cuDNNv6 support.</li>
<li><code>Estimator</code> now supports <code>Dataset</code>: <code>input_fn</code> can return a <code>Dataset</code>
    instead of <code>Tensor</code>s.</li>
<li>Add <code>RevBlock</code>, a memory-efficient implementation of reversible residual
    layers.</li>
<li>Reduce BFCAllocator internal fragmentation.</li>
<li>Add <code>cross_entropy</code> and <code>kl_divergence</code> to
    <code>tf.distributions.Distribution</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.nn.softmax_cross_entropy_with_logits_v2</code> which enables backprop
    w.r.t. the labels.</li>
<li>GPU back-end now uses <code>ptxas</code> to compile generated PTX.</li>
<li><code>BufferAssignment</code>'s protocol buffer dump is now deterministic.</li>
<li>Change embedding op to use parallel version of <code>DynamicStitch</code>.</li>
<li>Add support for sparse multidimensional feature columns.</li>
<li>Speed up the case for sparse float columns that have only 1 value.</li>
<li>Allow sparse float splits to support multivalent feature columns.</li>
<li>Add <code>quantile</code> to <code>tf.distributions.TransformedDistribution</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>NCHW_VECT_C</code> support for <code>tf.depth_to_space</code> on GPU.</li>
<li>Add <code>NCHW_VECT_C</code> support for <code>tf.space_to_depth</code> on GPU.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>API Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Rename <code>SqueezeDims</code> attribute to <code>Axis</code> in C++ API for Squeeze op.</li>
<li><code>Stream::BlockHostUntilDone</code> now returns Status rather than bool.</li>
<li>Minor refactor: move stats files from <code>stochastic</code> to <code>common</code> and remove
    <code>stochastic</code>.</li>
</ul>

He, Sandeep Dcunha, sandipmgiri, Sang Han, scott, Scott Mudge, Se-Won Kim, Simon

<h1>Release 1.4.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>LinearClassifier</code> fix.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.4.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features And Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.keras</code> is now part of the core TensorFlow API.</li>
<li><a href="http://tensorflow.org/guide/data"><code>tf.data</code></a> is now part of the core
    TensorFlow API.<ul>
<li>The API is now subject to backwards compatibility guarantees.</li>
<li>For a guide to migrating from the <code>tf.contrib.data</code> API, see the
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/r1.4/tensorflow/contrib/data/README.md">README</a>.</li>
<li>Major new features include <code>Dataset.from_generator()</code> (for building an
    input pipeline from a Python generator), and the <code>Dataset.apply()</code>
    method for applying custom transformation functions.</li>
<li>Several custom transformation functions have been added, including
    <code>tf.contrib.data.batch_and_drop_remainder()</code> and
    <code>tf.contrib.data.sloppy_interleave()</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add <code>train_and_evaluate</code> for simple distributed <code>Estimator</code> training.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.spectral.dct</code> for computing the DCT-II.</li>
<li>Add Mel-Frequency Cepstral Coefficient support to <code>tf.contrib.signal</code> (with
    GPU and gradient support).</li>
<li>Add a self-check on <code>import tensorflow</code> for Windows DLL issues.</li>
<li>Add NCHW support to <code>tf.depth_to_space</code> on GPU.</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg):<ul>
<li>Add <code>eval</code> command to allow evaluation of arbitrary Python/numpy
    expressions in tfdbg command-line interface. See
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/debugger">Debugging TensorFlow Programs</a>
    for more details.</li>
<li>Usability improvement: The frequently used tensor filter
    <code>has_inf_or_nan</code> is now added to <code>Session</code> wrappers and hooks by
    default. So there is no need for clients to call
    <code>.add_tensor_filter(tf_debug.has_inf_or_nan)</code> anymore.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>SinhArcsinh (scalar) distribution added to <code>contrib.distributions</code>.</li>
<li>Make <code>GANEstimator</code> opensource.</li>
<li><code>Estimator.export_savedmodel()</code> now includes all valid serving signatures
    that can be constructed from the Serving Input Receiver and all available
    ExportOutputs. For instance, a classifier may provide regression- and
    prediction-flavored outputs, in addition to the classification-flavored one.
    Building signatures from these allows TF Serving to honor requests using the
    different APIs (Classify, Regress, and Predict). Furthermore,
    <code>serving_input_receiver_fn()</code> may now specify alternative subsets of nodes
    that may act as inputs. This allows, for instance, producing a prediction
    signature for a classifier that accepts raw <code>Tensors</code> instead of a
    serialized <code>tf.Example</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.hmc</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.distributions.MixtureSameFamily</code>.</li>
<li>Make <code>Dataset.shuffle()</code> always reshuffles after each iteration by default.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.bayesflow.metropolis_hastings</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>log_rate</code> parameter to <code>tf.contrib.distributions.Poisson</code>.</li>
<li>Extend <code>tf.contrib.distributions.bijector</code> API to handle some non-injective
    transforms.</li>
<li>Java:<ul>
<li>Generics (e.g., <code>Tensor&lt;Integer&gt;</code>) for improved type-safety (courtesy
    @andrewcmyers).</li>
<li>Support for multi-dimensional string tensors.</li>
<li>Support loading of custom operations (e.g. many in <code>tf.contrib</code>) on
    Linux and OS X</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>All our prebuilt binaries have been built with CUDA 8 and cuDNN 6. We
    anticipate releasing TensorFlow 1.5 with CUDA 9 and cuDNN 7.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.nn.rnn_cell.DropoutWrapper</code> is now more careful about dropping out LSTM
    states. Specifically, it no longer ever drops the <code>c</code> (memory) state of an
    <code>LSTMStateTuple</code>. The new behavior leads to proper dropout behavior for
    LSTMs and stacked LSTMs. This bug fix follows recommendations from published
    literature, but is a behavioral change. State dropout behavior may be
    customized via the new <code>dropout_state_filter_visitor</code> argument.</li>
<li>Removed <code>tf.contrib.training.python_input</code>. The same behavior, in a more
    flexible and reproducible package, is available via the new
    <code>tf.contrib.data.Dataset.from_generator</code> method!</li>
<li>Fix <code>tf.contrib.distributions.Affine</code> incorrectly computing
    log-det-jacobian.</li>
<li>Fix <code>tf.random_gamma</code> incorrectly handling non-batch, scalar draws.</li>
<li>Resolved a race condition in TensorForest TreePredictionsV4Op.</li>
<li>Google Cloud Storage file system, Amazon S3 file system, and Hadoop file
    system support are now default build options.</li>
<li>Custom op libraries must link against libtensorflow_framework.so (installed
    at <code>tf.sysconfig.get_lib()</code>).</li>
<li>Change <code>RunConfig</code> default behavior to not set a random seed, making random
    behavior independently random on distributed workers. We expect this to
    generally improve training performance. Models that do rely on determinism
    should set a random seed explicitly.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<ul>
<li>The signature of the <code>tf.contrib.data.rejection_resample()</code> function has
    been changed. It now returns a function that can be used as an argument to
    <code>Dataset.apply()</code>.</li>
<li>Remove <code>tf.contrib.data.Iterator.from_dataset()</code> method. Use
    <code>Dataset.make_initializable_iterator()</code> instead.</li>
<li>Remove seldom used and unnecessary <code>tf.contrib.data.Iterator.dispose_op()</code>.</li>
<li>Reorder some TF-GAN loss functions in a non-backwards compatible way.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Issues</h2>
<ul>
<li>In Python 3, <code>Dataset.from_generator()</code> does not support Unicode strings.
    You must convert any strings to bytes objects before yielding them from the
    generator.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.3.0</h1>
<p>See also
<a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorboard/releases/tag/0.1.4">TensorBoard 0.1.4</a>
release notes.</p>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added canned estimators to Tensorflow library. List of added estimators:<ul>
<li><code>DNNClassifier</code></li>
<li><code>DNNRegressor</code></li>
<li><code>LinearClassifier</code></li>
<li><code>LinearRegressor</code></li>
<li><code>DNNLinearCombinedClassifier</code></li>
<li><code>DNNLinearCombinedRegressor</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>All our prebuilt binaries have been built with cuDNN 6. We anticipate
    releasing TensorFlow 1.4 with cuDNN 7.</li>
<li><code>import tensorflow</code> now goes much faster.</li>
<li>Adds a file cache to the GCS filesystem with configurable max staleness for
    file contents. This permits caching of file contents across close/open
    boundaries.</li>
<li>Added an axis parameter to <code>tf.gather</code>.</li>
<li>Added a <code>constant_values</code> keyword argument to <code>tf.pad</code>.</li>
<li>Adds <code>Dataset.interleave</code> transformation.</li>
<li>Add <code>ConcatenateDataset</code> to concatenate two datasets.</li>
<li>Added Mobilenet support to TensorFlow for Poets training script.</li>
<li>Adds a block cache to the GCS filesystem with configurable block size and
    count.</li>
<li>SinhArcSinh bijector added.</li>
<li>Added <code>Dataset.list_files</code> API.</li>
<li>Introduces new operations and Python bindings for the Cloud TPU.</li>
<li>Adding TensorFlow-iOS CocoaPod for symmetry with tensorflow-android.</li>
<li>Introduces base implementations of ClusterResolvers.</li>
<li>Unify memory representations of TensorShape and PartialTensorShape. As a
    consequence, tensors now have a maximum of 254 dimensions, not 255.</li>
<li>Changed references to LIBXSMM to use version 1.8.1.</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg):<ul>
<li>Display summaries of numeric tensor values with the <code>-s</code> flag to command
    <code>print_tensor</code> or <code>pt</code>.</li>
<li>Display feed values with the <code>print_feed</code> or <code>pf</code> command and clickable
    links in the curses UI.</li>
<li>Runtime profiler at the op level and the Python source line level with
    the <code>run -p</code> command.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Initial release of the statistical distribution library <code>tf.distributions</code>.</li>
<li>GPU kernels and speed improvements for unary <code>tf.where</code> and <code>tf.nn.top_k</code>.</li>
<li>Monotonic Attention wrappers added to <code>tf.contrib.seq2seq</code>.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.signal</code>, a library for signal processing primitives.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.resampler</code>, containing CPU and GPU ops for differentiable
    resampling of images.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>tf.RewriterConfig</code> was removed from the Python API after being available in
    1.2 release candidates (it was never in an actual release). Graph rewriting
    is still available, just not as <code>tf.RewriterConfig</code>. Instead add an explicit
    import.</li>
<li>Breaking change to <code>tf.contrib.data.Dataset</code> APIs that expect a nested
    structure. Lists are now converted to <code>tf.Tensor</code> implicitly. You may need
    to change uses of lists to tuples in existing code. In addition, dicts are
    now supported as a nested structure.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Changes to contrib APIs</h2>
<ul>
<li>Adds tf.contrib.nn.rank_sampled_softmax_loss, a sampled-softmax variant that
    can improve rank loss.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.metrics</code>.{streaming_covariance,streaming_pearson_correlation}
    modified to return nan when they have seen less or equal to 1 unit of
    weight.</li>
<li>Adds time series models to contrib. See contrib/timeseries/README.md for
    details.</li>
<li>Adds FULLY_CONNECTED Op to tensorflow/lite/schema.fbs</li>
</ul>
<h2>Known Issues</h2>
<ul>
<li>Tensorflow_gpu compilation fails with Bazel 0.5.3.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixes <code>strides</code> and <code>begin</code> dtype mismatch when slicing using int64 Tensor
    index in python.</li>
<li>Improved convolution padding documentation.</li>
<li>Add a tag constant, gpu, to present graph with GPU support.</li>
<li><code>saved_model.utils</code> now support SparseTensors transparently.</li>
<li>A more efficient implementation of non-max suppression.</li>
<li>Add support for the shrinkage-type L2 to FtrlOptimizer in addition to the
    online L2 it already supports.</li>
<li>Fix negative variance in moments calculation.</li>
<li>Expand UniqueOp Benchmark Tests to cover more collision cases.</li>
<li>Improves stability of GCS filesystem on Mac.</li>
<li>Add time estimation to HloCostAnalysis.</li>
<li>Fixed the bug in Estimator that params in constructor was not a deepcopy of
    the user provided one. This bugs inadvertently enabled user to mutate the
    params after the creation of Estimator, leading to potentially undefined
    behavior.</li>
<li>Added None check for save_path in <code>saver.restore</code>.</li>
<li>Register devices under their legacy names in device_mgr to ease the
    transition to clusterspec-propagated configurations.</li>
<li>VectorExponential added to distributions.</li>
<li>Add a bitwise module with bitwise_and, bitwise_or, bitwise_xor, and invert
    functions.</li>
<li>Add fixed-grid ODE integration routines.</li>
<li>Allow passing bounds to ScipyOptimizerInterface.</li>
<li>Correctness fixes for fft_length parameter to <code>tf.spectral.rfft</code> &amp;
    <code>tf.spectral.irfft</code>.</li>
<li>Exported model signatures using the 'predict' method will no longer have
    their input and output keys silently ignored and rewritten to 'inputs' and
    'outputs'. If a model was exported with different names before 1.2, and is
    now served with tensorflow/serving, it will accept requests using 'inputs'
    and 'outputs'. Starting at 1.2, such a model will accept the keys specified
    during export. Therefore, inference requests using 'inputs' and 'outputs'
    may start to fail. To fix this, either update any inference clients to send
    requests with the actual input and output keys used by the trainer code, or
    conversely, update the trainer code to name the input and output Tensors
    'inputs' and 'outputs', respectively. Signatures using the 'classify' and
    'regress' methods are not affected by this change; they will continue to
    standardize their input and output keys as before.</li>
<li>Add in-memory caching to the Dataset API.</li>
<li>Set default end_of_sequence variable in datasets iterators to false.</li>
<li>[Performance] Increase performance of <code>tf.layers.conv2d</code> when setting
    use_bias=True by 2x by using nn.bias_add.</li>
<li>Update iOS examples to use CocoaPods, and moved to tensorflow/examples/ios.</li>
<li>Adds a family= attribute in <code>tf.summary</code> ops to allow controlling the tab
    name used in Tensorboard for organizing summaries.</li>
<li>When GPU is configured, do not require --config=cuda, instead, automatically
    build for GPU if this is requested in the configure script.</li>
<li>Fix incorrect sampling of small probabilities in CPU/GPU multinomial.</li>
<li>Add a list_devices() API on sessions to list devices within a cluster.
    Additionally, this change augment the ListDevices master API to support
    specifying a session.</li>
<li>Allow uses of over-parameterized separable convolution.</li>
<li>TensorForest multi-regression bug fix.</li>
<li>Framework now supports armv7, cocoapods.org now displays correct page.</li>
<li>Script to create iOS framework for CocoaPods.</li>
<li>Android releases of TensorFlow are now pushed to jcenter for easier
    integration into apps. See
    https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/tools/android/inference_interface/README.md
    for more details.</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg):<ul>
<li>Fixed a bug that prevented tfdbg from functioning with multi-GPU setups.</li>
<li>Fixed a bug that prevented tfdbg from working with
    <code>tf.Session.make_callable</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.2.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Updating markdown version required to &gt;= 2.6.8.</li>
<li>Support tensors as dropout rates again, by removing the min(max(..))</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.2.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Python 3.6 support on Windows.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.layers.conv3d_transpose</code> layer for spatio temporal deconvolution.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.Session.make_callable()</code>, which provides a lower overhead means of
    running a similar step multiple times.</li>
<li>Added libverbs-based RDMA support to contrib (courtesy @junshi15 from
    Yahoo).</li>
<li>Bring <code>tf.feature_column.*</code> into the API. Non-deprecated functionality from
    <code>tf.contrib.layers.*</code> is moved to <code>tf.feature_column.*</code> with cosmetic
    changes.</li>
<li><code>RNNCell</code> objects now subclass <code>tf.layers.Layer</code>. The strictness described
    in the TensorFlow 1.1 release is gone: The first time an RNNCell is used, it
    caches its scope. All future uses of the RNNCell will reuse variables from
    that same scope. This is a breaking change from the behavior of RNNCells in
    TensorFlow versions &lt;= 1.0.1. TensorFlow 1.1 had checks in place to ensure
    old code works correctly with the new semantics; this version allows more
    flexible uses of RNNCell but can lead to subtle errors if using code meant
    for TensorFlow &lt;= 1.0.1. For example, writing: <code>MultiRNNCell([lstm] * 5)</code>
    will now build a 5-layer LSTM stack where each layer shares the <strong>same</strong>
    parameters. To get 5 layers each with their own parameters, write:
    <code>MultiRNNCell([LSTMCell(...) for _ in range(5)])</code>. If at all unsure, first
    test your code with TF 1.1; ensure it raises no errors, and then upgrade to
    TF 1.2.</li>
<li>RNNCells' variable names have been renamed for consistency with Keras
    layers. Specifically, the previous variable names "weights" and "biases"
    have been changed to "kernel" and "bias", respectively. This may cause
    backward incompatibility with regard to your old checkpoints containing such
    RNN cells, in which case you can use the tool
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/contrib/rnn/python/tools/checkpoint_convert.py">checkpoint_convert script</a>
    to convert the variable names in your old checkpoints.</li>
<li>
<p>Many of the RNN functions and classes that were in the <code>tf.nn</code> namespace
    before the 1.0 release and which were moved to <code>tf.contrib.rnn</code> have now
    been moved back to the core namespace. This includes <code>RNNCell</code>, <code>LSTMCell</code>,
    <code>GRUCell</code>, and a number of other cells. These now reside in <code>tf.nn.rnn_cell</code>
    (with aliases in <code>tf.contrib.rnn</code> for backwards compatibility). The original
    <code>tf.nn.rnn</code> function is now <code>tf.nn.static_rnn</code>, and the bidirectional static
    and state saving static rnn functions are also now back in the <code>tf.nn</code>
    namespace.</p>
<p>Notable exceptions are the <code>EmbeddingWrapper</code>, <code>InputProjectionWrapper</code> and
<code>OutputProjectionWrapper</code>, which will slowly be moved to deprecation in
<code>tf.contrib.rnn</code>. These are inefficient wrappers that should often be
replaced by calling <code>embedding_lookup</code> or <code>layers.dense</code> as pre- or post-
processing of the rnn. For RNN decoding, this functionality has been
replaced with an alternative API in <code>tf.contrib.seq2seq</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Intel MKL Integration
    (https://software.intel.com/en-us/articles/tensorflow-optimizations-on-modern-intel-architecture).
    Intel developed a number of optimized deep learning primitives: In addition
    to matrix multiplication and convolution, these building blocks include:
    Direct batched convolution Pooling: maximum, minimum, average Normalization:
    LRN, batch normalization Activation: rectified linear unit (ReLU) Data
    manipulation: multi-dimensional transposition (conversion), split, concat,
    sum and scale.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>TensorForest Estimator now supports SavedModel export for serving.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Support client-provided ClusterSpec's and propagate them to all workers to
    enable the creation of dynamic TensorFlow clusters.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>TensorFlow C library now available for Windows.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>We released a new open-source version of TensorBoard.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/guide/saved_model_cli"><code>SavedModel CLI</code></a>
    tool available to inspect and execute MetaGraph in SavedModel</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Android releases of TensorFlow are now pushed to jcenter for easier
    integration into apps. See
    https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/tools/android/inference_interface/README.md
    for more details.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Deprecations</h2>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow 1.2 may be the last time we build with cuDNN 5.1. Starting with
    TensorFlow 1.3, we will try to build all our prebuilt binaries with cuDNN
    6.0. While we will try to keep our source code compatible with cuDNN 5.1, it
    will be best effort.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>org.tensorflow.contrib.android.TensorFlowInferenceInterface</code> now throws
    exceptions where possible and has simplified method signatures.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Changes to contrib APIs</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.util.create_example</code>.</li>
<li>Added bilinear interpolation to <code>tf.contrib.image</code>.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.contrib.stateless</code> for random ops with custom seed control.</li>
<li>MultivariateNormalFullCovariance added to contrib/distributions/</li>
<li>tensorflow/contrib/rnn undergoes RNN cell variable renaming for consistency
    with Keras layers. Specifically, the previous variable names "weights" and
    "biases" are changed to "kernel" and "bias", respectively. This may cause
    backward incompatibility with regard to your old checkpoints containing such
    RNN cells, in which case you can use the
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/blob/master/tensorflow/contrib/rnn/python/tools/checkpoint_convert.py">checkpoint_convert script</a>
    to convert the variable names in your old checkpoints.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.kernel_methods</code> module with Ops and estimators for primal
    (explicit) kernel methods in TensorFlow.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>In python, <code>Operation.get_attr</code> on type attributes returns the Python DType
    version of the type to match expected get_attr documentation rather than the
    protobuf enum.</li>
<li>tensorflow/contrib/rnn undergoes RNN cell variable renaming for consistency
    with Keras layers. Specifically, the previous variable names "weights" and
    "biases" are changed to "kernel" and "bias", respectively.</li>
<li>Changed MIN_SDK version to 8.0 when building iOS libraries.</li>
<li>Fixed LIBXSMM integration.</li>
<li>Make decode_jpeg/decode_png/decode_gif handle all formats, since users
    frequently try to decode an image as the wrong type.</li>
<li>Improve implicit broadcasting lowering.</li>
<li>Improving stability of GCS/BigQuery clients by a faster retrying of stale
    transmissions.</li>
<li>Remove OpKernelConstruction::op_def() as part of minimizing proto
    dependencies.</li>
<li>VectorLaplaceDiag distribution added.</li>
<li>Android demo no longer requires libtensorflow_demo.so to run
    (libtensorflow_inference.so still required)</li>
<li>Added <code>categorical_column_with_vocabulary_file</code>.</li>
<li>Introduce ops for batching/unbatching tensors across Session::Run() calls.</li>
<li>Add tf.log_sigmoid(x) = tf.log(tf.sigmoid(x)) = -tf.nn.softplus(-x).</li>
<li>Changed hooks lists to immutable tuples, and now allow any iterable for the
    associated arguments.</li>
<li>Introduce TFDecorator.</li>
<li>Added an Mfcc op for speech feature generation.</li>
<li>Improved DirectSession::Run() overhead and error checking. Feeding a value
    of the wrong type will now synchronously raise an INVALID_ARGUMENT error
    instead of asynchronously raising an INTERNAL error. Code that depends on
    the (undefined) behavior when feeding a tensor of the wrong type may need to
    be updated.</li>
<li>Added unreduced NONE, and reduced MEAN options for losses. Removed
    "WEIGHTED_" prefix from other Reduction constants.</li>
<li>assertAllClose now handles dicts.</li>
<li>Added Gmock matcher for HloInstructions.</li>
<li>Add var name to errors on variable restore.</li>
<li>Added an AudioSpectrogram op for audio feature generation.</li>
<li>Added <code>reduction</code> arg to losses.</li>
<li><code>tf.placeholder</code> can represent scalar shapes and partially known.</li>
<li>Remove estimator_spec(mode) argument.</li>
<li>Added an AudioSpectrogram op for audio feature generation.</li>
<li>TensorBoard disables all runs by default if there are more than 40 runs.</li>
<li>Removed old doc generator code.</li>
<li>GCS file system integration now supports domain buckets, e.g
    gs://bucket.domain.com/path.</li>
<li>Add <code>tf.summary.text</code> for outputting text to TensorBoard.</li>
<li>The "run" command of tfdbg's command-line interface now supports filtering
    of tensors by node name, op type and tensor dtype.</li>
<li><code>tf.string_to_number</code> now supports int64 and float64 outputs.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 1.1.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added Java API support for Windows.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.spectral</code> module. Moved existing FFT ops to <code>tf.spectral</code> while
    keeping an alias in the old location (<code>tf.*</code>).</li>
<li>Added 1D, 2D and 3D Fourier transform ops for real signals to <code>tf.spectral</code>.</li>
<li>Added a <code>tf.bincount</code> function.</li>
<li>Added Keras 2 API to contrib.</li>
<li>Added a new lightweight queue-like object - <code>RecordInput</code>.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.image.compose_transforms</code> function.</li>
<li>Bring <code>tf.estimator.*</code> into the API. Non-deprecated functionality from
    <code>tf.contrib.learn.Estimator</code> is moved to <code>tf.estimator.Estimator</code> with
    cosmetic changes.</li>
<li>Docker images: TF images on gcr.io and Docker Hub are upgraded to
    ubuntu:16.04.</li>
<li>Added the following features to TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg):<ul>
<li>Ability to inspect Python source file against TF ops and tensors
    (command <code>print_source</code> / <code>ps</code>)</li>
<li>New navigation bar in Curses-based UI</li>
<li>NodeStepper (command <code>invoke_stepper</code>) now uses intermediate tensor
    dumps. It also uses <code>TensorHandles</code> as direct feeds during successive
    <code>cont</code> calls for improved performance and reduced memory consumption.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Initial release of installation guides for Java, C, and Go.</li>
<li>Added Text Dashboard to TensorBoard.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Deprecations</h2>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow 1.1.0 will be the last time we release a binary with Mac GPU
    support. Going forward, we will stop testing on Mac GPU systems. We continue
    to welcome patches that maintain Mac GPU support, and we will try to keep
    the Mac GPU build working.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Changes to contrib APIs</h2>
<ul>
<li>The behavior of RNNCells is now stricter due to the transition towards
    making RNNCells act more like Keras layers.<ul>
<li>If an RNNCell is used twice in two different variable scopes, an error
    is raised describing how to avoid this behavior.</li>
<li>If an RNNCell is used in a variable scope with existing conflicting
    variables, an error is raised showing that the RNNCell must be
    constructed with argument <code>reuse=True</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Deprecated contrib/distributions <code>pmf</code>, <code>pdf</code>, <code>log_pmf</code>, <code>log_pdf</code>.</li>
<li>Moved <code>bayesflow.special_math</code> to distributions.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.tensor_forest.python.tensor_forest.RandomForestDeviceAssigner</code>
    removed.</li>
<li>Changed some MVN classes and parameters:<ul>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalFull</code> replaced by
    <code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalTriL</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalCholesky</code> replaced by
    <code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalTriL</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalDiagWithSoftplusStDev</code>
    replaced by
    <code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalDiagWithSoftplusScale</code></li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalDiag</code> arguments changed from
    <code>mu</code>, <code>diag_stddev</code> to <code>log</code>, <code>scale_diag</code>.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalDiagPlusVDVT</code> removed.</li>
<li><code>tf.contrib.distributions.MultivariateNormalDiagPlusLowRank</code> added.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Java: Support for loading models exported using the SavedModel API (courtesy
    @EronWright).</li>
<li>Go: Added support for incremental graph execution.</li>
<li>Fix a bug in the WALS solver when single-threaded.</li>
<li>Added support for integer sparse feature values in
    <code>tf.contrib.layers.sparse_column_with_keys</code>.</li>
<li>Fixed <code>tf.set_random_seed(0)</code> to be deterministic for all ops.</li>
<li>Stability improvements for the GCS file system support.</li>
<li>Improved TensorForest performance.</li>
<li>Added support for multiple filename globs in <code>tf.matching_files</code>.</li>
<li><code>LogMessage</code> now includes a timestamp as beginning of a message.</li>
<li>Added MultiBox person detector example standalone binary.</li>
<li>Android demo: Makefile build functionality added to build.gradle to fully
    support building TensorFlow demo in Android on Windows.</li>
<li>Android demo: read MultiBox priors from txt file rather than protobuf.</li>
<li>Added colocation constraints to <code>StagingArea</code>.</li>
<li><code>sparse_matmul_op</code> reenabled for Android builds.</li>
<li>Restrict weights rank to be the same as the broadcast target, to avoid
    ambiguity on broadcast rules.</li>
<li>Upgraded libxsmm to 1.7.1 and applied other changes for performance and
    memory usage.</li>
<li>Fixed bfloat16 integration of LIBXSMM sparse mat-mul.</li>
<li>Improved performance and reduce memory usage by allowing ops to forward
    input buffers to output buffers and perform computations in-place.</li>
<li>Improved the performance of CPU assignment for strings.</li>
<li>Speed up matrix * vector multiplication and matrix * matrix with unknown
    shapes.</li>
<li>C API: Graph imports now support input remapping, control dependencies, and
    returning imported nodes (see <code>TF_GraphImportGraphDefWithReturnOutputs()</code>)</li>
<li>Multiple C++ API updates.</li>
<li>Multiple TensorBoard updates including:<ul>
<li>Users can now view image summaries at various sampled steps (instead of
    just the last step).</li>
<li>Bugs involving switching runs as well as the image dashboard are fixed.</li>
<li>Removed data download links from TensorBoard.</li>
<li>TensorBoard uses a relative data directory, for easier embedding.</li>
<li>TensorBoard automatically ignores outliers for domain calculation, and
    formats proportional values consistently.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Multiple tfdbg bug fixes:<ul>
<li>Fixed Windows compatibility issues.</li>
<li>Command history now persists across runs.</li>
<li>Bug fix in graph validation related to <code>tf.while_loops</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Java Maven fixes for bugs with Windows installation.</li>
<li>Backport fixes and improvements from external keras.</li>
<li>Keras config file handling fix.</li>
</ul>
