<h1>Release 1.0.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Change GraphConstructor to not increase the version when importing, but
    instead take the min of all versions.</li>
<li>Google Cloud Storage fixes.</li>
<li>Removed <code>tf.core</code> and <code>tf.python</code> modules from the API. These were never
    intended to be exposed. Please use the same objects through top-level <code>tf</code>
    module instead.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 1.0.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>XLA (experimental): initial release of
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/versions/master/experimental/xla/">XLA</a>, a
    domain-specific compiler for TensorFlow graphs, that targets CPUs and GPUs.</li>
<li>TensorFlow Debugger (tfdbg): command-line interface and API.</li>
<li>New python 3 docker images added.</li>
<li>Made pip packages pypi compliant. TensorFlow can now be installed by <code>pip
    install tensorflow</code> command.</li>
<li>Several python API calls have been changed to resemble NumPy more closely.</li>
<li>Android: person detection + tracking demo implementing Scalable Object
    Detection using Deep Neural Networks.</li>
<li>New (experimental)
    <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/master/tensorflow/java">Java API</a>.</li>
<li>Add new Android image stylization demo based on "A Learned Representation
    For Artistic Style", and add YOLO object detector support.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<p>To help you upgrade your existing TensorFlow Python code to match the API
changes below, we have prepared a
<a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tree/master/tensorflow/tools/compatibility">conversion script</a>.
* TensorFlow/models have been moved to a separate github repository. * Division
and modulus operators (/, //, %) now match Python (flooring) semantics. This
applies to <code>tf.div</code> and <code>tf.mod</code> as well. To obtain forced integer truncation
based behaviors you can use <code>tf.truncatediv</code> and <code>tf.truncatemod</code>. *
<code>tf.divide()</code> is now the recommended division function. <code>tf.div()</code> will remain,
but its semantics do not respond to Python 3 or <code>from future</code> mechanisms. *
tf.reverse() now takes indices of axes to be reversed. E.g. <code>tf.reverse(a,
[True, False, True])</code> must now be written as <code>tf.reverse(a, [0, 2])</code>.
<code>tf.reverse_v2()</code> will remain until 1.0 final. * <code>tf.mul</code>, <code>tf.sub</code> and <code>tf.neg</code>
are deprecated in favor of <code>tf.multiply</code>, <code>tf.subtract</code> and <code>tf.negative</code>. *
<code>tf.pack</code> and <code>tf.unpack</code> are deprecated in favor of <code>tf.stack</code> and
<code>tf.unstack</code>. * <code>TensorArray.pack</code> and <code>TensorArray.unpack</code> are getting
deprecated in favor of <code>TensorArray.stack</code> and <code>TensorArray.unstack</code>. * The
following Python functions have had their arguments changed to use <code>axis</code> when
referring to specific dimensions. We have kept the old keyword arguments for
compatibility currently, but we will be removing them well before the final 1.0.
* <code>tf.argmax</code>: <code>dimension</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.argmin</code>: <code>dimension</code> becomes
<code>axis</code> * <code>tf.count_nonzero</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.expand_dims</code>: <code>dim</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_all</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code>
becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_any</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.reduce_join</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_logsumexp</code>:
<code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_max</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code>
becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_mean</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.reduce_min</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_prod</code>:
<code>reduction_indices</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reduce_sum</code>: <code>reduction_indices</code>
becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.reverse_sequence</code>: <code>batch_dim</code> becomes <code>batch_axis</code>,
<code>seq_dim</code> becomes <code>seq_axis</code> * <code>tf.sparse_concat</code>: <code>concat_dim</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.sparse_reduce_sum</code>: <code>reduction_axes</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.sparse_reduce_sum_sparse</code>: <code>reduction_axes</code> becomes <code>axis</code> *
<code>tf.sparse_split</code>: <code>split_dim</code> becomes <code>axis</code> * <code>tf.listdiff</code> has been renamed
to <code>tf.setdiff1d</code> to match NumPy naming. * <code>tf.inv</code> has been renamed to be
<code>tf.reciprocal</code> (component-wise reciprocal) to avoid confusion with <code>np.inv</code>
which is matrix inversion * tf.round now uses banker's rounding (round to even)
semantics to match NumPy. * <code>tf.split</code> now takes arguments in a reversed order
and with different keywords. In particular, we now match NumPy order as
<code>tf.split(value, num_or_size_splits, axis)</code>. * <code>tf.sparse_split</code> now takes
arguments in reversed order and with different keywords. In particular we now
match NumPy order as <code>tf.sparse_split(sp_input, num_split, axis)</code>. NOTE: we have
temporarily made <code>tf.sparse_split</code> require keyword arguments. * <code>tf.concat</code> now
takes arguments in reversed order and with different keywords. In particular we
now match NumPy order as <code>tf.concat(values, axis, name)</code>. *
<code>tf.image.decode_jpeg</code> by default uses the faster DCT method, sacrificing a
little fidelity for improved speed. One can revert to the old behavior by
specifying the attribute <code>dct_method='INTEGER_ACCURATE'</code>. * <code>tf.complex_abs</code> has
been removed from the Python interface. <code>tf.abs</code> supports complex tensors and
should be used instead. * In the C++ API (in tensorflow/cc), Input, Output, etc.
have moved from the tensorflow::ops namespace to tensorflow. *
Template.<code>var_scope</code> property renamed to <code>.variable_scope</code> *
SyncReplicasOptimizer is removed and SyncReplicasOptimizerV2 renamed to
SyncReplicasOptimizer. * <code>tf.zeros_initializer()</code> and <code>tf.ones_initializer()</code>
now return a callable that must be called with initializer arguments, in your
code replace <code>tf.zeros_initializer</code> with <code>tf.zeros_initializer()</code>. *
<code>SparseTensor.shape</code> has been renamed to <code>SparseTensor.dense_shape</code>. Same for
<code>SparseTensorValue.shape</code>. * Replace tf.scalar_summary, tf.histogram_summary,
tf.audio_summary, tf.image_summary with tf.summary.scalar, tf.summary.histogram,
tf.summary.audio, tf.summary.image, respectively. The new summary ops take name
rather than tag as their first argument, meaning summary ops now respect
TensorFlow name scopes. * Replace tf.train.SummaryWriter and
tf.train.SummaryWriterCache with tf.summary.FileWriter and
tf.summary.FileWriterCache. * Removes RegisterShape from public API. Use C++
shape function registration instead. * Deprecated <code>_ref</code> dtypes from the python
API. * In the C++ API (in tensorflow/cc), Input, Output, etc. have moved from
the tensorflow::ops namespace to tensorflow. * Change arg order for
<code>{softmax,sparse_softmax,sigmoid}_cross_entropy_with_logits</code> to be (labels,
predictions), and force use of named args. * tf.nn.rnn_cell.<em> and most functions
in tf.nn.rnn.</em> (with the exception of dynamic_rnn and raw_rnn) are temporarily
in tf.contrib.rnn. They will be moved back into core for TF 1.2. *
<code>tf.nn.sampled_softmax_loss</code> and <code>tf.nn.nce_loss</code> have both changed their API
such that you need to switch the <code>inputs, labels</code> to <code>labels, inputs</code>
parameters. * The shape keyword argument of the <code>SparseTensor</code> constructor
changes its name to <code>dense_shape</code> between Tensorflow 0.12 and Tensorflow 1.0.</p>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Numerous C++ API updates.</li>
<li>New op: <code>parallel_stack</code>.</li>
<li>Introducing common tf io compression options constants for
    RecordReader/RecordWriter.</li>
<li>Add <code>sparse_column_with_vocabulary_file</code>, to specify a feature column that
    transform string features to IDs, where the mapping is defined by a
    vocabulary file.</li>
<li>Added <code>index_to_string_table</code> which returns a lookup table that maps indices
    to strings.</li>
<li>Add <code>string_to_index_table</code>, which returns a lookup table that matches
    strings to indices.</li>
<li>Add a <code>ParallelForWithWorkerId</code> function.</li>
<li>Add <code>string_to_index_table</code>, which returns a lookup table that matches
    strings to indices.</li>
<li>Support restore session from checkpoint files in v2 in
    <code>contrib/session_bundle</code>.</li>
<li>Added a tf.contrib.image.rotate function for arbitrary angles.</li>
<li>Added <code>tf.contrib.framework.filter_variables</code> as a convenience function to
    filter lists of variables based on regular expressions.</li>
<li><code>make_template()</code> takes an optional <code>custom_getter_ param</code>.</li>
<li>Added comment about how existing directories are handled by
    <code>recursive_create_dir</code>.</li>
<li>Added an op for QR factorizations.</li>
<li>Divides and mods in Python API now use flooring (Python) semantics.</li>
<li>Android: pre-built libs are now built nightly.</li>
<li>Android: cmake/gradle build for TensorFlow Inference library under
    <code>contrib/android/cmake</code></li>
<li>Android: Much more robust Session initialization code.</li>
<li>Android: TF stats now exposed directly in demo and log when debug mode is
    active</li>
<li>Android: new/better README.md documentation</li>
<li>saved_model is available as <code>tf.saved_model</code>.</li>
<li>Empty op is now stateful.</li>
<li>Improve speed of scatter_update on the cpu for ASSIGN operations.</li>
<li>Change <code>reduce_join</code> to treat <code>reduction_indices</code> in the same way as other
    <code>reduce_</code> ops.</li>
<li>Move <code>TensorForestEstimator</code> to <code>contrib/tensor_forest</code>.</li>
<li>Enable compiler optimizations by default and allow configuration in
    configure.</li>
<li><code>tf.divide</code> now honors the name field.</li>
<li>Make metrics weight broadcasting more strict.</li>
<li>Add new queue-like <code>StagingArea</code> and new ops: <code>stage</code> and <code>unstage</code>.</li>
<li>Enable inplace update ops for strings on CPU. Speed up string concat.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.12.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>TensorFlow now builds and runs on Microsoft Windows (tested on Windows 10,
    Windows 7, and Windows Server 2016). Supported languages include Python (via
    a pip package) and C++. CUDA 8.0 and cuDNN 5.1 are supported for GPU
    acceleration. Known limitations include: It is not currently possible to
    load a custom op library. The GCS and HDFS file systems are not currently
    supported. The following ops are not currently implemented: Dequantize,
    QuantizeAndDequantize, QuantizedAvgPool,
    QuantizedBatchNomWithGlobalNormalization, QuantizedBiasAdd, QuantizedConcat,
    QuantizedConv2D, QuantizedMatmul, QuantizedMaxPool,
    QuantizeDownAndShrinkRange, QuantizedRelu, QuantizedRelu6, QuantizedReshape,
    QuantizeV2, RequantizationRange, and Requantize.</li>
<li>Go: Experimental API in Go to create and execute graphs
    (https://godoc.org/github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/tensorflow/go)</li>
<li>New checkpoint format becomes the default in <code>tf.train.Saver</code>. Old V1
    checkpoints continue to be readable; controlled by the <code>write_version</code>
    argument, <code>tf.train.Saver</code> now by default writes out in the new V2 format.
    It significantly reduces the peak memory required and latency incurred
    during restore.</li>
<li>Added a new library for library of matrix-free (iterative) solvers for
    linear equations, linear least-squares, eigenvalues and singular values in
    tensorflow/contrib/solvers. Initial version has lanczos bidiagonalization,
    conjugate gradients and CGLS.</li>
<li>Added gradients for <code>matrix_solve_ls</code> and <code>self_adjoint_eig</code>.</li>
<li>Large cleanup to add second order gradient for ops with C++ gradients and
    improve existing gradients such that most ops can now be differentiated
    multiple times.</li>
<li>Added a solver for ordinary differential equations,
    <code>tf.contrib.integrate.odeint</code>.</li>
<li>New contrib module for tensors with named axes, <code>tf.contrib.labeled_tensor</code>.</li>
<li>Visualization of embeddings in TensorBoard.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>BusAdjacency</code> enum replaced with a protocol buffer <code>DeviceLocality</code>. PCI
    bus indexing now starts from 1 instead of 0, and <code>bus_id==0</code> is used where
    previously <code>BUS_ANY</code> was used.</li>
<li><code>Env::FileExists</code> and <code>FileSystem::FileExists</code> now return a
    tensorflow::Status instead of a bool. Any callers to this function can be
    converted to a bool by adding .ok() to the call.</li>
<li>The C API type <code>TF_SessionWithGraph</code> has been renamed to <code>TF_Session</code>,
    indicating its preferred use in language bindings for TensorFlow. What was
    previously <code>TF_Session</code> has been renamed to <code>TF_DeprecatedSession</code>.</li>
<li>Renamed <code>TF_Port</code> to <code>TF_Output</code> in the C API.</li>
<li>Removes RegisterShape from public API. Use C++ shape function registration
    instead. indexing now starts from 1 instead of 0, and <code>bus_id==0</code> is used
    where previously <code>BUS_ANY</code> was used.</li>
<li>Most RNN cells and RNN functions now use different variable scopes to be
    consistent with layers (<code>tf.contrib.layers</code>). This means old checkpoints
    written using this code will not load after this change without providing
    <code>Saver</code> a list of variable renames. Examples of variable scope changes
    include <code>RNN</code> -&gt; <code>rnn</code> in <code>tf.nn.rnn</code>, <code>tf.nn.dynamic_rnn</code> and moving from
    <code>Linear/Matrix</code> -&gt; <code>weights</code> and <code>Linear/Bias</code> -&gt; <code>biases</code> in most RNN
    cells.</li>
<li>Deprecated tf.select op. tf.where should be used instead.</li>
<li><code>SparseTensor.shape</code> has been renamed to <code>SparseTensor.dense_shape</code>. Same
    for <code>SparseTensorValue.shape</code>.</li>
<li><code>Env::FileExists</code> and <code>FileSystem::FileExists</code> now return a
    <code>tensorflow::Status</code> instead of a bool. Any callers to this function can be
    converted to a bool by adding <code>.ok()</code> to the call.</li>
<li>C API: Type <code>TF_SessionWithGraph</code> has been renamed to <code>TF_Session</code>,
    indicating its preferred use in language bindings for TensorFlow. What was
    previously <code>TF_Session</code> has been renamed to <code>TF_DeprecatedSession</code>.</li>
<li>C API: Renamed <code>TF_Port</code> to <code>TF_Output</code>.</li>
<li>C API: The caller retains ownership of <code>TF_Tensor</code> objects provided to
    <code>TF_Run</code>, <code>TF_SessionRun</code>, <code>TF_SetAttrTensor</code> etc.</li>
<li>Renamed <code>tf.image.per_image_whitening()</code> to
    <code>tf.image.per_image_standardization()</code></li>
<li>Move Summary protobuf constructors to <code>tf.summary</code> submodule.</li>
<li>Deprecate <code>histogram_summary</code>, <code>audio_summary</code>, <code>scalar_summary</code>,
    <code>image_summary</code>, <code>merge_summary</code>, and <code>merge_all_summaries</code>.</li>
<li>Combined <code>batch_*</code> and regular version of linear algebra and FFT ops. The
    regular op now handles batches as well. All <code>batch_*</code> Python interfaces were
    removed.</li>
<li><code>tf.all_variables</code>, <code>tf.VARIABLES</code> and <code>tf.initialize_all_variables</code> renamed
    to <code>tf.global_variables</code>, <code>tf.GLOBAL_VARIABLES</code> and
    <code>tf.global_variables_initializer</code> respectively.</li>
<li><code>tf.zeros_initializer()</code> and <code>tf.ones_initializer()</code> now return a callable
    that must be called with initializer arguments, in your code replace
    <code>tf.zeros_initializer</code> with <code>tf.zeros_initializer()</code></li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Use threadsafe version of <code>lgamma</code> function.</li>
<li>Fix <code>tf.sqrt</code> handling of negative arguments.</li>
<li>Fixed bug causing incorrect number of threads to be used for multi-threaded
    benchmarks.</li>
<li>Performance optimizations for <code>batch_matmul</code> on multi-core CPUs.</li>
<li>Improve trace, <code>matrix_set_diag</code>, <code>matrix_diag_part</code> and their gradients to
    work for rectangular matrices.</li>
<li>Support for SVD of complex valued matrices.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.11.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>CUDA 8 support.</li>
<li>cuDNN 5 support.</li>
<li>HDFS Support.</li>
<li>Adds Fused LSTM support via cuDNN 5 in <code>tensorflow/contrib/cudnn_rnn</code>.</li>
<li>Improved support for NumPy style basic slicing including non-1 strides,
    ellipses, newaxis, and negative indices. For example complicated expressions
    like <code>foo[1, 2:4, tf.newaxis, ..., :-3:-1, :]</code> are now supported. In
    addition we have preliminary (non-broadcasting) support for sliced
    assignment to variables. In particular one can write
    <code>var[1:3].assign([1,11,111])</code>.</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>tf.op_scope</code> and <code>tf.variable_op_scope</code> in favor of a unified
    <code>tf.name_scope</code> and <code>tf.variable_scope</code>. The new argument order of
    <code>tf.variable_scope</code> is incompatible with previous versions.</li>
<li>Introducing <code>core/util/tensor_bundle</code> module: a module to efficiently
    serialize/deserialize tensors to disk. Will be used in TF's new checkpoint
    format.</li>
<li>Added tf.svd for computing the singular value decomposition (SVD) of dense
    matrices or batches of matrices (CPU only).</li>
<li>Added gradients for eigenvalues and eigenvectors computed using
    <code>self_adjoint_eig</code> or <code>self_adjoint_eigvals</code>.</li>
<li>Eliminated <code>batch_*</code> methods for most linear algebra and FFT ops and
    promoted the non-batch version of the ops to handle batches of matrices.</li>
<li>Tracing/timeline support for distributed runtime (no GPU profiler yet).</li>
<li>C API gives access to inferred shapes with <code>TF_GraphGetTensorNumDims</code> and
    <code>TF_GraphGetTensorShape</code>.</li>
<li>Shape functions for core ops have moved to C++ via
    <code>REGISTER_OP(...).SetShapeFn(...)</code>. Python shape inference RegisterShape
    calls use the C++ shape functions with <code>common_shapes.call_cpp_shape_fn</code>. A
    future release will remove <code>RegisterShape</code> from python.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Documentation now includes operator overloads on Tensor and Variable.</li>
<li><code>tensorflow.__git_version__</code> now allows users to identify the version of the
    code that TensorFlow was compiled with. We also have
    <code>tensorflow.__git_compiler__</code> which identifies the compiler used to compile
    TensorFlow's core.</li>
<li>Improved multi-threaded performance of <code>batch_matmul</code>.</li>
<li>LSTMCell, BasicLSTMCell, and MultiRNNCell constructors now default to
    <code>state_is_tuple=True</code>. For a quick fix while transitioning to the new
    default, simply pass the argument <code>state_is_tuple=False</code>.</li>
<li>DeviceFactory's AddDevices and CreateDevices functions now return a Status
    instead of void.</li>
<li>Int32 elements of list(type) arguments are no longer placed in host memory
    by default. If necessary, a list(type) argument to a kernel can be placed in
    host memory using a HostMemory annotation.</li>
<li><code>uniform_unit_scaling_initializer()</code> no longer takes a <code>full_shape</code> arg,
    instead relying on the partition info passed to the initializer function
    when it's called.</li>
<li>The NodeDef protocol message is now defined in its own file <code>node_def.proto</code>
    <code>instead of graph.proto</code>.</li>
<li><code>ops.NoGradient</code> was renamed <code>ops.NotDifferentiable</code>. <code>ops.NoGradient</code> will
    be removed soon.</li>
<li><code>dot.h</code> / DotGraph was removed (it was an early analysis tool prior to
    TensorBoard, no longer that useful). It remains in history should someone
    find the code useful.</li>
<li>re2 / regexp.h was removed from being a public interface of TF. Should users
    need regular expressions, they should depend on the RE2 library directly
    rather than via TensorFlow.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.10.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added support for C++ shape inference</li>
<li>Added graph-construction C API</li>
<li>Major revision to the graph-construction C++ API</li>
<li>Support makefile build for iOS</li>
<li>Added Mac GPU support</li>

<li>Added k-Means clustering and WALS matrix factorization</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Allow gradient computation for scalar values.</li>
<li>Performance improvements for gRPC</li>
<li>Improved support for fp16</li>
<li>New high-level ops in tf.contrib. {layers,metrics}</li>
<li>New features for TensorBoard, such as shape display, exponential smoothing</li>
<li>Faster and more stable Google Cloud Storage (GCS) filesystem support</li>
<li>Support for zlib compression and decompression for TFRecordReader and
    TFRecordWriter</li>
<li>Support for reading (animated) GIFs</li>
<li>Improved support for SparseTensor</li>
<li>Added support for more probability distributions (Dirichlet, Beta,
    Bernoulli, etc.)</li>
<li>Added Python interfaces to reset resource containers.</li>
<li>Many bugfixes and performance improvements</li>
<li>Many documentation fixes</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.9.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Python 3.5 support and binaries</li>
<li>Added iOS support</li>
<li>Added support for processing on GPUs on MacOS</li>
<li>Added makefile for better cross-platform build support (C API only)</li>
<li>fp16 support and improved complex128 support for many ops</li>
<li>Higher level functionality in contrib. {layers,losses,metrics,learn}</li>
<li>More features to Tensorboard</li>
<li>Improved support for string embedding and sparse features</li>
<li>The RNN api is finally "official" (see, e.g., <code>tf.nn.dynamic_rnn</code>,
    <code>tf.nn.rnn</code>, and the classes in <code>tf.nn.rnn_cell</code>).</li>
<li>TensorBoard now has an Audio Dashboard, with associated audio summaries.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Turned on CuDNN Autotune.</li>
<li>Added support for using third-party Python optimization algorithms
    (contrib.opt).</li>
<li>Google Cloud Storage filesystem support.</li>
<li>HDF5 support</li>
<li>Add support for 3d convolutions and pooling.</li>
<li>Update gRPC release to 0.14.</li>
<li>Eigen version upgrade.</li>
<li>Switch to eigen thread pool</li>
<li><code>tf.nn.moments()</code> now accepts a <code>shift</code> argument. Shifting by a good
    estimate of the mean improves numerical stability. Also changes the behavior
    of the <code>shift</code> argument to <code>tf.nn.sufficient_statistics()</code>.</li>
<li>Performance improvements</li>
<li>Many bugfixes</li>
<li>Many documentation fixes</li>
<li>TensorBoard fixes: graphs with only one data point, Nan values, reload
    button and auto-reload, tooltips in scalar charts, run filtering, stable
    colors</li>
<li>Tensorboard graph visualizer now supports run metadata. Clicking on nodes
    while viewing a stats for a particular run will show runtime statistics,
    such as memory or compute usage. Unused nodes will be faded out.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.8.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added a distributed runtime using GRPC</li>
<li>Move skflow to <code>contrib/learn</code></li>
<li>Better linear optimizer in <code>contrib/linear_optimizer</code></li>
<li>Random forest implementation in <code>contrib/tensor_forest</code></li>
<li>CTC loss and decoders in <code>contrib/ctc</code></li>
<li>Basic support for <code>half</code> data type</li>
<li>Better support for loading user ops (see examples in <code>contrib/</code>)</li>
<li>Allow use of (non-blocking) Eigen threadpool with
    <code>TENSORFLOW_USE_EIGEN_THREADPOOL</code> define</li>
<li>Add an extension mechanism for adding network file system support</li>
<li>TensorBoard displays metadata stats (running time, memory usage and device
    used) and tensor shapes</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Utility for inspecting checkpoints</li>
<li>Basic tracing and timeline support</li>
<li>Allow building against cuDNN 5 (not incl. RNN/LSTM support)</li>
<li>Added instructions and binaries for ProtoBuf library with fast serialization
    and without 64MB limit</li>
<li>Added special functions</li>
<li><code>bool</code>-strictness: Tensors have to be explicitly compared to <code>None</code></li>
<li>Shape strictness: all fed values must have a shape that is compatible with
    the tensor they are replacing</li>
<li>Exposed <code>tf.while_loop</code> (deprecated <code>control_flow_ops.While</code>)</li>
<li>run() now takes RunOptions and RunMetadata, which enable timing stats</li>
<li>Fixed lots of potential overflow problems in op kernels</li>
<li>Various performance improvements, especially for RNNs and convolutions</li>
<li>Many bugfixes</li>
<li>Nightly builds, tutorial tests, many test improvements</li>
<li>New examples: transfer learning and deepdream ipython notebook</li>
<li>Added tutorials, many documentation fixes.</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.7.1</h1>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added gfile.Open and gfile.Copy, used by input_data.py.</li>
<li>Fixed Saver bug when MakeDirs tried to create empty directory.</li>
<li>GPU Pip wheels are built with cuda 7.5 and cudnn-v4, making them required
    for the binary releases. Lower versions of cuda/cudnn can be supported by
    installing from sources and setting the options during ./configure</li>
<li>Fix dataset encoding example for Python3 (@danijar)</li>
<li>Fix PIP installation by not packaging protobuf as part of wheel, require
    protobuf 3.0.0b2.</li>
<li>Fix Mac pip installation of numpy by requiring pip &gt;= 1.10.1.</li>
<li>Improvements and fixes to Docker image.</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 0.7.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Allow using any installed Cuda &gt;= 7.0 and cuDNN &gt;= R2, and add support for
    cuDNN R4</li>
<li>Added a <code>contrib/</code> directory for unsupported or experimental features,
    including higher level <code>layers</code> module</li>
<li>Added an easy way to add and dynamically load user-defined ops</li>
<li>Built out a good suite of tests, things should break less!</li>
<li>Added <code>MetaGraphDef</code> which makes it easier to save graphs with metadata</li>
<li>Added assignments for "Deep Learning with TensorFlow" udacity course</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes and Other Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added a versioning framework for <code>GraphDef</code>s to ensure compatibility</li>
<li>Enforced Python 3 compatibility</li>
<li>Internal changes now show up as sensibly separated commits</li>
<li>Open-sourced the doc generator</li>
<li>Un-fork Eigen</li>
<li>Simplified the <code>BUILD</code> files and cleaned up C++ headers</li>
<li>TensorFlow can now be used as a submodule in another bazel build</li>
<li>New ops (e.g., <code>*fft</code>, <code>*_matrix_solve</code>)</li>
<li>Support for more data types in many ops</li>
<li>Performance improvements</li>
<li>Various bugfixes</li>
<li>Documentation fixes and improvements</li>
</ul>
<h2>Breaking Changes to the API</h2>
<ul>
<li><code>AdjustContrast</code> kernel deprecated, new kernel <code>AdjustContrastv2</code> takes and
    outputs float only. <code>adjust_contrast</code> now takes all data types.</li>
<li><code>adjust_brightness</code>'s <code>delta</code> argument is now always assumed to be in
    <code>[0,1]</code> (as is the norm for images in floating point formats), independent
    of the data type of the input image.</li>
<li>The image processing ops do not take <code>min</code> and <code>max</code> inputs any more,
    casting safety is handled by <code>saturate_cast</code>, which makes sure over- and
    underflows are handled before casting to data types with smaller ranges.</li>
<li>For C++ API users: <code>IsLegacyScalar</code> and <code>IsLegacyVector</code> are now gone from
    <code>TensorShapeUtils</code> since TensorFlow is scalar strict within Google (for
    example, the shape argument to <code>tf.reshape</code> can't be a scalar anymore). The
    open source release was already scalar strict, so outside Google <code>IsScalar</code>
    and <code>IsVector</code> are exact replacements.</li>
<li>The following files are being removed from <code>tensorflow/core/public/</code>:<ul>
<li><code>env.h</code> -&gt; <code>../platform/env.h</code></li>
<li><code>status.h</code> -&gt; <code>../lib/core/status.h</code></li>
<li><code>tensor.h</code> -&gt; <code>../framework/tensor.h</code></li>
<li><code>tensor_shape.h</code> -&gt; <code>../framework/tensor_shape.h</code></li>
<li><code>partial_tensor_shape.h</code> -&gt; <code>../framework/partial_tensor_shape.h</code></li>
<li><code>tensorflow_server.h</code> deleted</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>For C++ API users: <code>TensorShape::ShortDebugString</code> has been renamed to
    <code>DebugString</code>, and the previous <code>DebugString</code> behavior is gone (it was
    needlessly verbose and produced a confusing empty string for scalars).</li>
<li><code>GraphOptions.skip_common_subexpression_elimination</code> has been removed. All
    graph optimizer options are now specified via
    <code>GraphOptions.OptimizerOptions</code>.</li>
<li><code>ASSERT_OK</code> / <code>EXPECT_OK</code> macros conflicted with external projects, so they
    were renamed <code>TF_ASSERT_OK</code>, <code>TF_EXPECT_OK</code>. The existing macros are
    currently maintained for short-term compatibility but will be removed.</li>
<li>The non-public <code>nn.rnn</code> and the various <code>nn.seq2seq</code> methods now return just
    the final state instead of the list of all states.</li>
<li><code>tf.scatter_update</code> now no longer guarantees that lexicographically largest
    index be used for update when duplicate entries exist.</li>
<li><code>tf.image.random_crop(image, [height, width])</code> is now <code>tf.random_crop(image,
    [height, width, depth])</code>, and <code>tf.random_crop</code> works for any rank (not just
    3-D images). The C++ <code>RandomCrop</code> op has been replaced with pure Python.</li>
<li>Renamed <code>tf.test.GetTempDir</code> and <code>tf.test.IsBuiltWithCuda</code> to
    <code>tf.test.get_temp_dir</code> and <code>tf.test.is_built_with_cuda</code> for PEP-8
    compatibility.</li>
<li><code>parse_example</code>'s interface has changed, the old interface is accessible in
    <code>legacy_parse_example</code> (same for related functions).</li>
<li>New <code>Variable</code>s are not added to the same collection several times even if a
    list with duplicates is passed to the constructor.</li>
<li>The Python API will now properly set the <code>list</code> member of <code>AttrValue</code> in
    constructed <code>GraphDef</code> messages for empty lists. The serialization of some
    graphs will change, but the change is both forwards and backwards
    compatible. It will break tests that compare a generated <code>GraphDef</code> to a
    golden serialized <code>GraphDef</code> (which is discouraged).</li>
</ul>

<h1>Release 0.6.0</h1>
<h2>Major Features and Improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Python 3.3+ support via changes to python codebase and ability to specify
    python version via ./configure.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Some improvements to GPU performance and memory usage:
    <a href="https://github.com/soumith/convnet-benchmarks/issues/66">convnet benchmarks</a>
    roughly equivalent with native cudnn v2 performance. Improvements mostly due
    to moving to 32-bit indices, faster shuffling kernels. More improvements to
    come in later releases.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Lots of fixes to documentation and tutorials, many contributed by the
    public.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>271 closed issues on github issues.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Backwards-Incompatible Changes</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>tf.nn.fixed_unigram_candidate_sampler</code> changed its default 'distortion'
    attribute from 0.0 to 1.0. This was a bug in the original release that is
    now fixed.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>added DeterministicRandomTestTool to migration_utils.py. This is useful when
    you are migrating from TF 1.x to TF2 and need to make sure your computation
    is still happening correctly along the way. See the
    <a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/guide/migrate/validate_correctness">validating correctness migration guide</a>
    for more info.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1>Release 0.5.0</h1>
<p>Initial release of TensorFlow.</p>
